# PRADY OS ‚ÄĒ SOVEREIGN EDITION

> *The machine owns execution. The Sovereign owns strategic authorization.*

PRADY OS is a Linux-based autonomous AI operating system in which a constellation of
specialist agents collectively governs the machine with administrator-level authority.
The human is elevated out of routine operation and positioned as the **Sovereign** who
approves or rejects projects, strategic initiatives, constitutional changes, and
irreversible high-impact actions.

The CLI is fully hidden. Agents own the terminal plane. The Sovereign sees only the
**Governance Chamber** ‚ÄĒ proposals, outcomes, incidents, approvals.

This is **Phase 0** of the build. It establishes the substrate: the hidden command
runner (TITAN OPS), the health telemetry mesh (WARDEN GRID), the orchestration kernel
(IMPERIUM), and the governance terminal seed (AURORA THRONE).

---

## The Three Laws

1. **Autonomous Execution** ‚ÄĒ all reversible and policy-compliant operational work is
   executed by the machine without routine human intervention.
2. **Sovereign Approval of Strategic Direction** ‚ÄĒ projects, strategic initiatives,
   constitutional changes, and irreversible actions cross the Sovereign boundary.
3. **Transparent Power** ‚ÄĒ broad operational authority is granted only because every
   significant action is observable, attributable, explainable, logged, and
   rollback-aware.

## Approval Boundary

Only the following require human approval:

- New projects surfaced by ORACLE
- Major strategic or architectural shifts
- Irreversible destructive actions on high-value state
- Data exfiltration beyond trusted boundaries
- Constitutional rule changes

Everything else executes autonomously within policy envelopes.

---

## Core Components

| Component | Role | Plane |
|-----------|------|-------|
| `pradyos.titan_ops` | Hidden command runner ‚ÄĒ admin-grade execution fabric | Execution |
| `pradyos.warden_grid` | Real-time health telemetry and incident detection | Recovery / Substrate |
| `pradyos.imperium` | Task queue, state machine, policy classifier, DAG | Orchestration |
| `pradyos.aurora_throne` | Sovereign Governance Chamber (terminal UI) | Experience |
| `pradyos.core` | Shared substrate ‚ÄĒ audit log, constitution, bus, IDs | Foundational |
| `pradyos.oracle` | AI reasoning, planning, autonomous proposal loop | Intelligence |
| `pradyos.campaign` | Campaign engine ‚ÄĒ multi-step DAG execution | Orchestration |
| `pradyos.proving_ground` | Constitutional admission gate | Safety |
| `pradyos.memory_citadel` | Persistent vector memory | Memory |
| `pradyos.sovereign` | Sovereign Web UI + CLI + REPL | Experience |

The raw CLI is never the user surface. `pradyos-throne` is the only sanctioned
entrypoint.

---

## Build Instructions

### Local development (no privilege escalation)

```bash
git clone <repo> pradyos
cd pradyos
python3.11 -m venv .venv
source .venv/bin/activate
pip install -e ".[dev]"
pytest -v
```

Launch the governance terminal:

```bash
python -m pradyos.service          # starts all daemons in-process
# in another terminal ‚ÄĒ but only this one, and only this surface, is sanctioned:
python -m pradyos.aurora_throne    # the Throne
```

### Docker dev environment

```bash
docker compose up --build
```

This brings up TITAN OPS, WARDEN GRID, and IMPERIUM as separate containers and
exposes the WARDEN GRID JSON API on `localhost:9701`.

### Systemd deployment (Sovereign build)

```bash
sudo cp deploy/systemd/*.service /etc/systemd/system/
sudo systemctl daemon-reload
sudo systemctl enable --now pradyos-titan.service \
                            pradyos-warden.service \
                            pradyos-imperium.service
# Throne is launched on Sovereign login, not as a service.
```

---

## Repo Layout

```
pradyos/
‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ core/            # shared substrate
‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ titan_ops/       # hidden command runner (Plane 2)
‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ warden_grid/     # health telemetry + incident mesh (Plane 1/9)
‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ imperium/        # orchestration kernel (Plane 3)
‚ĒĒ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ aurora_throne/   # governance terminal (Plane 10)
docs/                # architecture + API contracts
deploy/              # systemd units + Dockerfile
tests/               # pytest suite
var/                 # audit log + checkpoint state (gitignored)
```

## Status

**Phase 7 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 35 test modules green (82.7 s). Audit hooks,
metrics hooks, retry hooks, config watcher, REPL extensions, and deploy
pipeline are provably wired.

**Phase 8 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 37 test modules green. ORACLE autonomous proposal
loop and Campaign ‚ÜĒ Proving Ground admission bridge provably wired.

**Phase 9 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 37 test modules green. Four deliverables:
- ‚úÖ 9A: Production systemd units for **all five services** ‚ÄĒ `pradyos-titan`,
  `pradyos-warden`, `pradyos-imperium`, `pradyos-oracle` (new), and
  `pradyos-admission` (new). All units restart on failure, log to journald,
  and carry a full set of systemd sandboxing directives (`NoNewPrivileges`,
  `ProtectSystem=strict`, `PrivateTmp`, `PrivateDevices`,
  `ProtectKernelModules`, `ProtectControlGroups`, `RestrictNamespaces`,
  `LockPersonality`, `MemoryDenyWriteExecute`, `SystemCallFilter`). Dependency
  ordering: WARDEN + TITAN ‚Üí IMPERIUM ‚Üí ORACLE ‚Üí ADMISSION.
- ‚úÖ 9B: Docker hardening ‚ÄĒ `deploy/Dockerfile` upgraded to Python 3.12,
  `COPY --chown=pradyos` throughout. `deploy/docker-compose.yml` gains
  `oracle` and `admission` services wired with healthchecks
  (`/oracle/status` and
import-probe respectively), plus fleet-wide
  `cap_drop: [ALL]`, `security_opt: no-new-privileges:true`,
  `read_only: true`, `tmpfs: /tmp`, and a single named volume
  `pradyos-var` for audit log + state persistence. Secrets managed via
  `deploy/secrets.env` (template at `deploy/secrets.env.example`).
- ‚úÖ 9C: `tests/test_deploy.py` extended with 28 new assertions covering
  new systemd units, Docker hardening directives, oracle/admission
  service definitions, and healthcheck presence. All 37 modules remain green.
- ‚úÖ 9D: README updated.

**Phase 10 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 38 test modules green (28.7 s). Redis
inter-process bus live across Docker and systemd planes:
- ‚úÖ 10A: `pradyos/core/redis_bus.py` ‚ÄĒ `RedisBus` drop-in replacement for
  `EventBus` using redis-py Pub/Sub. A daemon thread polls
  `pubsub.get_message()` and dispatches to registered callbacks. Regular
  topics use `SUBSCRIBE`; the wildcard `"*"` topic uses `PSUBSCRIBE("*")`.
  Subscriber faults are isolated; unsubscribe triggers `UNSUBSCRIBE` /
  `PUNSUBSCRIBE` when the last handler is removed.
- ‚úÖ 10B: `pradyos/core/bus.py` ‚ÄĒ `get_bus()` factory updated. When
  `PRADYOS_BUS_BACKEND=redis`, returns `RedisBus`; otherwise the existing
  in-process `EventBus`. Zero call-site changes.
- ‚úÖ 10C: `deploy/docker-compose.yml` ‚ÄĒ `redis:7-alpine` service added with
  a `redis-cli ping` healthcheck and a named volume (`pradyos-redis`). All
  application services gain `PRADYOS_BUS_BACKEND=redis`,
  `PRADYOS_REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379/0`, and `depends_on: [redis]`.
- ‚úÖ 10D: All six `deploy/systemd/*.service` files (`pradyos-titan`,
  `pradyos-warden`, `pradyos-imperium`, `pradyos-oracle`, `pradyos-admission`,
  `pradyos-throne`) updated with
  `Environment=PRADYOS_BUS_BACKEND=redis` and
  `Environment=PRADYOS_REDIS_URL=redis://127.0.0.1:6379/0`.
- ‚úÖ 10E: `tests/test_redis_bus.py` ‚ÄĒ 16 tests using `fakeredis` (no real
  Redis server required). Covers pub/sub, wildcard, unsubscribe, fault
  isolation, payload round-trip, and `get_bus()` factory.
- ‚úÖ 10F: `pyproject.toml` dev deps extended with `redis>=5.0` and
  `fakeredis>=2.0`. `deploy/secrets.env.example` documents new env vars.


**Phase 11 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 41 test modules green. Autonomous self-healing live:
- ‚úÖ 11A: `pradyos/imperium/self_heal.py` ‚ÄĒ `SelfHealEngine` with `heal()`,
  `is_quarantined()`, `release_quarantine()`, `quarantine_list()`. Loads
  latest `SnapshotStore` entry as rollback reference, quarantines offending
  tasks in-memory + persisted to `var/state/quarantine.json`, publishes
  `system.self_heal` bus event (WARDEN auto-raises incident via `system.*`
  wildcard), and writes a structured audit entry.
- ‚úÖ 11B: `pradyos/imperium/kernel.py` ‚ÄĒ `Imperium.rollback()` method added;
  `Imperium._self_heal_hook()` callback wired into `RecoveryCore.on_exhausted`
  so any task that exhausts its retry budget is healed autonomously.
  `pradyos/imperium/recovery.py` extended with `on_exhausted` callback slot.
- ‚úÖ 11C: `pradyos/imperium/exceptions.py` ‚ÄĒ `TaskNotFound` custom exception.
- ‚úÖ 11D: `tests/test_self_heal.py` ‚ÄĒ 22 tests: `HealResult` correctness,
  quarantine persistence, `is_quarantined`, `release_quarantine`, bus events,
  audit entries, kernel integration (auto-heal on dead-letter), idempotency,
  snapshot reference, multi-task quarantine, and WARDEN notification.
- ‚úÖ 11E: `scripts/prove.py` updated; README Phase Map updated.

**Phase 16 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 49 test modules green. OTel-compatible telemetry pipeline ‚ÄĒ every significant OS event emits a structured span stored in a ring buffer and queryable via API:
- ‚úÖ 16A: `pradyos/core/telemetry.py` ‚ÄĒ `TelemetrySpan` dataclass (span_id, trace_id, parent_id, name, service, start_ts, end_ts, status, attributes) with `duration_ms()` and `to_dict()`. `TelemetryCollector` ring-buffer (collections.deque maxlen=500) with `start_span()`, `finish_span()`, `record()` (one-shot), `get_spans(limit, service, status)` returning most-recent-first, `clear()`, and `__len__()`. Thread-safe via threading.Lock. Auto-generates UUID4 hex span_id and trace_id. `finish_span()` returns None for unknown span_id ‚ÄĒ never raises.
- ‚úÖ 16B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `GET /api/v1/telemetry` endpoint wired via optional `telemetry` param in `create_app()`. Query params: `limit` (int, default 100, max 500), `service` (str|None), `status` (str|None). Returns `{"spans": [...], "count": int}`. Safe empty response `{"spans": [], "count": 0}` when telemetry not injected.
- ‚úÖ 16C: `tests/test_telemetry.py` ‚ÄĒ 20 unit tests covering start_span status/id generation/explicit trace_id/append, finish_span status/end_ts/merge/unknown-id, record default/duration_ms/error, get_spans list/limit/service filter/status filter/order, clear, maxlen eviction, and duration_ms None vs computed.
- ‚úÖ 16D: `tests/test_telemetry_web.py` ‚ÄĒ 10 FastAPI TestClient tests: HTTP 200, spans/count keys, spans is list, count==len(spans), limit param, service filter, status filter, count reflects filter, no-telemetry empty response.
- ‚úÖ 16E: `scripts/prove.py` updated with both new test modules (49 total).
- ‚úÖ 16F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 17 planned.

**Phase 17 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 51 test modules green. Sovereign Memory Graph ‚ÄĒ a knowledge graph layer where the OS stores facts, relationships, and inferences about campaigns, tasks, and system state ‚ÄĒ queryable via API and visualised in the Aurora Throne TUI:
- ‚úÖ 17A: `pradyos/core/memorygraph.py` ‚ÄĒ `GraphNode` and `GraphEdge` dataclasses with `to_dict()`. `SovereignMemoryGraph` with bounded storage (maxnodes/maxedges), LRU-by-age eviction, `add_node()`, `add_edge()`, `get_node()`, `get_edge()`, `neighbours(relation=None)`, `query_nodes(kind, label)` sorted newest-first, `remove_node()` cascading edge removal, `remove_edge()`, `stats()`, `clear()`. Thread-safe via `threading.Lock`. Auto-generates UUID4 hex ids.
- ‚úÖ 17B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `GET /api/v1/graph/stats` returns `{"nodes": int, "edges": int}`; `POST /api/v1/graph/nodes` body `{kind, label, node_id?, attributes?}` returns new node dict; `GET /api/v1/graph/nodes?kind&label&limit` returns `{"nodes": [...], "count": int}`; `GET /api/v1/graph/nodes/{node_id}/neighbours?relation` returns `{"neighbours": [...], "count": int}`. Wired via new `graph` param in `create_app()`. Safe empty responses when graph not injected.
- ‚úÖ 17C: `tests/test_memorygraph.py` ‚ÄĒ 20 unit tests covering add_node kind/label/auto-id/explicit-id/stats, add_edge fields/auto-id/stats, get_node hit/miss, get_edge hit, neighbours basic/relation-filter, query_nodes kind/label filter, remove_node true/false/cascade, remove_edge true/false, maxnodes eviction, and clear.

- ‚úÖ 19B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` ‚ÄĒ patched to add optional `intent` param to `create_app()`; `GET /api/v1/intent/rules` returns `{rules, count}`; `POST /api/v1/intent/rules` body `{rules:[...]}` returns `{loaded}`; `POST /api/v1/intent/suggest` body `{graph_stats, active_campaigns, recent_spans, recent_entries}` returns `{suggestions, count}`. Safe empty responses when no intent injected.

Each section shows up to 20 most-recent items; graceful "No data" when APIs return empty. Auto-refresh every 10 s via `setInterval`. Dark theme consistent with the existing dashboard.

**Phase 21 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 59 test modules green. Sovereign Config Hot-Reload ‚ÄĒ a file-watcher that monitors a YAML/JSON config file for changes and hot-reloads intent engine rules, scheduler jobs, and policy rules without restarting the server:
- ‚úÖ 21A: `pradyos/core/config_hot_reload.py` ‚ÄĒ `ReloadResult` dataclass with `to_dict()`; `ConfigHotReloader` class with `load()`, `start()`, `stop()`, `last_result()`, `status()`. Background daemon thread polls `config_path` every `poll_interval` seconds; reloads on mtime change. Uses `yaml.safe_load` if PyYAML present, falls back to `json.loads` (stdlib-only). Each config section (`intent_rules`, `scheduler_jobs`, `policy_rules`) is optional; missing sections and `None` components are silently skipped. Returns `ReloadResult(success=False, error=‚Ä¶)` on any exception.
- ‚úÖ 21B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` ‚ÄĒ patched via script to add `config_reloader` param to `create_app()` and two new endpoints: `GET /api/v1/config/status` returns `reloader.status()` (or stub dict when not injected); `POST /api/v1/config/reload` calls `reloader.load()` and returns `result.to_dict()`. `DASHBOARD_HTML` constant untouched.
- ‚úÖ 21C: `tests/test_config_hot_reload.py` ‚ÄĒ 20 unit tests covering `ReloadResult.to_dict()` keys, `load()` success/failure paths, all three config sections, missing sections, `None` components, file-not-found, invalid JSON, `status()` keys, `_running` transitions, `last_result()` lifecycle, start/stop cycle, changes list type and content.
- ‚úÖ 21D: `tests/test_config_reload_web.py` ‚ÄĒ 10 FastAPI TestClient tests: HTTP 200 for both endpoints, required response keys, no-reloader stubs, valid-reloader success, error=None on success, config_path reflection, changes list type.
- ‚úÖ 21E: `scripts/prove.py` updated with both new test modules (59 total).
- ‚úÖ 21F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 22 planned.

**Phase 23 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 63 test modules green. Sovereign Rate-Limit Shield ‚ÄĒ sliding-window, in-memory per-(client_id, endpoint) rate limiter with injectable clock for deterministic testing:
- ‚úÖ 23A: `pradyos/core/rate_limiter.py` ‚ÄĒ `RateLimitResult` dataclass with `to_dict()` + `RateLimiter` class. Sliding-window counter prunes timestamps older than `window_secs`. `check()` records hits when allowed, does NOT record when denied; returns `retry_after` seconds until reset. `set_rule()` / `get_rules()` for per-endpoint overrides. `reset(client_id, endpoint?)` clears timestamps. `status()` reports active_clients, total_hits, rules. Thread-safe via `threading.Lock`. Zero external dependencies.
- ‚úÖ 23B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` ‚ÄĒ patched via script to add `rate_limiter` optional param to `create_app()` and three new endpoints: `GET /api/v1/ratelimit/status` returns limiter.status() or stub; `POST /api/v1/ratelimit/rules` sets per-endpoint rule; `POST /api/v1/ratelimit/check` evaluates a (client_id, endpoint) pair and returns full RateLimitResult dict. `DASHBOARD_HTML` constant untouched.
- ‚úÖ 23C: `tests/test_rate_limiter.py` ‚ÄĒ 20 unit tests covering init, check result type, allowed/denied logic, hit recording, sliding window pruning with injectable clock, set_rule/get_rules mutation safety, reset by client and by endpoint, status keys and counts, to_dict keys, retry_after=None/float, 10-hit boundary, cross-endpoint and cross-client independence.
- ‚úÖ 23D: `tests/test_rate_limit_web.py` ‚ÄĒ 10 FastAPI TestClient tests: HTTP 200 for all endpoints, required keys in responses, allowed=True under limit, stub behaviour when no limiter injected, rule-then-check enforcement.
- ‚úÖ 23E: `scripts/prove.py` updated with both new test modules (63 total).
- ‚úÖ 23F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 24 planned.

**Phase 24 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 65 test modules green. Sovereign Health Scorecard ‚ÄĒ a composite health score (0‚Äď100) engine with thread-safe component registry, weighted-average scoring, and A/B/C/D/F grading:
- ‚úÖ 24A: `pradyos/core/health_scorecard.py` ‚ÄĒ `ComponentScore` and `HealthReport` dataclasses; `HealthScorecard` class with `register()`, `update()` (clamped 0‚Äď100, auto-registers), `get_report()` (weighted average, grade), `reset()`. Thread-safe via `threading.Lock`.
- ‚úÖ 24B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched ‚ÄĒ `scorecard` optional param added to `create_app()`; `GET /api/v1/health/score` returns composite report; `POST /api/v1/health/update` accepts name/score/details and calls `scorecard.update()`. Safe empty responses when scorecard not injected.
- ‚úÖ 24C: `tests/test_health_scorecard.py` ‚ÄĒ 20 unit tests covering init, default report, grade boundaries (A/B/C/D/F), clamping, auto-register, explicit weights, weighted average, `reset()`, `to_dict()` keys, details default, and 50-thread concurrency.
- ‚úÖ 24D: `tests/test_health_web.py` ‚ÄĒ 10 FastAPI TestClient tests covering GET/POST endpoints, no-scorecard fallbacks (score=100, updated=false), update-then-get round-trip, and grade A/F scenarios.
- ‚úÖ 24E: `scripts/prove.py` updated to 65 modules.
- ‚úÖ 24F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 25 planned.

**Phase 41 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 99 test modules green. Sovereign Heartbeat Loop ‚ÄĒ async background driver that calls `ControlPlane.tick()` on a fixed interval, transforming the OS from on-demand to self-driving; FastAPI startup/shutdown lifecycle hooks auto-start and auto-stop the loop; stdlib + asyncio only:

- ‚úÖ 41A: `pradyos/core/heartbeat.py` ‚ÄĒ `HeartbeatConfig` (interval_seconds default 5.0, max_ticks optional cap), `HeartbeatLoop` with `start()` (idempotent), `stop()` (graceful with timeout fallback to cancel), `_loop()` (swallows tick exceptions, increments thread-safe counter, stops at max_ticks), `status()`; thread-safe via `threading.Lock` on `tick_count`.
- ‚úÖ 41B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched ‚ÄĒ `@app.on_event("startup")` auto-calls `heartbeat.start()`, `@app.on_event("shutdown")` calls `heartbeat.stop()`; `GET /api/v1/heartbeat/status` (status dict), `POST /api/v1/heartbeat/stop` (graceful stop) wired into `create_app(heartbeat=...)`. Used `on_event` decorators (not lifespan) to avoid modifying the existing `FastAPI()` call.

**Phase 43 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 104 test modules green. **The most important phase.** Without this, the OS cannot safely act autonomously. `GuardrailGate` classifies every intended action by risk (SAFE/LOW/MEDIUM/HIGH/CRITICAL); SAFE/LOW are auto-approved with journal trail; MEDIUM/HIGH/CRITICAL are queued in `ApprovalQueue` for explicit user approval; CRITICAL requires a `reason`. The queue supports approve/reject/expire-stale with TTL fallback. Stdlib only, thread-safe:

- ‚úÖ 43A: `pradyos/core/guardrail.py` ‚ÄĒ `RiskLevel` enum, `ActionRequest` dataclass (uuid id + to_dict), `GuardrailGate.submit()` (raises ValueError on CRITICAL+no-reason, auto-approves SAFE/LOW with journal record, queues MEDIUM/HIGH/CRITICAL), `status()` (auto_approve_levels + pending queue_size).
- ‚úÖ 43B: `pradyos/core/approval_queue.py` ‚ÄĒ `ApprovalStatus` enum (PENDING/APPROVED/REJECTED/EXPIRED), `ApprovalEntry` dataclass, `ApprovalQueue` with `add()` (creates PENDING from request), `approve()`/`reject()` (sets resolved_at + resolver_note), `expire_stale()` (TTL sweep), `get()`, `list_by_status()` (sorted by requested_at), `count()` (by status string/enum/None); thread-safe via `threading.Lock`.
- ‚úÖ 43C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched ‚ÄĒ `GET /api/v1/guardrail/status`, `POST /api/v1/guardrail/submit`, `GET /api/v1/approvals?status=X`, `POST /api/v1/approvals/{id}/approve`, `POST /api/v1/approvals/{id}/reject`, `POST /api/v1/approvals/expire` wired into `create_app(guardrail_gate=..., approval_queue=...)`.
- ‚úÖ 43D: `tests/test_guardrail.py` ‚ÄĒ 20 unit tests covering ActionRequest fields/serialization, RiskLevel enum, gate init/submit-safe/submit-low/submit-medium-queues/submit-high-queues, CRITICAL-no-reason raises, CRITICAL-with-reason queues, journal integration (auto vs pending), status keys, queue add/approve/reject/expire/count.
- ‚úÖ 43E: `tests/test_approval_web.py` ‚ÄĒ 10 FastAPI tests (guardrail status no-gate/with-gate, submit safe/medium/invalid-risk, approvals list, approve/reject endpoints, expire count, full submit-HIGH‚Üíapprove‚Üílist-shows-approved flow).
- ‚úÖ 43F: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 104 test modules registered.
- ‚úÖ 43G: README Phase Map updated; Phase 44 planned.

**Phase 52 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 122 test modules green. Sovereign DistributedLock ‚ÄĒ TTL-based named mutex; crashed holders cannot deadlock the system because every lock expires automatically; same-holder re-acquire refreshes TTL by design; stdlib only:

- ‚úÖ 52A: `pradyos/core/distributed_lock.py` ‚ÄĒ `DistributedLock` dataclass with `is_expired()` and `to_dict()`; `LockManager` with `acquire(name, holder_id, ttl=30)` (returns None if held by another non-expired holder; same holder re-acquires by replacing; expired locks can be taken by anyone), `release(name, holder_id)` (True only if caller is non-expired current holder), `refresh()` (extend TTL when caller is current holder and not expired), `is_locked()` (only True if held and not expired), `list_locks()` (excludes expired but doesn't remove them, sorted by acquired_at), `expire_stale()` (removes expired, returns count), `count(include_expired=False)`; thread-safe via `threading.Lock`.
- ‚úÖ 52B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched ‚ÄĒ `GET /api/v1/locks`, `POST /api/v1/locks` (400 on missing keys, 409 when already held), `POST /api/v1/locks/{name}/refresh` (registered BEFORE delete so the literal `/refresh` doesn't get consumed), `DELETE /api/v1/locks/{name}?holder_id=...` wired into `create_app(lock_manager=...)`.
- ‚úÖ 52C: `tests/test_distributed_lock.py` ‚ÄĒ 20 unit tests (init, acquire fields/is_locked/second-caller-None/same-holder-replaces/expired-can-be-taken, release true/wrong-holder/unknown, refresh true/wrong-holder/expired, is_locked unknown/after-release, list excludes-expired/sorted, expire_stale removes-and-counts, count excludes/includes-expired).
- ‚úÖ 52D: `tests/test_distributed_lock_web.py` ‚ÄĒ 10 FastAPI TestClient tests covering all 4 endpoints, no-manager fallbacks, 400/404/409 status codes, end-to-end acquire‚Üírefresh‚Üírelease.

**Phase 53 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 124 test modules green. Sovereign CircuitBreaker ‚ÄĒ per-service failure tracker with CLOSED ‚Üí OPEN ‚Üí HALF_OPEN ‚Üí CLOSED/OPEN state machine; OPEN refuses calls immediately, recovery_timeout transitions to HALF_OPEN, success returns to CLOSED, failure flips back to OPEN; stdlib only:

- ‚úÖ 53A: `pradyos/core/circuit_breaker.py` ‚ÄĒ `CircuitOpenError`, `BreakerState` dataclass with `to_dict()` (omits internal `half_open_probes` counter), `CircuitBreaker(failure_threshold=5, recovery_timeout=30.0, half_open_max=1)` with `call(name, fn, *args, **kwargs)` (auto-creates state on first use; OPEN check at entry ‚Üí maybe transition to HALF_OPEN or raise; fn executes OUTSIDE lock so slow handlers don't block other callers; success in CLOSED resets failure_count; success in HALF_OPEN ‚Üí CLOSED; failure in CLOSED checks threshold ‚Üí OPEN; failure in HALF_OPEN increments probe count ‚Üí OPEN at half_open_max), `get_state()`, `reset()` (zeros out all state), `list_breakers()` (sorted by name), `count()`; thread-safe via `threading.Lock`.
- ‚úÖ 53B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched ‚ÄĒ `GET /api/v1/breakers`, `POST /api/v1/breakers` (registers a named breaker via `_get_or_create_locked`), `POST /api/v1/breakers/{name}/reset` (registered BEFORE bare `/{name}` GET so the literal `/reset` doesn't get captured), `GET /api/v1/breakers/{name}` (404 if missing) wired into `create_app(circuit_breaker=...)`.

**Phase 64 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 146 test modules green. Sovereign Command Bus ‚ÄĒ named handlers register at runtime, dispatch by name with a payload dict; each call produces a `CommandResult` recorded in a ring-buffer history (max 500). Stdlib only:

Sovereign Saga Orchestrator ‚ÄĒ long-running multi-step workflow engine; each step is a named callable that transforms a payload dict, output of step N becomes input of step N+1; on any failure the saga records `status="failed"` with the failing step + error and stops. **Phase 69 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 155 test modules green. Sovereign Signal Anomaly Detector ‚ÄĒ z-score statistical outlier detection over a named `SignalAggregator` signal. Downsamples the windowed history into 1-second buckets (the mean of all readings sharing `floor(recorded_at)`) for a sampling-rate-independent baseline, scores the most recent bucket as a z-score against the windowed population mean/stddev, and maps `|z|` to a severity label (`normal` < 2 ‚Č§ `warning` < 3 ‚Č§ `critical`). Pure stdlib ‚ÄĒ no numpy/scipy:

- ‚úÖ 69A: `pradyos/core/anomaly_detector.py` ‚ÄĒ `_severity(z)` (|z|‚Č•3 ‚Üí critical, ‚Č•2 ‚Üí warning, else normal); `AnomalyResult(signal, sample_size, window, mean, stddev, latest_value, z_score, severity, computed_at)` dataclass with `to_dict()`; `AnomalyDetector(aggregator)` with `detect(signal, window=3600.0)` (filters points by `recorded_at >= now ‚ąí window` via the aggregator's public `get()`; 1-second bucketing; `n==0` ‚Üí all-zero `normal` result; `n<2` ‚Üí no-spread `normal`; else population stddev + `z=(latest ‚ąí mean)/stddev`, `0.0` when stddev is 0; mean/stddev/latest/z rounded to 6 dp), `get_cached(signal, window)`, `cache_result(result)` (insertion-order LRU, evicts oldest beyond 128); thread-safe via `threading.Lock`. **Deviation:** the literal Phase 69 brief ("Sovereign Correlation Engine") already shipped as Phase 33, and the previously-planned Circuit Breaker likewise overlapped existing work ‚ÄĒ so Phase 69 delivers a new, non-colliding Anomaly Detector that reuses the Phase 31 `SignalAggregator` without modifying it.
- ‚úÖ 69B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase69.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged) ‚ÄĒ added `anomaly_detector: Any | None = None` param and 2 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/anomaly?signal=X&window=Y&use_cache=bool` and `POST /api/v1/anomaly` (body `{signal, window?, use_cache?}`); both return `{"error": ...}` when no detector is configured or `signal` is missing, and tag each response with `"cached"` (true only on a `use_cache` hit).
- ‚úÖ 69C: `tests/test_anomaly_detector.py` ‚ÄĒ 20 unit tests (init; return type; missing-signal zero result; single-bucket/constant no-spread; clear positive + negative anomaly ‚Üí critical; mean + population stddev; z-score formula; parametrized severity normal/warning/critical bands incl. negative z; 1-second bucketing averages same-second readings; window excludes old points; window value preserved; 6-dp rounding; `to_dict` keys; cache miss/store/retrieve; LRU eviction caps at 128; 30-thread concurrent detect/cache safety).
- ‚úÖ 69D: `tests/test_anomaly_web.py` ‚ÄĒ 10 FastAPI TestClient tests (no-engine GET/POST errors; valid GET 200 + all fields; valid POST 200; unknown signal ‚Üí sample_size 0; `use_cache` miss-then-hit; window defaults to 3600.0; window filter excludes old points).
- ‚úÖ 69E: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 155 test modules registered (running total; Phase 69 appends `test_anomaly_detector.py` + `test_anomaly_web.py`).
- ‚úÖ 69F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 70 planned.

**Phase 70 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 157 test modules green. Sovereign Dependency Graph ‚ÄĒ tracks directed dependencies between named components (an edge `a -> b` means "a depends on b"), stored as a forward adjacency map plus a mirror reverse map so both "what does X need?" and "who needs X?" are O(1). Pure stdlib ‚ÄĒ no third-party deps; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- ‚úÖ 70A: `pradyos/core/dependency_graph.py` ‚ÄĒ `CycleError(cycle)` (carries the offending node path, closed on itself); `DependencyGraph` with `add_dependency(frm, to)` (idempotent, auto-creates nodes), `remove_dependency(frm, to)` (returns whether the edge existed; nodes retained), `get_dependencies(node)` / `get_dependents(node)` (direct, sorted), `impact_score(node)` (count of transitive dependents ‚ÄĒ how far a failure ripples), `find_cycle()` (DFS back-edge search ‚Üí closed cycle path or `None`), `topological_sort(start=None)` (Kahn's algorithm, dependency-first, alphabetical tie-break for determinism; restricted to a node's transitive closure when `start` is given; raises `CycleError` on cycles), `describe(node)` (JSON snapshot), `has_node` / `nodes`. **Deviation:** the literal Phase 70 brief ("Sovereign Correlation Engine") already shipped as Phase 33 ‚ÄĒ so, following the Phase 69 precedent, Phase 70 delivers a new, non-colliding Dependency Graph; the previously-planned Anomaly Watch is deferred to Phase 71.
- ‚úÖ 70B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase70.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ‚ÄĒ added `dependency_graph: Any | None = None` param and 5 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/deps/{node}` (node snapshot), `POST /api/v1/deps` (body `{from, to}`; 422 when either is missing), `DELETE /api/v1/deps/{from}/{to}`, `GET /api/v1/deps/{node}/sort` (topo sort from the node; 409 + cycle path on a cycle), and `GET /api/v1/deps/{node}/impact`; all return `{"error": ...}` when no graph is configured.
- ‚úÖ 70C: `tests/test_dependency_graph.py` ‚ÄĒ 23 unit tests (init; add creates both nodes; dependencies/dependents; idempotent add; remove true/false + node retention; membership; unknown-node empties; linear-chain + edge-respecting + deterministic topo sort; scoped sort from a node; cycle ‚Üí `CycleError` with a valid path; `find_cycle` none/simple/self-loop; impact score direct + transitive; `describe` fields; 20-thread concurrent-add safety).
- ‚úÖ 70D: `tests/test_dependency_web.py` ‚ÄĒ 10 FastAPI TestClient tests (no-engine GET/POST errors; node info + fields; POST adds edge; POST missing field ‚Üí 422; DELETE removes / non-existent ‚Üí false; topo sort order; cycle ‚Üí 409 with closed path; impact score).
- ‚úÖ 70E: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 157 test modules registered (running total; Phase 70 appends `test_dependency_graph.py` + `test_dependency_web.py`).

**Phase 71 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 159 test modules green. Sovereign Anomaly Watch ‚ÄĒ a real-time anomaly-detection watchdog that polls registered service health metrics and scores the latest reading of each source with a scikit-learn `IsolationForest` (the same algorithm the hardware-intel service uses), flagging statistical outliers; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- ‚úÖ 71A: `pradyos/core/anomaly_watch.py` ‚ÄĒ `SourceNotFoundError(name)` (carries the offending source name); `AnomalyWatch(min_samples=10, window=256, contamination="auto", n_estimators=100, random_state=42)` with `register_source(name, metric_fn, baseline=None)` (a zero-arg `metric_fn` returns the live metric; the optional `baseline` pre-seeds the rolling window), `tick()` (polls every source, appends its reading to a bounded window, and scores the latest value once ‚Č• `min_samples` readings exist ‚ÄĒ returning `{"status": "warming_up"}` before that, and isolating any source whose `metric_fn` raises as `{"status": "error"}` rather than aborting the tick), `get_anomalies()` (latest results currently flagged anomalous), `get_status()` (latest per-source results), `deregister(name)` (raises `SourceNotFoundError`), `sources()` / `has_source()` / `sample_count()`, and `clear()`. **Deviation:** the README's earlier Phase 71 sketch (a z-score `AnomalyDetector` loop over `SignalAggregator`) is superseded by this brief's IsolationForest design; it ships as a new module distinct from the Phase 69 detector, so nothing is overwritten.

These sub-paths coexist with the Phase 69 `GET`/`POST /api/v1/anomaly` z-score routes without shadowing them.

**Phase 72 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 161 test modules green. Sovereign Bloom Filter ‚ÄĒ a space-efficient probabilistic set-membership structure: items are hashed into a fixed bit array via Kirsch‚ÄďMitzenmacher double-hashing (two 64-bit halves of one SHA-256 digest), so `contains` may false-positive but **never** false-negatives ‚ÄĒ ideal for cheap "have I seen this?" guards. Pure stdlib (`hashlib` + a `bytearray`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. **Pivot:** the previously-planned Phase 72 "Policy Engine" namespace is fully occupied by Phase 14 (`pradyos/imperium/policy_engine.py`, `/api/v1/policy/rules`, both test modules), and "Event Bus" collided with `pradyos/core/bus.py::EventBus` + the Phase 48 `/api/v1/events` event store ‚ÄĒ so, following the standing pivot precedent, Phase 72 ships a new, namespace-verified Bloom Filter.

- ‚úÖ 72A: `pradyos/core/bloom_filter.py` ‚ÄĒ `BloomFilter(capacity=1000, error_rate=0.01)` derives the optimal bit count `m = ceil(-(n¬∑ln p)/(ln 2)¬≤)` and hash count `k = round((m/n)¬∑ln 2)`; `add(item) ‚Üí bool` (True when a new bit was set), `add_many(items) ‚Üí int` (count newly set), `contains(item)` / `__contains__`, `clear()`, `__len__` (approx distinct added), `fill_ratio()`, `estimated_false_positive_rate()`, `stats()` (JSON snapshot), plus `capacity` / `error_rate` / `bits` / `hashes` properties. Any key type is accepted (strings hashed directly, others via `repr`). Invalid `capacity` / `error_rate` raise `ValueError`.
- ‚úÖ 72B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase72.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ‚ÄĒ added a `bloom_filter: Any | None = None` param and 4 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/bloom` (stats), `POST /api/v1/bloom/add` (body `{item}` or `{items: [...]}`; 422 on missing/non-string), `GET /api/v1/bloom/contains/{item}`, and `DELETE /api/v1/bloom` (clear); all return `{"error": ...}` when no filter is configured. The `/api/v1/bloom` prefix was verified free against every existing route.
- ‚úÖ 72C: `tests/test_bloom_filter.py` ‚ÄĒ 26 unit tests (sizing from capacity/error_rate; invalid-arg `ValueError`; add new/dup; contains hit/miss + `in` operator; `add_many` counts; `len`; the no-false-negative guarantee over 500 items; empirical false-positive rate within bound; clear; stats keys/count; fill-ratio; estimated-fpp; property accessors; non-string + unicode keys; 10-thread concurrent-add safety).
- ‚úÖ 72D: `tests/test_bloom_filter_web.py` ‚ÄĒ 14 FastAPI TestClient tests (no-filter errors on all four routes; stats keys; add single/list; missing / non-string ‚Üí 422; contains hit/miss; clear resets; no-false-negative over HTTP).
- ‚úÖ 72E: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 161 test modules registered (running total; Phase 72 appends `test_bloom_filter.py` + `test_bloom_filter_web.py`).
- ‚úÖ 72F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 73 planned.

**Phase 73 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 163 test modules green. Sovereign Consistent Hash Ring ‚ÄĒ maps arbitrary keys to a changing set of nodes so that adding or removing a node reshuffles only that node's keys, never the rest (the consistent-hashing property). Each node is placed at `replicas` points around a 2^64 SHA-256 ring; a key is owned by the first node clockwise, located in O(log V) via `bisect`. Pure stdlib (`hashlib` + `bisect`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- ‚úÖ 73A: `pradyos/core/hash_ring.py` ‚ÄĒ `NodeNotFoundError(node)` (carries the offending name); `HashRing(nodes=None, *, replicas=100)` with `add_node` (idempotent), `remove_node` (raises `NodeNotFoundError`), `get_node(key)` (owner, or `None` on an empty ring), `get_nodes(key, count)` (distinct clockwise nodes for replication), `nodes()` / `has_node()`, `distribution(keys)` (per-node key counts), `stats()` (JSON snapshot), and `clear()`. Invalid `replicas` raises `ValueError`.
- ‚úÖ 73B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase73.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ‚ÄĒ added a `hash_ring: Any | None = None` param and 4 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/hashring` (stats), `POST /api/v1/hashring/nodes` (body `{node}`; 422 on missing), `GET /api/v1/hashring/node/{key}` (owner lookup), and `DELETE /api/v1/hashring/nodes/{node}` (404 on unknown); all return `{"error": ...}` when no ring is configured. The `/api/v1/hashring` prefix was verified free against every existing route.
- ‚úÖ 73C: `tests/test_hash_ring.py` ‚ÄĒ 25 unit tests (construction + invalid `replicas`; idempotent add; remove + `NodeNotFoundError` carrying the name; lookup determinism / membership; `get_nodes` distinct / cap / empty / non-positive; balanced distribution; the consistent-hashing guarantee on **both** add and remove; stats; virtual-point math; clear; 10-thread concurrency).
- ‚úÖ 73D: `tests/test_hash_ring_web.py` ‚ÄĒ 13 FastAPI TestClient tests (no-ring errors on all four routes; stats keys; add + node_count; missing ‚Üí 422; empty-ring lookup ‚Üí null; member lookup; determinism; remove; unknown ‚Üí 404).

**Phase 74 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 165 test modules green. Sovereign Cardinality Estimator ‚ÄĒ a HyperLogLog sketch that counts *distinct* items in a stream using fixed memory (m = 2^precision one-byte registers), independent of stream size. Each item is hashed (SHA-1 ‚Üí 64 bits); the top `precision` bits pick a register, which keeps the largest leading-zero rank seen. The estimate uses the bias-corrected harmonic-mean formula with linear-counting in the small range, for ‚Čą1.04/‚ąöm relative error (~0.8% at precision 14). Pure stdlib (`hashlib` + `math`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- ‚úÖ 74A: `pradyos/core/hyperloglog.py` ‚ÄĒ `HyperLogLog(precision=14)` with `add(item)` / `add_many(items)`, `estimate()` (rounded distinct count) / `__len__`, `merge(other)` (register-wise max union; raises `ValueError` on precision mismatch or non-HLL), `clear()`, `fill_ratio()`, `stats()` (JSON snapshot), and `precision` / `registers` properties. Any key type is accepted (strings hashed directly, others via `repr`). Invalid `precision` (outside 4‚Äď16) raises `ValueError`.
- ‚úÖ 74B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase74.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ‚ÄĒ added a `hyperloglog: Any | None = None` param and 4 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/cardinality` (stats), `POST /api/v1/cardinality/add` (body `{item}` or `{items: [...]}`; 422 on missing/non-string), `GET /api/v1/cardinality/estimate`, and `DELETE /api/v1/cardinality` (clear); all return `{"error": ...}` when no estimator is configured. The `/api/v1/cardinality` prefix was verified free against every existing route.

**Phase 75 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 167 test modules green. Sovereign Vector Clock ‚ÄĒ tracks the causal ordering of events across independent actors. Each actor bumps its own counter on a local event (`tick`); receiving a message folds in the sender's clock via element-wise max (`merge`); comparing two clocks (`compare`) reports `before` / `after` / `equal` / `concurrent` (causally independent ‚ÄĒ a conflict). Missing actors count as 0 so clocks with different actor sets compare cleanly. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- ‚úÖ 75A: `pradyos/core/vectorclock.py` ‚ÄĒ `VectorClock(initial=None)` with `tick(actor)` (returns the new counter), `merge(other)` (element-wise max; `ValueError` on non-VectorClock), `compare(other)` ‚Üí `before|after|equal|concurrent`, `get(actor)`, `actors()`, `to_dict()` (copy), `copy()`, `clear()`, and `stats()`. Negative or non-integer initial values raise `ValueError`.
- ‚úÖ 75B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase75.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ‚ÄĒ added a `vectorclock: Any | None = None` param and 4 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/clocks` (state), `POST /api/v1/clocks/tick` (body `{actor}`; 422 on missing), `POST /api/v1/clocks/merge` (body `{clock}`; 422 on non-dict or bad values), and `POST /api/v1/clocks/compare` (body `{clock}` ‚Üí `{relation}`); all return `{"error": ...}` when no clock is configured. The `/api/v1/clocks` prefix was verified free against every existing route.

**Phase 76 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 169 test modules green. Sovereign Frequency Sketch ‚ÄĒ a Count-Min Sketch that estimates per-item frequencies over a stream in fixed `depth √ó width` memory. Each item is hashed into one counter per row via Kirsch‚ÄďMitzenmacher double-hashing (two 64-bit halves of one SHA-256 digest, combined as `(h1 + row¬∑h2) mod width`); `estimate` is the minimum across rows, so collisions can only inflate it ‚ÄĒ it **never under-counts**. Pure stdlib (`hashlib`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- ‚úÖ 76A: `pradyos/core/countminsketch.py` ‚ÄĒ `CountMinSketch(width=2000, depth=5)` with `add(item, count=1)` (count must be a positive integer), `estimate(item) ‚Üí int` (min across rows ‚ÄĒ an upper bound), `merge(other) ‚Üí CountMinSketch` (element-wise sum into a NEW sketch; neither input mutated; `ValueError` on dimension mismatch or non-sketch), `clear()`, `stats()` (width / depth / cells / total), and `width` / `depth` properties. Invalid `width` / `depth` (‚Č§ 0) raise `ValueError`.
- ‚úÖ 76B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase76.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ‚ÄĒ added a `countminsketch: Any | None = None` param and 4 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/frequency` (stats), `POST /api/v1/frequency/add` (body `{item, count=1}`; 422 on missing item or non-positive count), `POST /api/v1/frequency/estimate` (body `{item}`), and `POST /api/v1/frequency/merge` (body `{items: [...], item?}` ‚ÄĒ merges a sketch built from those items with the live one via `merge()` and reports the merged total / estimate); all return `{"error": ...}` when no sketch is configured. Sovereign Merkle Tree ‚ÄĒ hashes an ordered list of items into a single root such that any change to any item flips the root, and membership is provable with an audit path of only ‚Ćąlog‚āā n‚ĆČ sibling hashes (without revealing the other items). Leaves are SHA-256 of each item; each level hashes adjacent pairs (`H(left || right)`), duplicating the last node on odd levels to stay balanced. Pure stdlib (`hashlib`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- ‚úÖ 77A: `pradyos/core/merkle_tree.py` ‚ÄĒ `MerkleTree` with `add(item)` (leaf append; `ValueError` on None), `build()` / `root` property (hex root, or `None` when empty), `proof(item)` (audit path of `{"hash", "side"}` entries; `ValueError` if the tree is empty or the item is absent), `verify(item)` (recomputes the root from the item + its proof ‚Üí bool), `clear()`, `stats()` (leaves / height / root), and `__len__`. Odd-leaf duplication keeps the tree balanced; the proof length is ‚Ćąlog‚āā n‚ĆČ.
- ‚úÖ 77B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase77.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ‚ÄĒ added a `merkle_tree: Any | None = None` param and 4 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/merkle` (stats), `POST /api/v1/merkle/add` (body `{item}`; 422 on missing), `POST /api/v1/merkle/verify` (body `{item}` ‚Üí `{verified}`), and `POST /api/v1/merkle/proof` (body `{item}` ‚Üí audit path + root; 404 when the item isn't a leaf); all return `{"error": ...}` when no tree is configured. The `/api/v1/merkle` prefix was verified free.

**Phase 79 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 175 test modules green. Sovereign T-Digest ‚ÄĒ estimates streaming quantiles (median, p95, p99 ‚Ä¶) in compact, mergeable memory. **Phase 80 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 177 test modules green. Sovereign Fenwick Tree ‚ÄĒ a binary indexed tree answering prefix-sum queries and point updates both in O(log n) by exploiting the binary structure of indices (each slot covers a range of length `i & -i`; updates walk up by adding that bit, prefix sums walk down by subtracting it). 1-indexed; `range_sum(lo, hi) = prefix_sum(hi) - prefix_sum(lo-1)`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- ‚úÖ 80A: `pradyos/core/fenwick.py` ‚ÄĒ `FenwickTree(size)` with `update(i, delta)` (1-indexed; int or float, may be negative), `prefix_sum(i)` (sum of 1..i; `prefix_sum(0)=0`), `range_sum(lo, hi)` (inclusive), `point_query(i)` (value at i), `resize(new_size)` (preserves the overlap), `clear()`, `size` property, and `stats()` (size / total). Out-of-bounds indices, `lo > hi`, non-integer indices, non-numeric deltas, and `size < 1` raise `ValueError`.
- ‚úÖ 80B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase80.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ‚ÄĒ added a `fenwick: Any | None = None` param and 4 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/fenwick` (stats), `POST /api/v1/fenwick/update` (body `{index, delta}`), `POST /api/v1/fenwick/query` (body `{lo, hi}` ‚Üí range sum), and `POST /api/v1/fenwick/point` (body `{index}` ‚Üí value); invalid input maps the core's `ValueError` to 422; all return `{"error": ...}` when no tree is configured. The `/api/v1/fenwick` prefix was verified free.
- ‚úÖ 80C: `tests/test_fenwick.py` ‚ÄĒ 30 unit tests (size validation; update/prefix-sum round-trip; `prefix_sum(0)=0`; cumulative sums; range_sum inclusive / single / full / identity; point_query after updates; accumulation; negative + float deltas; resize grow / shrink; clear; stats; out-of-bounds & lo>hi & bad-delta `ValueError`; 100-update correctness vs a reference array; million-element O(log n) timing; 10-thread exact-update concurrency).

**Phase 81 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 179 test modules green. Sovereign Segment Tree ‚ÄĒ O(log n) range queries (sum / min / max, fixed at construction) with point updates over a fixed-size array, more general than a Fenwick tree. Implemented as an iterative bottom-up tree (a flat `2¬∑n` array, leaves in `[n, 2n)`) for cache-friendly speed; sum/min/max are commutative + associative so the bottom-up combine order is correct. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- ‚úÖ 81A: `pradyos/core/segtree.py` ‚ÄĒ `SegmentTree(size, mode='sum')` (mode ‚ąą sum/min/max) with `update(i, val)` (1-indexed point *set*; int/float, may be negative), `query(lo, hi)` (inclusive range aggregate), `point_query(i)`, `resize(new_size)` (preserves the overlap, clears the extension), `clear()`, `size` / `mode` properties, and `stats()` (size / mode / aggregate). Invalid size, invalid mode, out-of-bounds indices, `lo > hi`, and non-numeric values raise `ValueError`. **Note:** uses the iterative `2¬∑n` layout rather than the textbook recursive `4¬∑n` because recursive Python missed the O(log n) latency budget on n=1M (‚Čą0.14 s vs ‚Čą0.08 s).
- ‚úÖ 81B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase81.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ‚ÄĒ added a `segtree: Any | None = None` param and 4 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/segtree` (stats), `POST /api/v1/segtree/update` (body `{index, value}`), `POST /api/v1/segtree/query` (body `{lo, hi}` ‚Üí `{mode, result}`), and `POST /api/v1/segtree/point` (body `{index}` ‚Üí value); invalid input maps the core's `ValueError` to 422; all return `{"error": ...}` when no tree is configured. The `/api/v1/segtree` prefix was verified free.

**Phase 82 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 181 test modules green. Sovereign Union-Find ‚ÄĒ a disjoint-set forest tracking a partition of n elements with effectively constant-time connectivity queries. Union by rank keeps trees shallow and path-halving `find` flattens them as a side effect of the query, giving the near-O(őĪ(n)) bound (őĪ ‚Č§ 4 for any practical n). 1-indexed. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`:

- ‚úÖ 82A: `pradyos/core/unionfind.py` ‚ÄĒ `UnionFind(size)` with `union(a, b)` (returns whether a merge happened; a self-union or an already-connected union is a no-op), `find(a)` (iterative path halving), `connected(a, b)`, `component_size(a)`, `component_count()`, `reset()`, `size` property, and `stats()` (size / components / largest_component). Out-of-bounds and non-integer elements raise `ValueError`. Rank (a height bound) drives unions; element counts are tracked separately for `component_size`.
- ‚úÖ 82B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase82.py` (never rewritten; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code) ‚ÄĒ added a `unionfind: Any | None = None` param and 4 endpoints: `GET /api/v1/unionfind` (stats), `POST /api/v1/unionfind/union` (body `{a, b}` ‚Üí `{united, components}`), `POST /api/v1/unionfind/find` (body `{a}` ‚Üí `{root, component_size}`), and `POST /api/v1/unionfind/connected` (body `{a, b}` ‚Üí `{connected}`); invalid input maps the core's `ValueError` to 422; all return `{"error": ...}` when no structure is configured. The `/api/v1/unionfind` prefix was verified free.
- ‚úÖ 82C: `tests/test_unionfind.py` ‚ÄĒ 30 unit tests (size validation; initial count; union return value / self-union & redundant-union no-ops; find singleton; connected / transitivity / shared-root; component-count decrement; component-size growth; union-all-into-one; reset; correctness vs a reference DSU; path-compression correctness; stats; boundaries i=1 / i=n; out-of-bounds & non-integer `ValueError`; O(őĪ(n)) 100k-ops-on-n=1M timing; 10-thread concurrency).
- ‚úÖ 82D: `tests/test_unionfind_web.py` ‚ÄĒ 16 FastAPI TestClient tests (no-structure errors on all four routes; stats keys; union merges / decrements / already-connected ‚Üí false / self ‚Üí no-op / out-of-bounds ‚Üí 422; find root + size / out-of-bounds ‚Üí 422; connected true / false / out-of-bounds ‚Üí 422; transitivity via sequential unions; plus a regression check that the Phase 77‚Äď81 routes are still live).

Sovereign Trie ‚ÄĒ a prefix tree mapping string keys to values: O(len(key)) insert / search / delete and an O(len(prefix) + matches) prefix scan (the primitive behind autocomplete and namespace lookups). Traversals are iterative (explicit stack) so a pathologically long key can never blow the recursion limit; deleting a key prunes its dangling node chain. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. **Structure note:** this phase introduces `pradyos/web/` ‚ÄĒ the routes live in their own module (`trie_web.py`) wired into the existing `create_app()` factory, with the trie held in factory scope (no module-level singleton).

Empty / non-string keys raise `ValueError`. Modelled on the Phase 70 `dependency_graph.py` template.

**Phase 84 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 185 test modules green. Sovereign LRU Cache ‚ÄĒ a fixed-capacity key‚Üívalue cache with least-recently-used eviction and optional per-key TTL. Backed by a `collections.OrderedDict` (a hash map over a doubly-linked list): every `get` / `put` moves the key to the most-recent end in O(1) and an overflow evicts the LRU front; expired keys are treated as misses and lazily purged. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/lru_web.py` module (the Phase 83 pattern), wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

The clock is injectable for deterministic TTL tests. Invalid capacity / ttl / key raise `ValueError`.

The static `/snapshot` + `/resize` routes are declared before `/{key}` so the path param never shadows them.

**Phase 85 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 187 test modules green. Sovereign Reservoir Sampler ‚ÄĒ draws a statistically uniform random sample of fixed size k from a stream of unknown length in O(k) memory and one pass (Vitter's Algorithm R): the first k items fill the reservoir, then the i-th item replaces a uniformly chosen slot with probability k/(i+1), so every item seen is equally likely (k/n) to be retained. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/reservoir_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 85A: `pradyos/core/reservoir.py` ‚ÄĒ `ReservoirError(capacity)`; `SovereignReservoir(k, random_fn=random.random)` with `feed(item)` (Algorithm R step), `feed_many(items)`, `sample()` (copy; unordered, ‚Č§ k), `reset(k=None)` (clear / resize), `__len__`, `capacity` / `seen` properties, and `stats()` (capacity / seen / filled). The RNG is injectable (zero-arg ‚Üí float in [0,1)) for deterministic tests. Invalid capacity raises `ReservoirError`.
- ‚úÖ 85B: `pradyos/web/reservoir_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_reservoir_routes(app, reservoir=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sampler, k=16) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/reservoir/feed` (body `{item}` or `{items: [...]}`; 422 on neither), `GET /api/v1/reservoir/sample`, `POST /api/v1/reservoir/reset` (body `{capacity?}`; 422 on bad capacity), `GET /api/v1/reservoir/stats`.
- ‚úÖ 85C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase85.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `reservoir` param, and a single `register_reservoir_routes(app, reservoir)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 85D: `tests/test_reservoir.py` (32) + `tests/test_reservoir_web.py` (16) ‚ÄĒ capacity validation + `ReservoirError`; fill behaviour (fewer / exactly / more than k); seen / filled / stats; sample-is-a-copy; deterministic Algorithm R + k=1 always / never-replace (injected RNG); statistical uniformity over 3000 seeded trials + a k=1 uniformity check; reset clear / resize / invalid; feed_many; arbitrary item types; 10-thread concurrency; all 4 endpoints incl. deterministic-over-HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 86 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 189 test modules green. Sovereign Cuckoo Filter ‚ÄĒ a probabilistic set-membership structure like the Phase 72 Bloom filter but supporting **deletion**. Each item is reduced to a small fingerprint stored in one of two candidate buckets via partial-key cuckoo hashing (`i1 = h(item) mod m`, `i2 = i1 XOR (h(fp) mod m)`); when both are full an existing fingerprint is "kicked" to its alternate bucket and the cascade repeats up to `max_kicks` times. A failed insert is rolled back atomically, so `contains` may false-positive (‚Čą `2¬∑bucket_size / 2^fp_bits`) but **never** false-negatives a present item. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/cuckoo_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 86A: `pradyos/core/cuckoo.py` ‚ÄĒ `CuckooError(detail)`; `SovereignCuckooFilter(capacity, bucket_size=4, fingerprint_bits=8, max_kicks=500, hash_fn=None)` with `insert(item)` ‚Üí bool (False if full after `max_kicks`; rolls back the kick cascade on failure ‚Üí no false negatives), `contains(item)` ‚Üí bool, `delete(item)` ‚Üí bool (False if absent), `reset()`, `__contains__`, `__len__`, `capacity` property, and `stats()` (capacity / count / load_factor / fingerprint_bits / max_kicks). Bucket count rounds up to a power of two so the XOR alternate-index is a clean involution; the hash is injectable for deterministic tests. Invalid config raises `CuckooError`.
- ‚úÖ 86B: `pradyos/web/cuckoo_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_cuckoo_routes(app, cuckoo=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app filter, capacity 1024) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/cuckoo/insert` (body `{item}`; 422 on missing), `POST /api/v1/cuckoo/contains`, `DELETE /api/v1/cuckoo/delete` (body `{item}`), `GET /api/v1/cuckoo/stats`, `POST /api/v1/cuckoo/reset`.
- ‚úÖ 86C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase86.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `cuckoo` param, and a single `register_cuckoo_routes(app, cuckoo)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 86D: `tests/test_cuckoo.py` (43) + `tests/test_cuckoo_web.py` (19) ‚ÄĒ insert / contains / delete correctness; delete-absent ‚Üí False; re-insert after delete; no-false-negative guarantee under saturation (rollback); injected-hash false positives + their clearing on delete; power-of-two capacity rounding + config validation / `CuckooError` (incl. `bool` rejection); load-factor tracking; full-filter max-kicks behaviour (single-bucket constant hash); seeded false-positive-rate bound + wider-fingerprint comparison; 10-thread concurrency + concurrent insert/delete; all 5 endpoints incl. deterministic membership-with-deletion over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.
- ‚úÖ 86E: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 189 test modules registered (Phase 86 appends `test_cuckoo.py` + `test_cuckoo_web.py`).
- ‚úÖ 86F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 87 planned.

**Phase 87 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 191 test modules green. Sovereign Top-K (Space-Saving) ‚ÄĒ a streaming heavy-hitters sketch that tracks the approximate `k` most frequent items in **bounded O(k) memory** regardless of stream length (Metwally‚ÄďAgrawal Space-Saving). At most `k` (item ‚Üí count, error) entries are monitored; a monitored item increments, an unmonitored one is admitted while fewer than `k` are tracked, and once full the **minimum-count** entry is evicted and reassigned to the new item (its count becomes `min_count + 1`, its error the evicted `min_count`). Because every step keeps the invariant `sum(counts) == total`, the minimum count is ‚Č§ `n/k` when full ‚ÄĒ giving the **heavy-hitter guarantee** (any item with true frequency > `n/k` is always monitored) and the **error bound** (a reported count over-estimates by at most its error ‚Č§ `n/k`). Where Phase 76's Count-Min Sketch answers point queries ("how often did X appear?"), this answers ranking ("what are the top K?") ‚ÄĒ together the complete approximate-frequency stack. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/topk_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 87A: `pradyos/core/space_saving.py` ‚ÄĒ `SpaceSavingError(detail)`; `SpaceSaving(k=10)` with `add(item)` / `add_many(items)` (items must be hashable; raises `TypeError` *before* mutating, so the sum-invariant survives a bad item), `count(item)` / `error(item)` (0 if unmonitored), `top(n=None)` (descending by count, ties keep first-monitored order), `reset(k=None)` (clear / resize), `__len__`, `__contains__`, `k` / `total` properties, and `stats()` (k / monitored / total / min_count). Invalid `k` raises `SpaceSavingError`.
- ‚úÖ 87B: `pradyos/web/topk_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_topk_routes(app, space_saving=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch, k=10) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/topk/insert` (body `{item}` or `{items: [...]}`; 422 on neither / non-list / unhashable), `GET /api/v1/topk/query` (`?n=N`, `Query(ge=0)` ‚Üí 422 on negative / non-int; omit N for all), `GET /api/v1/topk/stats`, `POST /api/v1/topk/reset` (body `{k?}`; 422 on bad k).
- ‚úÖ 87C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase87.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `space_saving` param, and a single `register_topk_routes(app, space_saving)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 87D: `tests/test_space_saving.py` (44) + `tests/test_topk_web.py` (20) ‚ÄĒ add / count / `add_many`; deterministic eviction (k=2 : a,b,a,c ‚Üí b evicted, c carries error 1); exact-before-eviction (error 0); top ordering / `n`-slicing / tie order / structure; heavy-hitter guarantee + correct ranking on a seeded skewed stream; `sum(counts) == total` invariant (incl. under 8-thread contention with eviction); error bound `est ‚ąí true ‚Č§ error ‚Č§ min_count`; k validation / `SpaceSavingError` (incl. `bool` & `float` rejection); stats / reset / resize; integer & mixed hashable items; unhashable-without-corruption; 10-thread concurrency; all 4 endpoints incl. deterministic eviction over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.
- ‚úÖ 87E: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 191 test modules registered (Phase 87 appends `test_space_saving.py` + `test_topk_web.py`).
- ‚úÖ 87F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 88 planned.

**Phase 88 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 193 test modules green. Sovereign MinHash ‚ÄĒ estimates the **Jaccard similarity** `|A‚ą©B| / |A‚ą™B|` of two sets in compact O(num_hashes) space, never storing raw members. For each of `num_hashes` universal hash functions it keeps, per named set, the *minimum* hashed value across that set's members (its "signature"); since `P[min_i(A) == min_i(B)] == Jaccard(A,B)`, the **fraction of signature positions where two sets agree is an unbiased estimate of their Jaccard similarity** (variance ‚ąĚ 1/num_hashes). The hash family is `h_i(x) = (a_i¬∑x + b_i) mod p` with `p = 2**61‚ąí1` and coefficients seeded once at init (deterministic given a fixed `seed`); members fold to a stable BLAKE2b integer so determinism holds across processes. Where Phase 74's HyperLogLog estimates *cardinality* and Phases 76/87 estimate *frequency*, this estimates set *similarity* ‚ÄĒ the Jaccard third of the sketch stack. A deliberate deviation from a loosely-sketched `‚Ä¶mod p mod num_hashes`: that final reduction collapses every hash into `[0, num_hashes)` and inflates all estimates toward 1.0 (empirically est 0.78 vs true 0.16), so the standard full-range construction is used. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/minhash_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 88A: `pradyos/core/minhash.py` ‚ÄĒ `MinHashError(detail)`; `MinHash(num_hashes=128, seed=0)` is a multi-set store (shared hash family + one signature per named set) with `add(set, element)` / `add_many(set, elements)`, `similarity(a, b)` ‚Üí Jaccard estimate (0.0 if either set is unknown), `signature(set)` (copy or None), `sets()`, `reset(num_hashes=None, seed=None)` (clear / reconfigure), `__len__`, `__contains__`, `num_hashes` / `seed` properties, and `stats()` (num_hashes / sets / total_added / seed). Invalid `num_hashes` or `seed` raises `MinHashError`.
- ‚úÖ 88B: `pradyos/web/minhash_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_minhash_routes(app, minhash=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app store, num_hashes=128) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/minhash/add` (body `{set, element}` or `{set, elements: [...]}`; 422 on missing set / neither / non-list), `GET /api/v1/minhash/similarity` (`?a=&b=`, required ‚Üí 422 if absent), `GET /api/v1/minhash/stats`, `POST /api/v1/minhash/reset` (body `{num_hashes?, seed?}`; 422 on bad num_hashes).
- ‚úÖ 88C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase88.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `minhash` param, and a single `register_minhash_routes(app, minhash)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 88D: `tests/test_minhash.py` (44) + `tests/test_minhash_web.py` (20) ‚ÄĒ add / signature / sets; self-similarity = 1.0, identical-content = 1.0, disjoint ‚Čą 0, missing-set = 0.0, symmetry; seeded accuracy (mean |error| < 0.05 at 256 hashes) + a 1/3-Jaccard estimate within 0.08; determinism + order-independence + idempotent re-add; the sum-of-minima monotone-non-increasing invariant + element-wise-min lowering + values within `2**61‚ąí1`; `num_hashes` / `seed` validation / `MinHashError` (incl. `bool` & `float` rejection, negative seed allowed); stats / reset / reconfigure; mixed element types; 10-thread concurrency + a same-set order-independent signature check; all 4 endpoints incl. deterministic Jaccard over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.
- ‚úÖ 88E: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 193 test modules registered (Phase 88 appends `test_minhash.py` + `test_minhash_web.py`).
- ‚úÖ 88F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 89 planned.

**Phase 89 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 195 test modules green. Sovereign SimHash ‚ÄĒ locality-sensitive fingerprints for **near-duplicate detection** (Charikar). A document (a bag of feature tokens) folds to a single `num_bits` integer: for every token we take a stable hash and, per bit position, cast a weighted vote (+1 if that bit of the token hash is set, ‚ąí1 otherwise); summing the votes over all tokens and thresholding at zero yields the fingerprint. Because votes are summed, it is a **bag-of-words** signature ‚ÄĒ token order is irrelevant, token frequency is not. The **Hamming distance** (popcount of the XOR) between two fingerprints measures dissimilarity: identical documents share every bit (distance 0), near-duplicates differ in only a handful of bits, and unrelated documents sit near `num_bits/2`; the normalized similarity is `1 ‚ąí hamming/num_bits`. At 64 bits a Hamming distance ‚Č§ `NEAR_DUPLICATE_HAMMING` (= 3, a documented module constant) is the conventional near-duplicate cutoff (Manku et al.). The token hash mixes in a `seed` (deterministic yet injectable) and uses BLAKE2b ‚ÄĒ not the salted built-in `hash` ‚ÄĒ so fingerprints reproduce across processes. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/simhash_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 89A: `pradyos/core/simhash.py` ‚ÄĒ `SimHashError(detail)` + `NEAR_DUPLICATE_HAMMING = 3`; `SimHash(num_bits=64, seed=0)` is a multi-document store with `hash(doc, tokens)` ‚Üí fingerprint int (stored), `fingerprint(doc)` (or None), `hamming(a, b)` / `similarity(a, b)` / `near_duplicate(a, b, threshold=3)` (all None if either doc is unknown), `documents()`, `reset(num_bits=None, seed=None)` (clear / reconfigure), `__len__`, `__contains__`, `num_bits` / `seed` properties, and `stats()` (num_bits / docs / total_hashed / seed). Invalid `num_bits` (‚Č§0 or >512) or non-int `seed` raises `SimHashError`.
- ‚úÖ 89B: `pradyos/web/simhash_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_simhash_routes(app, simhash=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app store, num_bits=64) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/simhash/hash` (body `{doc, tokens: [...]}`; 422 on missing doc / non-list tokens), `GET /api/v1/simhash/similarity` (`?a=&b=`, required ‚Üí 422 if absent, 404 on unknown doc), `GET /api/v1/simhash/hamming` (adds a `near_duplicate` flag; 404 on unknown doc), `GET /api/v1/simhash/stats`, `POST /api/v1/simhash/reset` (body `{num_bits?, seed?}`; 422 on bad num_bits).
- ‚úÖ 89C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase89.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `simhash` param, and a single `register_simhash_routes(app, simhash)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.

**Phase 90 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 197 test modules green. Sovereign Quotient Filter ‚ÄĒ a cache-friendly approximate-membership structure (Bender et al., "Don't Thrash") that, unlike the Phase 72 Bloom filter, supports **exact deletion, duplicate counting, and merging**. Each item folds to a `q + r` bit fingerprint, split into a *quotient* `fq = fp >> r` (the canonical slot, one of `2**q`) and a *remainder* `fr = fp & (2**r ‚ąí 1)` (stored in the slot). Collisions are resolved by linear probing, with three metadata bits per slot ‚ÄĒ `is_occupied`, `is_continuation`, `is_shifted` ‚ÄĒ that keep every quotient's remainders in one contiguous sorted *run* and group overlapping runs into *clusters*; those bits alone drive run/cluster navigation (no quotient is stored ‚ÄĒ that is the space win). Deletion is exact (no false negatives), duplicates are counted natively, and a membership test false-*positives* with probability `‚Čą 2**(-r)`. Pure stdlib; the hash is injectable for deterministic tests; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/quotient_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 90A: `pradyos/core/quotient.py` ‚ÄĒ `QuotientError(detail)`; `QuotientFilter(q=8, r=8, seed=0, hash_fn=None)` with `insert(item)` ‚Üí bool (False only when full), `contains(item)` ‚Üí bool, `count(item)` ‚Üí int, `delete(item)` ‚Üí bool (exact; decrements the duplicate count, contracting the cluster when it hits 0), `merge(other)` (same `q`/`r`), `reset(q=None, r=None, seed=None)`, `__contains__`, `__len__`, `q` / `remainder_bits` / `slots` properties, and `stats()` (q / slots / remainder_bits / used / items / load_factor / `false_positive_rate = 2**-r`). Invalid config raises `QuotientError`. The canonical Bender et al. insert/delete maintain the three metadata bits and reconstruct shifted-bits on delete via run-by-run quotient tracking.
- ‚úÖ 90B: `pradyos/web/quotient_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_quotient_routes(app, quotient=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app filter, q=10 ‚Üí 1024 slots) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/quotient/insert` (body `{item}`; returns count), `POST /api/v1/quotient/contains` (returns count), `DELETE /api/v1/quotient/delete` (body `{item}`), `GET /api/v1/quotient/stats`, `POST /api/v1/quotient/reset` (body `{q?, r?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config). 422 on missing item.
- ‚úÖ 90C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase90.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `quotient` param, and a single `register_quotient_routes(app, quotient)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 90D: `tests/test_quotient.py` (46) + `tests/test_quotient_web.py` (21) ‚ÄĒ insert / contains / delete / count correctness; no-false-negatives (500 inserted); duplicate counting + delete-decrement + delete-to-zero; **run/cluster navigation** ‚ÄĒ 40 items sharing one quotient all found, mid-run and run-head deletes, adjacent-quotient runs; a **randomized differential test vs `collections.Counter`** (6 seeds √ó 2000 ops, injected distinct-fingerprint hash ‚Üí exact); seeded false-positive-rate bound + wider-remainder comparison; merge (count-accumulating; mismatched `q`/non-filter ‚Üí `QuotientError`); full-filter ‚Üí False; `q`/`r`/`seed` validation (bool & float rejection); stats / `false_positive_rate` formula / reset / reconfigure; determinism via injected hash; 10-thread concurrency + concurrent insert/delete; all 5 endpoints incl. run-collision over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 91 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 199 test modules green. Sovereign GK Quantile Sketch (Greenwald‚ÄďKhanna, 2001) ‚ÄĒ streaming **őĶ-approximate quantiles** (p50/p95/p99) over an unbounded stream in `O((1/őĶ)¬∑log(őĶn))` space, with a hard guarantee: the value returned for a quantile `ŌÜ` has true rank within `¬Ī‚ĆąőĶn‚ĆČ` of the requested rank. The summary is a value-sorted list of tuples `(v, g, őĒ)` where `g = r_min(v_i) ‚ąí r_min(v_{i‚ąí1})` (so `r_min(v_i) = ő£ g_j`) and `őĒ = r_max(v_i) ‚ąí r_min(v_i)`; the invariant `g_i + őĒ_i ‚Č§ ‚Ćä2őĶn‚Ćč` is what bounds the error. **Insert** places `v` in sorted order with `g = 1`, `őĒ = ‚Ćä2őĶn‚Ćč` (new min/max get `őĒ = 0` ‚ÄĒ exact extremes). **Compress** (every `‚Ćä1/2őĶ‚Ćč` inserts) merges an adjacent pair when `g_i + g_{i+1} + őĒ_{i+1} ‚Č§ ‚Ćä2őĶn‚Ćč`, which preserves the invariant. **Query** for rank `r = ‚ĆąŌÜn‚ĆČ` returns the first `v` whose running `r_min` exceeds `r ‚ąí őĶn`; the invariant then guarantees `r_max ‚Č§ r + őĶn`. GK is deterministic by construction (`seed` is accepted for parity). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/gk_quantile_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 91A: `pradyos/core/gk_quantile.py` ‚ÄĒ `GKError(detail)`; `GKSummary(epsilon=0.01, seed=0)` with `insert(value)` / `insert_many(values)` (numbers only), `query(phi)` ‚Üí ŌÜ-quantile (None if empty; `GKError` on `ŌÜ‚ąČ[0,1]`), `count()`, `compress()`, `reset(epsilon=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `epsilon` / `seed` / `summary_size` properties, and `stats()` (epsilon / n / summary_size / capacity = `(1/2őĶ)¬∑log2(2őĶn)`). Invalid `epsilon` (‚ąČ(0,1)) / `seed` / value / `phi` raise `GKError`.
- ‚úÖ 91B: `pradyos/web/gk_quantile_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_gk_quantile_routes(app, gk=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app summary, őĶ=0.01) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/quantile/insert` (body `{value}` or `{values: [...]}`; 422 on neither / non-list / non-number), `GET /api/v1/quantile/query` (`?phi=`, `Query(ge=0.0, le=1.0)` ‚Üí 422 on ŌÜ‚ąČ[0,1]; **422 on empty summary**), `GET /api/v1/quantile/count`, `GET /api/v1/quantile/stats`, `POST /api/v1/quantile/reset` (body `{epsilon?, seed?}`; 422 on bad epsilon).
- ‚úÖ 91C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase91.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `gk_quantile` param, and a single `register_gk_quantile_routes(app, gk_quantile)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 91D: `tests/test_gk_quantile.py` (44) + `tests/test_gk_quantile_web.py` (22) ‚ÄĒ insert / count / query; median accuracy on 10k uniform (`|est‚ąí0.5| ‚Č§ őĶ + 2/n`); exact min/max; **rank-error guarantee** (every p10‚Äďp99 within `őĶn`, incl. an adversarial sorted stream); monotonicity across 101 quantiles; order-independence of *estimates* (ascending vs reversed); summary-size sub-linear / below `O((1/őĶ)log(őĶn))`; őĶ effect on size; determinism (seed is a no-op ‚ÄĒ GK has no RNG); epsilon / seed / value / phi validation + `GKError`; stats / capacity / reset / reconfigure; duplicate & negative values; 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. empty-summary ‚Üí 422 + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 92 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 201 test modules green. Sovereign KLL Sketch (Karnin‚ÄďLang‚ÄďLiberty, 2016) ‚ÄĒ a randomized, space-optimal, natively **mergeable** streaming-quantile sketch. It maintains a hierarchy of *compactors* (one list per level `h`); an item stored at level `h` carries weight `2**h`. New items enter level 0; when a compactor reaches capacity `k` it **compacts** ‚ÄĒ sort, randomly keep the even- or odd-indexed half (a fair coin discards one of each adjacent pair), and promote the survivors up a level. Each compaction conserves total weight, so `ő£ 2**h == n` always holds; compaction bounds total stored size to `O(k¬∑log(n/k))` while levels grow as `O(log(n/k))`, giving `O(n/k)` rank error with high probability. **Query** flattens every stored item with its weight, sorts, and returns the weighted-rank `‚ĆąŌÜn‚ĆČ` value. **Merge** ‚ÄĒ the defining advantage over Phase 91's GK ‚ÄĒ aligns two sketches level-by-level, concatenates the compactors, and re-compacts, combining distributed sketches with the same guarantee. Randomness is per-*compaction* (a `random.Random(seed)` advancing each compaction), so a fixed insert sequence is deterministic. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/kll_sketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 92A: `pradyos/core/kll_sketch.py` ‚ÄĒ `KLLError(detail)`; `KLLSketch(k=200, seed=0)` with `update(value)` / `update_many(values)`, `query(phi)` ‚Üí ŌÜ-quantile (None if empty; `KLLError` on ŌÜ‚ąČ[0,1]), `rank(value)` (weighted), `merge(other)` (level-aligned re-compaction), `count()`, `reset(k=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `k` / `seed` / `num_levels` properties, and `stats()` (k / n / num_levels / num_compactors / sketch_size_ratio). Invalid `k` (<2) / `seed` / value / `phi` raise `KLLError`. (Uniform per-level capacity `k`: a starved top compactor would let a few heavy items skew the estimate, so every weight keeps a full-resolution buffer ‚ÄĒ measured ratio ‚Čą 0.03 at n=10k.)
- ‚úÖ 92B: `pradyos/web/kll_sketch_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_kll_sketch_routes(app, kll=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch, k=200) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/kll/insert` (body `{value}` or `{values: [...]}`; 422 on neither / non-list / non-number), `GET /api/v1/kll/query` (`?phi=`, `Query(ge=0.0, le=1.0)`; **422 on empty sketch**), `POST /api/v1/kll/merge` (body `{values: [...]}` ‚Üí builds a temp sketch and merges it in), `GET /api/v1/kll/stats`, `POST /api/v1/kll/reset` (body `{k?, seed?}`; 422 on bad k).
- ‚úÖ 92C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase92.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `kll` param, and a single `register_kll_sketch_routes(app, kll)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 92D: `tests/test_kll_sketch.py` (45) + `tests/test_kll_sketch_web.py` (24) ‚ÄĒ update / count / query; rank-error guarantee ‚ÄĒ every p0‚Äďp100 (incl. extremes) within `3n/k` on uniform and adversarial sorted streams; monotonicity; weighted `rank()` bounds; **merge** (median accuracy, count combination, preserved rank error, empty-into-populated, non-sketch ‚Üí `KLLError`); space ratio < 0.1 + level growth + the `ő£ weights == n` invariant; determinism (same seed ‚Üí identical levels); k (<2) / seed / value / phi validation + `KLLError`; stats / reset / reconfigure; duplicate & negative values; 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. the merge endpoint + empty ‚Üí 422 + a prior-phase regression check.
