**Phase 93 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 203 test modules green. Sovereign Theta Sketch (K-Minimum-Values) ‚ÄĒ distinct-count (cardinality) estimation that, unlike Phase 74's HyperLogLog, supports a **lossless set union** of two sketches. Each element is hashed uniformly into `[0, 1)`; the sketch retains the `k` smallest *distinct* hashes. Once `k` distinct hashes are retained, `őł` is the largest of them (the `k`-th smallest), so `estimate = (k ‚ąí 1) / őł`; below the threshold the retained count is the exact distinct count. Duplicates hash to an already-retained value and are ignored ‚ÄĒ repeats never inflate the count. Relative error is `‚Čą 1/‚ąö(k‚ąí1)` (‚Čą 1.6 % at `k = 4096`). **Union** keeps the `k` smallest hashes of the two retained sets (itself a valid KMV sketch of `A ‚ą™ B`); **intersection** follows by inclusion‚Äďexclusion `|A ‚ą© B| ‚Čą est(A) + est(B) ‚ąí est(A ‚ą™ B)`. The BLAKE2b hash is seeded for determinism. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/theta_sketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 93A: `pradyos/core/theta_sketch.py` ‚ÄĒ `ThetaError(detail)`; `ThetaSketch(k=4096, seed=0)` with `update(element)` / `update_many(elements)`, `estimate()` (0 when empty; exact int below `k`), `merge(other)` (mutating union), `union_estimate(other)` / `intersection_estimate(other)` (non-destructive), `reset(k=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `k` / `seed` / `retained_count` / `is_exact` properties, and `stats()` (k / n / theta / retained_count / is_exact / estimate). A max-heap of retained hashes gives O(log k) eviction; a set gives O(1) dedup. Invalid `k` (<2) / `seed` raise `ThetaError`.
- ‚úÖ 93B: `pradyos/web/theta_sketch_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_theta_sketch_routes(app, theta=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch, k=4096) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/theta/insert` (body `{element}` or `{elements: [...]}`; 422 on neither / non-list), `GET /api/v1/theta/estimate` (**0 when empty ‚ÄĒ never 422**), `POST /api/v1/theta/merge` (`?op=union|intersection`, default union ‚ÄĒ union mutates & returns `|A‚ą™B|`, intersection is non-destructive & returns `|A‚ą©B|`; 422 on bad op / missing values), `GET /api/v1/theta/stats`, `POST /api/v1/theta/reset` (body `{k?, seed?}`; 422 on bad k).
- ‚úÖ 93C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase93.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `theta` param, and a single `register_theta_sketch_routes(app, theta)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 93D: `tests/test_theta_sketch.py` (45) + `tests/test_theta_sketch_web.py` (24) ‚ÄĒ 10k-distinct estimate within 5 %; duplicates ‚Üí exactly 1; exact regime below `k` (estimate == count, `is_exact`); larger-`k` tighter error; **union** (no-overlap ‚Üí ~2√ó, full-overlap ‚Üí ~1√ó, non-destructive `union_estimate`, count combination, empty/populated edges); **intersection** by inclusion‚Äďexclusion (2500-overlap within 10 %, disjoint ‚Čą 0, full overlap); őł = 1.0 below `k` / <1 when full; retained-count caps at `k`; determinism (same seed ‚Üí identical retained set) ; k (<2) / seed validation + `ThetaError`; stats / reset / reconfigure; integer elements; 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. `op=union|intersection` (incl. non-destructive intersection) + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 94 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 205 test modules green. Sovereign Count Sketch (Charikar‚ÄďChen‚ÄďFarach-Colton, 2002) ‚ÄĒ sub-linear **frequency** estimation that, unlike Phase 76's Count-Min Sketch, gives an **unbiased** estimate. A `depth √ó width` integer table is paired with a *bucket* hash `h_i` and a *sign* hash `s_i ‚ąą {‚ąí1, +1}` per row; each `(element, count)` update adds `s_i(element)¬∑count` to `table[i][h_i(element)]`, and a point query returns the **median** of the `depth` signed readings `table[i][h_i(x)]¬∑s_i(x)`. The sign flip makes collision noise cancel in expectation ‚ÄĒ the estimator is unbiased (vs Count-Min's always-positive `min`, which only over-counts). The trade-off is symmetric noise: a never-inserted element can read a small **negative** estimate when it collides with negatively-signed updates (expected and correct). The median over rows tolerates a few heavily-collided rows; updates accept **negative counts** (deletion). A side dict of every element seen powers `heavy_hitters(threshold)` (the sketch itself is not enumerable). Pure stdlib; the hash families are injectable for tests; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/count_sketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 94A: `pradyos/core/count_sketch.py` ‚ÄĒ `CountSketchError(detail)`; `CountSketch(depth=5, width=2048, seed=0, bucket_fn=None, sign_fn=None)` with `update(element, count=1)` (count may be negative ‚Üí deletion), `estimate(element)` (signed median; 0 for unseen in an empty table), `heavy_hitters(threshold)` ‚Üí elements above `threshold¬∑total_count`, highest first, `reset(depth=None, width=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `depth` / `width` / `seed` / `total_count` / `unique_elements` properties, and `stats()` (depth / width / total_count / unique_elements / table_cells). Two seeded BLAKE2b hash families (bucket + sign); invalid config / non-int count raise `CountSketchError`.
- ‚úÖ 94B: `pradyos/web/count_sketch_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_count_sketch_routes(app, count_sketch=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch, depth 5 √ó width 2048) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/countsketch/update` (`?count=N`, default 1, may be negative; body `{element}` or `{elements: [...]}`; elements normalised to str), `GET /api/v1/countsketch/estimate` (`?element=`, required ‚Üí 422 absent; **0 for unseen, never 422**), `GET /api/v1/countsketch/heavy_hitters` (`?threshold=`, `Query(ge=0.0, le=1.0)`), `GET /api/v1/countsketch/stats`, `POST /api/v1/countsketch/reset` (body `{depth?, width?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ‚úÖ 94C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase94.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `count_sketch` param, and a single `register_count_sketch_routes(app, count_sketch)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 94D: `tests/test_count_sketch.py` (41) + `tests/test_count_sketch_web.py` (25) ‚ÄĒ single-element **unbiasedness** (10k ‚Üí exactly 10k, no inflation amid 5k singletons); **heavy hitters** on a Zipf stream (top-3 identified & ranked, none above 0.99, sorted desc, threshold validation); **deletion** via negative count (1000‚ąí300 ‚Üí 700, delete-to-zero); **collision tolerance** (2048 elements forced into one row-0 bucket via injected hash ‚Üí median still recovers 1); **negative estimate** for an unseen colliding element (documented trade-off); determinism (same seed ‚Üí identical table); depth/width/seed/count validation + `CountSketchError`; stats / table_cells / reset / reconfigure; integer elements; 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. `?count=` deletion over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 95 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 207 test modules green. Sovereign Lossy Counting (Manku‚ÄďMotwani, 2002) ‚ÄĒ **deterministic** approximate frequency / heavy-hitter detection with a clean őĶ-error guarantee and *no hashing*. The stream is divided into buckets of width `w = ‚Ćą1/őĶ‚ĆČ`, numbered `1, 2, ‚Ä¶`; a dictionary holds `{element: (freq, őĒ)}` where `őĒ` bounds the count's under-estimate. On each arrival the element's `freq` is incremented, or it is inserted as `(count, b_current ‚ąí 1)`; at every bucket boundary the table is swept and every entry with `freq + őĒ ‚Č§ b_current` is deleted. This guarantees **no false negatives** (every element with true frequency ‚Č• `support¬∑n` is returned by `heavy_hitters(support)`), **no false positives above threshold** (every returned element has true frequency ‚Č• `(support ‚ąí őĶ)¬∑n`), and a **space bound** of `(1/őĶ)¬∑log(őĶn)` entries. The algorithm is fully deterministic (no RNG ‚ÄĒ `seed` is accepted for parity but unused), and **append-only**: a negative `count` raises `LossyCountError` (deletion is unsupported by design). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/lossy_count_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 95A: `pradyos/core/lossy_count.py` ‚ÄĒ `LossyCountError(detail)`; `LossyCount(epsilon=0.001, seed=None)` with `update(element, count=1)` (negative count ‚Üí `LossyCountError("‚Ä¶does not support deletion")`; count=0 is a no-op), `estimate(element)` ‚Üí tracked frequency (0 if absent), `heavy_hitters(support)` ‚Üí elements with freq ‚Č• `(support ‚ąí őĶ)¬∑n`, highest first, `reset(epsilon=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `epsilon` / `bucket_width` / `n` / `entries` properties, and `stats()` (epsilon / n / bucket_width / entries / current_bucket). The bucket-boundary sweep loop handles batch counts crossing multiple boundaries. Invalid `epsilon` (‚ąČ(0,1)) / non-int count raise `LossyCountError`.
- ‚úÖ 95B: `pradyos/web/lossy_count_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_lossy_count_routes(app, lossy=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app counter, őĶ=0.001) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/lossycount/update` (`?count=N`; body `{element}` or `{elements: [...]}`; **negative count ‚Üí 422 "does not support deletion"**; elements normalised to str), `GET /api/v1/lossycount/estimate` (`?element=`, required ‚Üí 422 absent; 0 if not retained), `GET /api/v1/lossycount/heavy_hitters` (`?support=`, `Query(gt=0, le=1.0)`), `GET /api/v1/lossycount/stats`, `POST /api/v1/lossycount/reset` (body `{epsilon?}`; 422 on bad epsilon).

Existing routes untouched.

**Phase 96 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 209 test modules green. Sovereign DDSketch (Masson‚ÄďLee, 2019) ‚ÄĒ a **relative-error** quantile sketch (a different guarantee from the *rank*-error sketches of Phases 91/92). Each positive value `v` is mapped to a logarithmic bucket `i = ‚Ćąlog_ő≥(v)‚ĆČ` with `ő≥ = (1+őĪ)/(1‚ąíőĪ)`, and a dict `{bucket ‚Üí count}` tallies them; a quantile query walks the buckets in value order to the `q`-th item and returns that bucket's representative value `r_i = 2¬∑ő≥**i/(ő≥+1)` (the geometric midpoint, whose worst-case relative error is exactly `(ő≥‚ąí1)/(ő≥+1) = őĪ`). So for any quantile `q` with true value `v`, the estimate satisfies `|vŐā ‚ąí v|/v ‚Č§ őĪ` regardless of distribution ‚ÄĒ ideal for long-tailed latencies where p99 accuracy matters proportionally. **Merge** adds per-bucket counts of two same-`őĪ` sketches ‚ÄĒ *exact*, not approximate (the key differentiator over t-Digest), so distributed sketches compose losslessly. Deterministic (`seed` accepted but unused); non-positive values are rejected. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/ddsketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 96A: `pradyos/core/ddsketch.py` ‚ÄĒ `DDSketchError(detail)`; `DDSketch(alpha=0.01, seed=None)` with `update(value, count=1)` (value > 0 or `DDSketchError("DDSketch requires positive values")`; count ‚Č• 1), `quantile(q)` ‚Üí relative-error estimate (None if empty; `DDSketchError` on q‚ąČ[0,1]), `merge(other)` (exact bucket-count union; same `őĪ` or `DDSketchError`), `reset(alpha=None, seed=None)`, `count()`, `__len__`, `alpha` / `gamma` / `num_buckets` properties, and `stats()` (alpha / gamma / n / num_buckets / min / max). Representative value uses the standard `2¬∑ő≥**i/(ő≥+1)` (which bounds relative error by `őĪ`) ‚ÄĒ not a naive `(1+őĪ)**i`, which mixes bases and would not bound the error. Invalid `alpha` (‚ąČ(0,1)) raises `DDSketchError`.
- ‚úÖ 96B: `pradyos/web/ddsketch_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_ddsketch_routes(app, ddsketch=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch, őĪ=0.01) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/ddsketch/update` (`?value=` `Query(gt=0)` ‚Üí **422 on non-positive**, `?count=` `Query(ge=1)`, or body `{values: [...]}`), `GET /api/v1/ddsketch/quantile` (`?q=`, `Query(ge=0, le=1)`; **422 on empty sketch**), `POST /api/v1/ddsketch/merge` (body `{values: [...]}` ‚Üí builds a same-`őĪ` sketch and merges it in ‚ÄĒ the single-shared-sketch server's composability demonstration), `GET /api/v1/ddsketch/stats`, `POST /api/v1/ddsketch/reset` (body `{alpha?}`; 422 on bad alpha).
- ‚úÖ 96C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase96.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `ddsketch` param, and a single `register_ddsketch_routes(app, ddsketch)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 96D: `tests/test_ddsketch.py` (45) + `tests/test_ddsketch_web.py` (24) ‚ÄĒ uniform & exponential & wide-range (1..1e6) streams with **every quantile level within `őĪ` relative error**; monotonicity; extremes within `őĪ`; **exact merge** (merged sketch identical to a single sketch of all values) + preserved relative error + min/max update + alpha-mismatch/non-sketch ‚Üí `DDSketchError`; non-positive value guard (`update(0)`/`update(-1)` raise) + invalid count; determinism (seed ignored); alpha / q validation + `gamma` formula; stats / sub-linear bucket count / reset / reconfigure; floats below 1; 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. the merge endpoint + empty ‚Üí 422 + a prior-phase regression check.

Sovereign Exponential Histogram (Datar‚ÄďGionis‚ÄďIndyk‚ÄďMotwani, 2002) ‚ÄĒ the first **sliding-window** primitive: how many 1-bits occurred in the last `window` ticks of a binary stream, in `O((1/őĶ)¬∑log¬≤(window))` space (it never stores the raw stream). The window is summarised by buckets `(timestamp, size=2ŠĶŹ)` ordered oldest‚Üínewest; each update appends a size-1 bucket at the current tick, then ‚ÄĒ while more than `k = ‚Ćą1/őĶ‚ĆČ` buckets share a size ‚ÄĒ merges the two **oldest** of that size into one of double the size (taking the newer timestamp); buckets older than `window` ticks expire. `count()` returns `ő£ size ‚ąí ¬Ĺ¬∑(oldest bucket size)` (the DGIM end-correction, since the oldest bucket may straddle the boundary), estimating the windowed count with **relative error ‚Č§ őĶ/2** (empirically validated). Deterministic (`seed` accepted but unused); a binary-stream model (`value` = number of 1-bits at a tick; no fractional/weighted updates). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/exponential_histogram_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 97A: `pradyos/core/exponential_histogram.py` ‚ÄĒ `ExponentialHistogramError(detail)`; `ExponentialHistogram(window, epsilon=0.5, seed=None)` with `update(value=1, timestamp=None)` (value ‚Č• 1 1-bits; timestamp defaults to the next internal tick, must be non-decreasing else `ExponentialHistogramError`), `count()` ‚Üí DGIM windowed estimate, `oldest()` ‚Üí oldest surviving bucket timestamp (None if empty), `reset(window=None, epsilon=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `window` / `epsilon` / `k` / `now` / `num_buckets` properties, and `stats()` (window / epsilon / k / num_buckets / count / oldest / now). Invalid `window` (‚Č§0) / `epsilon` (‚ąČ(0,1]) raise `ExponentialHistogramError`.
- ‚úÖ 97B: `pradyos/web/exponential_histogram_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_exponential_histogram_routes(app, histogram=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app histogram, window=1000) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/window/update` (`?value=` `Query(ge=1)`, `?timestamp=` `Query(ge=0)`; **422 on non-monotone timestamp**), `GET /api/v1/window/count`, `GET /api/v1/window/oldest`, `GET /api/v1/window/stats`, `POST /api/v1/window/reset` (`?window=` `Query(gt=0)`, `?epsilon=` `Query(gt=0, le=1)`; 422 on bad params).
- ‚úÖ 97C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase97.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `exp_histogram` param, and a single `register_exponential_histogram_routes(app, exp_histogram)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 97D: `tests/test_exponential_histogram.py` (42) + `tests/test_exponential_histogram_web.py` (20) ‚ÄĒ dense count within `őĶ/2` (incl. the directive's window=500/őĶ=0.5 scenario, tighter őĶ, and sub-window n); **sliding expiry** (200 then advance 600 then 100 ‚Üí ~100); old-buckets-expire + expiry invariant + oldest-advances; **merge invariant** (‚Č§ `k+1` buckets per size after every update) + power-of-two sizes + poly-log space; explicit timestamps + multi-bit `value`; determinism (seed ignored); window/epsilon/value/non-monotone-timestamp validation + `ExponentialHistogramError`; stats / reset / reconfigure; the single-bit DGIM end-correction (`count`=0.5); 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. sliding expiry over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 98 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 213 test modules green. Sovereign Weighted Reservoir Sampling (Efraimidis‚ÄďSpirakis "A-Res", 2006) ‚ÄĒ a random sample of `k` items from a stream of `(item, weight)` pairs in one pass and `O(k)` space, where an item is retained with probability **proportional to its weight** (unlike Phase 85's *uniform* Algorithm R). Each arrival gets a priority key `u**(1/weight)` (`u ‚ąľ Uniform(0,1)`); a **min-heap** keeps the `k` items with the largest keys (push while under capacity, else replace the smallest if beaten). Heavier weights drive `1/weight` toward 0 and thus the key toward 1, so heavy items win more ‚ÄĒ verified empirically at a ~96:1 selection ratio for weight 100 vs 1. This is the first **randomized** primitive in a while: a seeded `random.Random` makes it reproducible/injectable. `reset()` clears the reservoir but deliberately does *not* re-seed the RNG (the generator state continues ‚ÄĒ correct for a long-lived sampler). A counter tiebreaker `(key, counter, item)` means the heap never compares items, so any item type is safe. Weights must be positive; `k ‚Č• 1`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/weighted_reservoir_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 98A: `pradyos/core/weighted_reservoir.py` ‚ÄĒ `WeightedReservoirError(detail)`; `WeightedReservoir(k, seed=0)` with `update(item, weight=1.0)` (weight > 0 or `WeightedReservoirError("weight must be positive")`), `sample()` ‚Üí reservoir contents (`[]` if empty, order not guaranteed), `reset()` (clears; RNG continues), `__len__`, `k` / `seed` / `n` / `size` properties, and `stats()` (k / n / size / seed). `k < 1` raises `WeightedReservoirError("k must be at least 1")`. No `merge` ‚ÄĒ A-Res reservoirs are not composable.
- ‚úÖ 98B: `pradyos/web/weighted_reservoir_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_weighted_reservoir_routes(app, reservoir=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sampler, k=100) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/sample/update` (`?item=` required str, `?weight=` `Query(gt=0)` ‚Üí **422 on non-positive**), `GET /api/v1/sample/sample` (`{items, n, k}`), `GET /api/v1/sample/stats`, `POST /api/v1/sample/reset`.
- ‚úÖ 98C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase98.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `weighted_reservoir` param, and a single `register_weighted_reservoir_routes(app, weighted_reservoir)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 98D: `tests/test_weighted_reservoir.py` (35) + `tests/test_weighted_reservoir_web.py` (18) ‚ÄĒ capacity fills to `k` (10k items ‚Üí 50) / under-capacity keeps all / exactly-k; **weight-proportional bias** (weight 100 selected >10√ó weight 1; top-10 by frequency all from the top-20 by weight) + uniform-weights-unbiased; determinism (same seed ‚Üí identical reservoir) + different-seed-differs; **reset does not re-seed the RNG** (replay diverges from a fresh same-seed reservoir); weight guard (0 / negative / non-number raise) + `k`/`seed` validation + `WeightedReservoirError`; arbitrary non-comparable item types (counter tiebreaker); stats / reset / refill; 10-thread concurrency; all 4 endpoints incl. injected capacity + a high-weight-retained check + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 99 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 215 test modules green. Sovereign Misra-Gries (Misra‚ÄďGries, 1982) ‚ÄĒ the original **deterministic counter-based heavy-hitter** algorithm. At most `k` monitored `(item ‚Üí count)` counters are kept: on a hit increment; on a new item with a free slot start a counter; otherwise **decrement every counter** by the item's count and drop those that reach zero (the arriving item is absorbed by that decrement, not stored). This is the distinctive Misra-Gries step ‚ÄĒ compared with Space-Saving's *evict-minimum* (P87) and Lossy Counting's *window-sweep* (P95). Guarantees: any element with true frequency `> n/(k+1)` is retained; every reported count under-estimates the true frequency by at most `n/(k+1)`; space is exactly `k` counters. So `heavy_hitters(support)` (counts `‚Č• (support ‚ąí 1/(k+1))¬∑n`) has no false negatives among elements with true frequency `‚Č• support¬∑n` **provided `support > 1/(k+1)`** (a larger `k` covers smaller support). Deterministic (no RNG ‚ÄĒ `seed` accepted but unused); append-only (non-positive `count` raises `MisraGriesError`). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/misra_gries_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 99A: `pradyos/core/misra_gries.py` ‚ÄĒ `MisraGriesError(detail)`; `MisraGries(k, seed=None)` with `update(element, count=1)` (count ‚Č• 1; non-positive ‚Üí `MisraGriesError("Misra-Gries does not support deletion")`), `estimate(element)` ‚Üí stored under-count (0 if absent), `heavy_hitters(support)` ‚Üí elements with count `‚Č• (support ‚ąí 1/(k+1))¬∑n`, highest first, `reset(k=None)`, `__len__`, `k` / `n` / `counters` properties, and `stats()` (k / n / counters / `threshold = n/(k+1)`). `k < 1` raises `MisraGriesError("k must be at least 1")`.
- ‚úÖ 99B: `pradyos/web/misra_gries_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_misra_gries_routes(app, misra=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app counter, k=100) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/misragries/update` (`?count=` `Query(ge=1)` ‚Üí **422 on non-positive (the no-deletion guard)**; body `{element}` or `{elements: [...]}`), `GET /api/v1/misragries/estimate` (`?element=`, required ‚Üí 422 absent), `GET /api/v1/misragries/heavy_hitters` (`?support=`, `Query(gt=0, le=1)`), `GET /api/v1/misragries/stats`, `POST /api/v1/misragries/reset` (body `{k?}`; 422 on bad k).
- ‚úÖ 99C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase99.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `misra_gries` param, and a single `register_misra_gries_routes(app, misra_gries)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 99D: `tests/test_misra_gries.py` (40) + `tests/test_misra_gries_web.py` (25) ‚ÄĒ Zipf no-false-negatives at `support=0.05` with `k=20` (so `support > 1/(k+1)`) + correct ranking; the **rigorous retention guarantee** (every element with freq `> n/(k+1)` retained, tested at `k=10`); under-count bounded by `n/(k+1)`; estimate never over-counts; the **decrement-all** step (a,b,c at k=2 ‚Üí empty table; batch `a√ó5, b√ó3, c-miss√ó2 ‚Üí a=3, b=1`); counter cap ‚Č§ k; monitored-increment / free-slot-insert; no-deletion guard (count 0 / negative / non-int raise); determinism (seed ignored); k validation + `MisraGriesError`; support validation; stats / `threshold` / reset / reconfigure; integer elements; 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. the Zipf no-false-negative check over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 100 ‚ÄĒ Complete. ūüéĮ Centennial.** All 217 test modules green. Sovereign XOR Filter (Graf‚ÄďLemire, 2020) ‚ÄĒ a **static, space-optimal** approximate-membership filter that beats Bloom (P72) and Cuckoo (P86) on lookup speed (exactly **three memory probes, no search**) and is built **once** from a complete key set (then immutable ‚ÄĒ the design difference from the incremental Bloom and Cuckoo). Each key maps to three buckets `h0, h1, h2` (one per segment); a **peeling** construction repeatedly removes a key that owns a bucket no other unassigned key touches, then assigns fingerprints in reverse peel order so `F[b] = fingerprint(k) ‚äē F[other1] ‚äē F[other2]` ‚ÄĒ making `fingerprint(k) == F[h0] ‚äē F[h1] ‚äē F[h2]` hold for every built key (zero false negatives). A non-member matches with probability `‚Čą 2**-bits_per_entry` (‚Čą 0.4 % at 8 bits, 0 observed at 16 bits over 10 000 queries). Fingerprints are the low `bits_per_entry` bits of a seeded BLAKE2b digest. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/xor_filter_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 100A: `pradyos/core/xor_filter.py` ‚ÄĒ `XorFilterError(detail)`; `XorFilter(bits_per_entry=8, seed=0)` with `build(keys)` (static; dedups; replaces any prior filter; `XorFilterError("peeling failed ‚ÄĒ retry with different seed")` on a rare stall), `contains(key)` (`XorFilterError("filter not built ‚ÄĒ call build() first")` before build), `reset(bits_per_entry=None, seed=None)`, `__contains__`, `__len__`, `bits_per_entry` / `seed` / `built` / `array_size` properties, and `stats()` (bits_per_entry / built / n / array_size / segment_size / `false_positive_rate = 2**-bits`). Invalid `bits_per_entry` (‚ąČ[1,64]) / `seed` raise `XorFilterError`.
- ‚úÖ 100B: `pradyos/web/xor_filter_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_xor_filter_routes(app, xor=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app filter, 8-bit, unbuilt) mounts 4 (all-static) routes ‚ÄĒ **no insert (the filter is static)**: `POST /api/v1/xorfilter/build` (body `{keys: [...]}`; 422 on missing / non-list / peeling failure), `GET /api/v1/xorfilter/contains` (`?key=`; **422 before build**), `GET /api/v1/xorfilter/stats`, `POST /api/v1/xorfilter/reset` (body `{bits_per_entry?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ‚úÖ 100C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase100.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `xor_filter` param, and a single `register_xor_filter_routes(app, xor_filter)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 100D: `tests/test_xor_filter.py` (39) + `tests/test_xor_filter_web.py` (20) ‚ÄĒ membership (10 000 keys all contained, zero false negatives); 8-bit FPR `< 1/128` & 16-bit FPR `0`/10 000 & wider-fingerprint-fewer-FPs; **static constraint** (contains before build / after reset raises); **rebuild replaces** (set A ‚Üí set B; A survives only at FP level); `build` dedups; determinism (same seed ‚Üí identical array) + different-seed-differs; **peeling robustness** (0 failures across 20 varied key sets at one seed); bits / seed validation + `XorFilterError`; stats / FPR formula / reset / reconfigure; integer & mixed key types; 10-thread concurrent membership; all 4 endpoints incl. build ‚Üí contains over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.
- ‚úÖ 100E: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 217 test modules registered (Phase 100 appends `test_xor_filter.py` + `test_xor_filter_web.py`).
- ‚úÖ 100F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 101 planned.

**Phase 101 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 219 test modules green. Sovereign Ribbon Filter (Dillinger‚ÄďWalzer, 2021) ‚ÄĒ the **retrieval-based** static membership filter that succeeds the XOR filter (P100) with better space efficiency: it frames membership as a **sparse linear system over GF(2)** and solves it down a narrow diagonal *ribbon* band rather than by peeling. Each key maps to a start column `s(k) ‚ąą [0, m-w]`, a `w`-bit coefficient row `c(k)` anchored at `s` (bit 0 forced to 1), and a `bits_per_entry`-bit fingerprint `f(k)`; its equation is `‚äē_{j: c(k)[j]=1} Z[s(k)+j] = f(k)` over a slot table `Z`. Rows are reduced into an incremental row-echelon form keyed by pivot column (each insert shifts to its leftmost set bit and, if that pivot is occupied, XORs against the resident row ‚ÄĒ the band never widens past `w`, so each insert is `O(w)`), then a back-substitution from the high column down fills `Z`. A query recomputes `s, c` and XORs the selected slots, so `‚äē Z[s+j] == f(k)` holds for every built key (**zero false negatives**); a non-member matches only by fingerprint collision (`‚Čą 2**-bits`, ‚Čą 0.4 % at 8 bits, 0 observed at 16 bits over 10 000 queries). With ribbon width `w = 64` and target load `0.85`, the table is `m = ‚Ćąn / 0.85‚ĆČ + w` slots ‚ÄĒ an overhead of **‚Čą 1.18√ó at scale, below the XOR filter's 1.23√ó theoretical bound and far below its 3.69√ó peeling construction**; wider `w` pushes the load toward the `n ¬∑ bits` limit. If a row reduces to zero coefficients with a non-zero residual the system is singular ‚ÄĒ `RibbonFilterError` asks for a different seed (astronomically rare at load 0.85). Fingerprint / start / coefficient are slices of a seeded BLAKE2b digest. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock` (the heavy solve runs lock-free on a snapshot, published with one locked assignment). Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/ribbon_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

Invalid `bits_per_entry` (‚ąČ[1,64]) / `seed` raise `RibbonFilterError`.
- ‚úÖ 101B: `pradyos/web/ribbon_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_ribbon_routes(app, ribbon=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app filter, 8-bit, unbuilt) mounts 4 (all-static) routes ‚ÄĒ **no insert (the filter is static)**: `POST /api/v1/ribbon/build` (body `{keys: [...]}`; 422 on missing / non-list / singular-system), `GET /api/v1/ribbon/contains` (`?key=`; **422 before build**), `GET /api/v1/ribbon/stats`, `POST /api/v1/ribbon/reset` (body `{bits_per_entry?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).

**Phase 102 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 221 test modules green. Sovereign HeavyKeeper (Gong et al., 2018) ‚ÄĒ a probabilistic **heavy-hitter / top-K frequency** sketch (pivot: the originally-eyed Count-Min Sketch was already shipped at P76 ‚ÄĒ `class CountMinSketch` ‚ÄĒ so Phase 102 stays in the frequency family but ships a genuinely-new algorithm). It keeps a `depth √ó width` grid of `(fingerprint, count)` cells (`count == 0` marks empty); for each occurrence of an item `x` (fingerprint `f = fp(x)`), every row hashes `x` to a cell and applies **exponential-decay-on-collision**: an empty cell is claimed `(f, 1)`, a matching fingerprint does `count += 1`, and a *mismatching* cell decays the resident only with probability `decay ** -count` ‚ÄĒ evicting and re-claiming it when the count hits 0. Because a genuine heavy hitter's count is large, `decay ** -count` is minuscule, so it is almost never decayed while cold items evaporate fast. The frequency estimate is the **max** matching counter across rows (not the *min*, as in Count-Min P76 ‚ÄĒ decay makes over-counting the failure mode to guard), and a bounded **indexed min-heap of size k** (`O(log k)` updates) tracks the live top-K, replacing its minimum only when exceeded. This decay rule is the distinctive mechanism ‚ÄĒ versus Count-Min's *min counters* (P76), Count Sketch's *signed estimate* (P94), Space-Saving's *evict-minimum* (P87), Misra-Gries' *decrement-all* (P99) and Lossy Counting's *window-sweep* (P95). Hashing is seeded BLAKE2b; the decay draws from a seeded `random.Random` so `seed` + stream is fully deterministic. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/heavykeeper_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 102A: `pradyos/core/heavykeeper.py` ‚ÄĒ `HeavyKeeperError(detail)`; `HeavyKeeper(k=10, width=1024, depth=4, decay=1.08, seed=0)` with `add(item, count=1)` (returns the updated estimate; reconciles the top-K heap), `query(item)` (max matching counter, 0 if absent), `top_k(n=None)` (`(item, estimate)` sorted by estimate desc; defaults to `k`), `reset(k=None, width=None, depth=None, decay=None, seed=None)` (clears buckets + heap; optional reconfigure), `__len__` (tracked count), `k`/`width`/`depth`/`decay`/`seed` properties, and `stats()` (k / width / depth / decay / seed / tracked / total). Invalid `k`/`width`/`depth` (‚ąČ ‚Ą§‚Āļ), `decay` (‚Č§ 1) or `seed` / non-positive `count` raise `HeavyKeeperError`.
- ‚úÖ 102B: `pradyos/web/heavykeeper_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_heavykeeper_routes(app, heavykeeper=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/heavykeeper/add` (body `{item, count?}`; 422 on missing item / bad count), `GET /api/v1/heavykeeper/topk` (`?n=` with `Query(ge=1)` ‚Üí auto-422; defaults to `k`), `GET /api/v1/heavykeeper/stats`, `POST /api/v1/heavykeeper/reset` (body `{k?, width?, depth?, decay?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ‚úÖ 102C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase102.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `heavykeeper` param, and a single `register_heavykeeper_routes(app, heavykeeper)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 102D: `tests/test_heavykeeper.py` (41) + `tests/test_heavykeeper_web.py` (20) ‚ÄĒ **heavy-hitter detection** (1 @ 1000 + 9 @ 100 in a 10 000 stream ‚Üí all 10 in `top_k(10)`); **frequency accuracy** (top item within 20 % of 1000); **eviction** (freq < 5 noise never in top-K); **decay sensitivity** (decay 1.02 forgets faster ‚Üí less surviving bucket mass & lower hot-item counts than 1.5); **estimate = max not min**; determinism (same seed + stream ‚Üí identical top-K, survives reset); top-K bounded by `k` / sorted desc / `n` param / keeps-largest; config + `count` validation + `HeavyKeeperError.detail`; stats / reset / reconfigure; integer & mixed items; 8-thread concurrent adds (heap ‚Č§ k, index map consistent, dominant hitter retained); all 4 endpoints over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 103 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 223 test modules green. Sovereign Spectral Bloom Filter (Cohen & Matias, 2003) ‚ÄĒ a **frequency-aware** Bloom filter that replaces the standard filter's single presence *bit* (P12) with an array of integer **counters**, estimating an item's multiplicity as the **minimum** counter across its `k` hash positions. That minimum is the natural estimator and the exact counterpoint to HeavyKeeper's *max* (P102): collisions can only push a counter higher, so the smallest of an item's counters is the tightest estimate and over-counting (never under-counting) is the only failure mode ‚ÄĒ zero false negatives, like any Bloom. Because the cells are counters, it also supports **deletion**: `remove` decrements an item's counters (guarded so a non-member, whose minimum is already 0, is never touched and counters never go negative) ‚ÄĒ the practical edge over a plain Bloom. Sizing uses the standard Bloom formulae from `capacity` and `error_rate`: `m = ‚Ćą-capacity¬∑ln(error_rate)/ln(2)¬≤‚ĆČ` counter slots and `k = round((m/capacity)¬∑ln2)` hashes, so membership FPR (`min > 0`) equals a standard Bloom's. The `k` positions come from one seeded BLAKE2b digest split into two 64-bit halves combined by Kirsch‚ÄďMitzenmacher double hashing (`h1 + i¬∑h2 mod m`), deterministic per `seed`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/spectralbloom_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 103A: `pradyos/core/spectral_bloom.py` ‚ÄĒ `SpectralBloomError(detail)`; `SpectralBloom(capacity=10000, error_rate=0.01, seed=0)` with `add(element, count=1)` (returns the updated multiplicity estimate), `query(element)` (min counter; 0 if absent), `remove(element, count=1)` (removes up to `count` occurrences only if present; returns the number removed; guards ‚Č• 0), `reset(capacity=None, error_rate=None, seed=None)` (clears; re-derives `m`/`k`), `__contains__` (min > 0), `__len__` (net occurrences), `capacity`/`error_rate`/`seed`/`num_bits`/`num_hashes` properties, and `stats()` (capacity / error_rate / num_bits / num_hashes / num_added / estimated_fill_ratio). Invalid `capacity` (‚ąČ ‚Ą§‚Āļ), `error_rate` (‚ąČ (0,1)) or `seed`, and non-positive `count`, raise `SpectralBloomError`.
- ‚úÖ 103B: `pradyos/web/spectralbloom_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_spectralbloom_routes(app, spectral=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app filter) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/spectralbloom/add` (body `{item, count?}`), `GET /api/v1/spectralbloom/query` (`?item=` ‚Üí auto-422 if absent), `DELETE /api/v1/spectralbloom/remove` (body `{item, count?}` ‚ÄĒ deletion), `GET /api/v1/spectralbloom/stats`, `POST /api/v1/spectralbloom/reset` (body `{capacity?, error_rate?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ‚úÖ 103C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase103.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `spectral_bloom` param, and a single `register_spectralbloom_routes(app, spectral_bloom)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 103D: `tests/test_spectral_bloom.py` (43) + `tests/test_spectralbloom_web.py` (21) ‚ÄĒ **zero false negatives** (1 000 members all query ‚Č• 1); **FPR ‚Č§ 2 √ó error_rate** (and near-0 under-loaded); **multiplicity exact at low load** (add √ó5 ‚Üí query 5; batch `add(x, 7)`); **estimate = min not max**; **deletion** (add 3 ‚Üí remove ‚Üí 2 ‚Üí remove to 0/not-member; remove non-member is a no-op that never corrupts shared counters; over-remove clamped); standard Bloom sizing (`m`/`k` formulae; smaller error_rate grows `m`); determinism (same seed ‚Üí identical positions, survives reset); config + `count` validation + `SpectralBloomError.detail`; stats / num_added / fill_ratio / reset / reconfigure; membership operator; integer & mixed items; 8-thread concurrent adds (no lost increments); all 5 endpoints incl. `DELETE`-with-body over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 104 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 225 test modules green. Sovereign Augmented Sketch / ASketch (Roy, Khan & Pomerantz, 2016) ‚ÄĒ a **two-stage frequency** estimator that bolts a small *exact* filter of the current heavy hitters onto a sketch base (pivot: the directive's eyed Cuckoo Filter is already shipped at P86 ‚ÄĒ `class CuckooFilter`, `/api/v1/cuckoo` ‚ÄĒ so Phase 104 ships a genuinely-new structure). **Stage 1** is a **Count Sketch** base (Charikar‚ÄďChen‚ÄďFarach-Colton 2002), *not* Count-Min (P76): each of `depth` rows maps an item to a bucket and an independent **sign** `s ‚ąą {+1,-1}`, `add` does `counter[d][j] += s¬∑delta`, and the estimate is the **median** of `s¬∑counter[d][j]` across rows ‚ÄĒ a *signed median*, so colliding items contribute `¬Ī` and cancel in expectation (an *unbiased* estimate), where Count-Min's min only ever over-counts. **Stage 2** is an exact-count dict of ‚Č§ `k` items: on `add`, a tracked item's count is bumped exactly, otherwise the sketch is updated and the item is **promoted** (evicting the dict minimum when full) once its sketch estimate exceeds the smallest tracked count; `query` returns the exact dict count when tracked, else the sketch median, and `top_k` reads exact counts straight off the dict. Hashing is seeded BLAKE2b (one digest per row ‚Üí bucket + sign bit). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/augmentedsketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 104A: `pradyos/core/augmented_sketch.py` ‚ÄĒ `AugmentedSketchError(detail)`; `AugmentedSketch(width=1024, depth=4, k=10, seed=0)` with `add(item, delta=1)` (returns updated estimate; promotes into the dict), `query(item)` (exact if tracked, else signed-median sketch estimate), `sketch_estimate(item)` (the Count Sketch base estimate alone), `top_k(n=None)` (`(item, exact_count)` desc; defaults to `k`), `reset(width=None, depth=None, k=None, seed=None)`, `__len__` (tracked count), `width`/`depth`/`k`/`seed` properties, and `stats()` (width / depth / k / seed / tracked / total). Invalid `width`/`depth`/`k` (‚ąČ ‚Ą§‚Āļ) or `seed`, and non-positive `delta`, raise `AugmentedSketchError`.
- ‚úÖ 104B: `pradyos/web/augmentedsketch_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_augmentedsketch_routes(app, augmented=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/augmentedsketch/add` (body `{item, delta?}`; 422 on missing item / bad delta), `GET /api/v1/augmentedsketch/query` (`?item=` ‚Üí auto-422 if absent), `GET /api/v1/augmentedsketch/topk` (`?n=` with `Query(ge=1)`; defaults to `k`), `GET /api/v1/augmentedsketch/stats`, `POST /api/v1/augmentedsketch/reset` (body `{width?, depth?, k?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ‚úÖ 104C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase104.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `augmented_sketch` param, and a single `register_augmentedsketch_routes(app, augmented_sketch)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 104D: `tests/test_augmented_sketch.py` (39) + `tests/test_augmentedsketch_web.py` (22) ‚ÄĒ **heavy-hitter detection** (1 @ 1000 + 4 @ 100 in a 10 000 stream ‚Üí all in `top_k`, counts within 50 of true since promoted); **sketch quality** (mid-frequency signed-median within ~30 %); **sign cancellation** (Count Sketch base estimate of an item stays ‚Čą its true count under heavy colliding noise ‚ÄĒ not inflated as Count-Min's min would be); **promotion** (a riser transitions from sketch estimate to exact dict count; a light item is not promoted past a full dict); top-K bounded by `k` / sorted desc / `n` param / keeps-largest; determinism (same seed + stream ‚Üí identical top-K and sketch array; survives reset); config + `delta` validation + `AugmentedSketchError.detail`; stats / reset / reconfigure; integer & mixed items; 8-thread concurrent adds (dict ‚Č§ k, dominant hitter retained); all 5 endpoints over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 105 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 227 test modules green. Sovereign Q-Digest (Shrivastava, Buragohain, Agrawal & Suri, 2004) ‚ÄĒ a **mergeable quantile sketch** for streaming percentile estimation (p50/p95/p99). It lays a *complete binary tree* over the value universe `[0, value_range)` (rounded up to a power-of-two capacity so the tree is complete), each node spanning `[lower, upper)`; only nodes with a positive count are stored (a `dict` keyed by heap-numbered node id), so the empty regions of a sparse universe cost nothing. `add` increments the value's leaf, then **compresses**: with `n` total elements and factor `k` the threshold is `‚Ćän/k‚Ćč`, and the tree is swept bottom-up merging any node/sibling/parent triple whose summed count falls below it up into the parent ‚ÄĒ enforcing the digest property and bounding the structure to `O(k¬∑log ŌÉ)` nodes (`ŌÉ = value_range`). `quantile(q)` walks stored nodes by increasing upper boundary, accumulating counts until the running sum reaches `q¬∑n`, and reports that node's max value; `rank(v)` sums counts of nodes lying entirely at/below `v`; `merge` adds node counts of two same-universe digests and recompresses (ideal for distributed aggregation). Fully deterministic (no randomness; the `seed` is carried for API parity and reported in stats). *(Pivot note: the directive's eyed **t-Digest is already shipped at Phase 79** ‚ÄĒ `class TDigest`, `/api/v1/tdigest` ‚ÄĒ and **DDSketch at Phase 96** ‚ÄĒ `/api/v1/ddsketch`; both quantile sketches collide, so Phase 105 ships a genuinely-new one, distinct from those plus Greenwald-Khanna (P91) and KLL (P92) ‚ÄĒ a tree/domain-decomposition approach.)* Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/qdigest_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 105A: `pradyos/core/q_digest.py` ‚ÄĒ `QDigestError(detail)`; `QDigest(compression_factor=100, value_range=65536, seed=0)` with `add(value, count=1)` (range-checked; recompresses), `quantile(q)` (`q` strictly in (0,1); `QDigestError` on empty / bad `q`), `rank(value)`, `merge(other)` (same-universe node-wise add + recompress; returns self; does not mutate `other`), `reset(compression_factor=None, value_range=None, seed=None)`, `__len__` (total count), `compression_factor`/`value_range`/`seed`/`num_nodes`/`total_count` properties, and `stats()` (compression_factor / value_range / total_count / num_nodes / theoretical_max_nodes = `k¬∑log ŌÉ`). Invalid config, out-of-range / non-int value, or non-positive count raise `QDigestError`.
- ‚úÖ 105B: `pradyos/web/qdigest_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_qdigest_routes(app, qdigest=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app digest) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/qdigest/add` (body `{value, count?}`; 422 on missing value / out-of-range / bad count), `GET /api/v1/qdigest/quantile` (`?q=` with `Query(gt=0.0, lt=1.0)`; **422 on empty digest**), `POST /api/v1/qdigest/merge` (body `{values: [...]}` ‚Üí builds a temp digest and merges it in), `GET /api/v1/qdigest/stats`, `POST /api/v1/qdigest/reset` (body `{compression_factor?, value_range?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ‚úÖ 105C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase105.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `qdigest` param, and a single `register_qdigest_routes(app, qdigest)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 105D: `tests/test_q_digest.py` (64) + `tests/test_qdigest_web.py` (24) ‚ÄĒ **uniform p50** (10 000 values over [0,1000) ‚Üí p50 ‚ąą [475,525]); **tail p99** within 5 % of 990; **merge correctness** (two 5 000-value halves ‚Üí merged p50 within 5 % of true); **compression bound** (`num_nodes ‚Č§ 4¬∑k¬∑log‚āā(value_range)`); **strict monotonicity** of `quantile(0.25..0.99)`; **determinism** (same seed + values + order ‚Üí identical tree and quantiles); low-count full-resolution (n < k ‚Üí no merging); rank monotonicity; skewed-distribution accuracy; config / value / count / `q` validation + `QDigestError.detail`; stats / reset / reconfigure; 8-thread concurrent adds; all 5 endpoints over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 106 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 229 test modules green. Sovereign Moment Sketch (Gan, Ding, Tai, Sheng, Bailis & Madden, 2018) ‚ÄĒ a **mergeable quantile sketch** that summarises a stream by its first `k` *power-sum moments* `C[i] = ő£ x‚ĀĪ` (`i = 0..k-1`) together with the observed `min` / `max`. Quantiles are reconstructed at query time by fitting a **maximum-entropy (MaxEnt)** distribution to the moments: among all densities on `[min, max]` whose moments match the observed ones, the maximum-entropy choice is `p(x) ‚ąĚ exp(ő£‚Īľ őĽ‚Īľ¬∑x ≤)`, with the values rescaled to the Chebyshev domain `[-1, 1]` for conditioning and the Lagrange multipliers `őĽ` solved by minimising the convex dual potential `log ‚ąę exp(ő£‚Īľ őĽ‚Īľ x ≤) dx ‚ąí ő£‚Īľ őĽ‚Īľ őľ‚Īľ` (gradient = fitted ‚ąí empirical moment) via `scipy.optimize.minimize` (L-BFGS-B). `quantile(q)` integrates the fitted density to a CDF and inverts it to find `v` with `CDF(v) = q`. Power sums are **trivially mergeable** ‚ÄĒ element-wise addition plus `min`/`max` of bounds ‚ÄĒ so distributed partitions combine in constant time. Fully deterministic (no randomness; `seed` carried for API parity). *(Collision note: the directive's originally-eyed **KLL Sketch is already shipped at Phase 92** ‚ÄĒ `class KLLSketch`, `pradyos/core/kll_sketch.py`, `/api/v1/kll` ‚ÄĒ so `kll_sketch` / `KLLSketch` read non-zero and were not reused; Phase 106 ships Moment Sketch instead.)* Depends on `numpy` / `scipy` (declared in `pyproject.toml`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/moment_sketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 106A: `pradyos/core/moment_sketch.py` ‚ÄĒ `MomentSketchError(detail)`; `MomentSketch(k=15, seed=0)` with `add(x)` (updates each power sum + min/max), `add_many(values)`, `quantile(q)` (`q` strictly in (0,1); MaxEnt fit; `MomentSketchError` on empty / bad `q`), `merge(other)` (same-`k` element-wise add + min/max; returns self; does not mutate `other`), `merge_state(dict)` / `from_state(dict)` (serialized-state round-trip), `reset(k=None, seed=None)`, `__len__` (= C[0]), `k`/`seed`/`total_count` properties, and `stats()` (k / seed / total_count / min_val / max_val / moments). Invalid `k`/`seed`, non-numeric value, or mismatched-`k` merge raise `MomentSketchError`.
- ‚úÖ 106B: `pradyos/web/moment_sketch_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_momentsketch_routes(app, sketch=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/momentsketch/add` (body `{value}`; 422 on missing / non-numeric value), `GET /api/v1/momentsketch/quantile` (`?q=` with `Query(gt=0.0, lt=1.0)`; **422 on empty sketch**), `POST /api/v1/momentsketch/merge` (body = a serialized `stats()` state with a `moments` list ‚Üí reconstructs and merges), `GET /api/v1/momentsketch/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/momentsketch/reset` (body `{k?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ‚úÖ 106C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase106.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `moment_sketch` param, and a single `register_momentsketch_routes(app, moment_sketch)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.

**Phase 107 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 231 test modules green. Sovereign Counting Bloom Filter ‚ÄĒ a Bloom variant whose single-bit array is replaced by an array of small integer **counters**, which buys the one thing a classic Bloom cannot do: **deletion**. `add` increments each of an element's `k` hashed counters; `remove` decrements them (guarded by a membership check first, so an absent element raises rather than under-decrementing and corrupting genuine members' counts); `contains` reports membership when *every* hashed counter is `‚Č• 1`. Standard Bloom sizing ‚ÄĒ `m = ‚Ćą-n¬∑ln(p)/(ln2)¬≤‚ĆČ` counters and `k = ‚Ćą(m/n)¬∑ln2‚ĆČ` hash functions for capacity `n` and target error_rate `p`. Counters are **4-bit-valued** (16 states `0..15`, one byte each in an `array.array('B')`) and `add` **saturates** at 15, so a hot element can never overflow and corrupt the structure (the bounded cost: exact deletion is lost only for an element added more than 15 times). Hashing is a **double-hashing** scheme `h_i(x) = (h1(x) + i¬∑h2(x)) mod m` for `i = 0..k-1`, where `h1`/`h2` are the two halves of one seeded BLAKE2b digest (the same stable, process-independent folding idiom as MinHash P88). Like any Bloom it admits **false positives** (bounded by `error_rate`) but ‚ÄĒ saturation aside ‚ÄĒ **no false negatives**. Pure stdlib (`array` + `hashlib`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/counting_bloom_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 107A: `pradyos/core/counting_bloom.py` ‚ÄĒ `CountingBloomError(detail)`; `CountingBloom(capacity=10000, error_rate=0.01, seed=0)` with `add(element)` (saturating increment), `contains(element)` / `__contains__`, `remove(element)` (decrement; raises `CountingBloomError("element not in filter")` if absent), `false_positive_rate()` (= `(1 - e^(-k¬∑n/m))^k`), `reset(capacity=None, error_rate=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `capacity`/`error_rate`/`seed`/`num_hash_functions`/`num_counters`/`count` properties (`count` = number of `add` calls, *not* unique elements ‚ÄĒ noted in the docstring), and `stats()` (capacity / error_rate / num_hash_functions / num_counters / count / false_positive_rate). Invalid `capacity` (‚ąČ ‚Ą§‚Āļ), `error_rate` (‚ąČ (0,1)) or `seed` raise `CountingBloomError`.
- ‚úÖ 107B: `pradyos/web/counting_bloom_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_countingbloom_routes(app, counting_bloom=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app filter) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/countingbloom/add` (body `{element}`; 422 on missing element), `GET /api/v1/countingbloom/contains` (`?element=`), `POST /api/v1/countingbloom/remove` (body `{element}`; **400 when the element is absent** ‚ÄĒ a state error, distinct from a 422 validation error), `GET /api/v1/countingbloom/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/countingbloom/reset` (body `{capacity?, error_rate?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ‚úÖ 107C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase107.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `counting_bloom` param, and a single `register_countingbloom_routes(app, counting_bloom)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 107D: `tests/test_counting_bloom.py` (51) + `tests/test_countingbloom_web.py` (20) ‚ÄĒ **FPR accuracy** (1 000 members, 10 000 non-member probes ‚Üí measured FPR ‚Č§ 0.02); **no false negatives** (all 1 000 members contained); **deletion** (add ‚Üí contains ‚Üí remove ‚Üí not contains); **double-add/single-remove** still present, **double-remove** gone; **no under-decrement corruption** (removing one element leaves 200 neighbours intact); **saturation** (add √ó20 ‚Üí counter capped at 15, no crash, still contained); **remove-of-absent raises** `CountingBloomError`; standard Bloom sizing (`m`/`k` formulae; tighter error_rate grows `m`); FPR formula + grows-with-load + zero-when-empty; determinism (same seed ‚Üí identical counter array; survives reset; insertion-order independent; different seed ‚Üí different array); config validation + `CountingBloomError.detail`; stats / reset / reconfigure; 8-thread concurrent adds; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. `DELETE`-with-body reset + the absent-remove **400** + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 108 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 233 test modules green. Sovereign Binary Fuse Filter (Graf & Lemire, 2022 ‚ÄĒ the segmented refinement of the fuse-graph construction, Dietzfelbinger & Walzer). Like the Phase 100 XOR filter it is a **static, space-optimal** approximate-membership filter built once from a complete key set; a query XORs three 8-bit fingerprint slots and compares against the key's own fingerprint, so there are **zero false negatives** and a false-positive rate of `‚Čą 2**-8 = 1/256 ‚Čą 0.39 %`. Hashing is a single seeded **xxhash-style** 64-bit integer mix ‚ÄĒ `mix(x, seed) = ((x ^ seed) ¬∑ 0x517cc1b727220a95) & MASK64` (pure Python, no external dependency) ‚ÄĒ sliced into three segment-local indices `h_i = (mix >> 21¬∑i) % segment` and a fingerprint `f = mix & 0xFF`; the three probed slots live in consecutive segments (`array[h0]`, `array[h1+seg]`, `array[h2+2¬∑seg]`). Construction **peels** the 3-XOR hypergraph (repeatedly removing a slot touched by exactly one unassigned key) then assigns fingerprints in reverse peel order so each key's equation holds; peeling is probabilistic, so a stall triggers an **internal seed retry** (the seed is advanced deterministically, so a fixed key set still yields a reproducible filter). The filter is **immutable after build** ‚ÄĒ there is no incremental `add`; `reset` returns it to the unbuilt state. Keys are sorted internally, so build order does not change the result. Pure stdlib (`hashlib` + integer mixing); thread-safe via a single `threading.RLock` (build and contains can race). Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/binary_fuse_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 108A: `pradyos/core/binary_fuse.py` ‚ÄĒ `BinaryFuseError(detail)`; `BinaryFuseFilter(seed=0)` with `build(keys)` (static; sorts + dedups; `BinaryFuseError("duplicate keys")` on dups, `BinaryFuseError("build failed: cycle detected")` if peeling never converges across the internal seed retries), `contains(key)` / `__contains__` (`BinaryFuseError("filter not built")` before build), `reset(seed=None)` (back to unbuilt), `__len__`, `seed`/`built`/`array_size` properties, and `stats()` (built / num_keys / array_size / bits_per_key = `8¬∑m/n` when built and non-empty else None / seed). Segments are sized at `‚Ćą1.23¬∑n/3‚ĆČ + 4` slots each (`m = 3¬∑segment`, ‚Čą 9.9 bits/key) ‚ÄĒ the regime where 3-segment peeling is reliable.
- ‚úÖ 108B: `pradyos/web/binary_fuse_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_binaryfuse_routes(app, binary_fuse=None)` (defaults to a fresh unbuilt filter) mounts 4 (all-static) routes ‚ÄĒ **no insert (the filter is static)**: `POST /api/v1/binaryfuse/build` (body `{keys: [...]}`; 422 on missing / non-list keys, **400** on duplicate / build cycle), `GET /api/v1/binaryfuse/contains` (`?key=`; **400 before build**), `GET /api/v1/binaryfuse/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/binaryfuse/reset` (body `{seed?}`; 422 on bad seed).
- ‚úÖ 108C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase108.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `binary_fuse` param, and a single `register_binaryfuse_routes(app, binary_fuse)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 108D: `tests/test_binary_fuse.py` (49) + `tests/test_binaryfuse_web.py` (20) ‚ÄĒ **no false negatives** (every built key contained, small and large key sets); **FPR** ‚Č§ 0.005 over 10 000 non-member probes (‚Čą 1/256 theory); **space efficiency** (`bits_per_key ‚Č§ 10`, `array_size ‚Čą 1.23¬∑n + 12`); **determinism** (same seed + keys ‚Üí identical array, survives retries) + **order-independence** (`build([a,b,c]) == build([c,a,b])`, incl. large reversed sets) + different-seed ‚Üí different array; **immutability** (no `add`; rebuild replaces); duplicate-keys / not-built / cycle ‚Üí `BinaryFuseError`; build across sizes `n = 1..3000`; reset ‚Üí unbuilt + contains raises + rebuildable; 8-thread concurrent `contains`; all 4 endpoints over HTTP incl. `DELETE`-with-body reset, the build-duplicate **400**, the contains-before-build **400**, + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 109 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 235 test modules green. Sovereign Vacuum Filter (Wang, Zhou, Yang, Du, Yang & Uhlig, 2019) ‚ÄĒ a space-efficient approximate-membership filter in the **cuckoo-fingerprint** family (cf. the Phase 86 cuckoo filter) supporting both **insertion** and **deletion** while using *less* space than the cuckoo filter at the same false-positive rate. The cuckoo filter recovers an item's alternate bucket by `i2 = i1 XOR H(fp)`, which is an involution over `[0, m)` **only when the bucket count `m` is rounded up to a power of two** ‚ÄĒ wasting on average ~1.5√ó (up to 2√ó) the space actually needed. The Vacuum Filter removes that constraint with an **Alternate Range** `L` (a power of two): both candidate buckets are confined to the same `L`-aligned *chunk* of `L` consecutive buckets via `i2 = i1 XOR (H(fp) mod L)`. Because `H(fp) mod L < L` flips only the low `log2(L)` bits, `i1` and `i2` always share the chunk `[‚Ćäi1/L‚Ćč¬∑L, ‚Ćäi1/L‚Ćč¬∑L + L)`; the bucket count then only has to be a **multiple of `L`** (`m = num_chunks ¬∑ L`) rather than a power of two, so it sits much closer to the true required size (measured **18‚Äď44 % smaller** than the cuckoo filter's next-power-of-two across n = 1.1k‚Äď100k). Each chunk is an independent power-of-two cuckoo sub-table, so intra-chunk partial-key kicking reaches high occupancy (**‚Čą 0.95 load** at first insert failure, measured) while the chunk count absorbs the rest at fine granularity. The XOR stays an involution because `‚Ćäi1/L‚Ćč¬∑L` is a multiple of `L` (low bits zero) and `m` is a multiple of `L` (so `chunk_base + L ‚Č§ m`), and the displacement depends only on the fingerprint ‚ÄĒ so a kicked fingerprint **never leaves its origin chunk** and the filter **never reports a false negative** (a failed insert is rolled back atomically), while `contains` may false-positive at `‚Čą 2¬∑bucket_size / 2^fingerprint_bits` exactly as the cuckoo filter does. The hash is injectable (`hash_fn`) for deterministic tests, with a `seed` salting the default stable BLAKE2b fold (process-independent). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock` (the public surface acquires it; internal helpers under the lock never re-acquire it). Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/vacuum_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 109A: `pradyos/core/vacuum_filter.py` ‚ÄĒ `VacuumFilterError(detail)`; `VacuumFilter(capacity, bucket_size=4, fingerprint_bits=8, max_kicks=500, alt_range=None, seed=0, hash_fn=None)` with `insert(item)` (partial-key cuckoo kicking confined to the item's chunk; atomic rollback ‚Üí returns `False` when the chunk is full), `contains(item)` / `__contains__`, `delete(item)` (removes one fingerprint; `False` if absent), `reset()`, `__len__`, and `capacity` (bucket count = `num_chunks¬∑alt_range`) / `alt_range` / `num_chunks` / `seed` properties, plus `stats()` (capacity / num_chunks / alt_range / count / load_factor / fingerprint_bits / max_kicks). `alt_range` defaults to an auto-chosen power of two (~8 large chunks) and is validated as a power of two (and clamped to fit `capacity`); invalid `capacity` / `bucket_size` / `fingerprint_bits` (>32) / `max_kicks` / `seed` / `alt_range` raise `VacuumFilterError` (bools rejected).
- ‚úÖ 109B: `pradyos/web/vacuum_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_vacuum_routes(app, vacuum_filter=None)` (defaults to a fresh `VacuumFilter` cap 1024) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/vacuum/insert` (body `{item}`; 422 on missing / non-dict body), `POST /api/v1/vacuum/contains` (body `{item}`; 422 on missing), `DELETE /api/v1/vacuum/delete` (body `{item}`; 422 on missing), `GET /api/v1/vacuum/stats`, `POST /api/v1/vacuum/reset`.
- ‚úÖ 109C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase109.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `vacuum_filter` param, and a single `register_vacuum_routes(app, vacuum_filter)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 109D: `tests/test_vacuum_filter.py` (61) + `tests/test_vacuum_web.py` (20) ‚ÄĒ **no false negatives** (every inserted key contained, small sets and high-occupancy fills); **involution + chunk confinement** (`alt(alt(i,fp),fp)==i`, `i1`/`i2` share the `L`-aligned chunk, both in `[0,m)` over thousands of keys); **space efficiency** (`m` a multiple of `alt_range`, `m == num_chunks¬∑alt_range`, `m ‚Č§ next_pow2(capacity)` at every size and strictly `<` for non-power-of-two chunk counts ‚ÄĒ `cap=3000 ‚Üí m=3072 < 4096`); **high occupancy** (‚Č• 0.90 load before first failure, zero false negatives); **FPR** (default hash, 8-bit fp, `b=4` ‚Üí measured ‚Č§ 0.05 over the ~3.1 % theory) + **wider fingerprint** (16-bit ‚Üí ‚Č§ 0.005); **deletion** (insert ‚Üí contains ‚Üí delete ‚Üí absent; reinsert; injected-collision false-positive clears on delete); **determinism** (injected hash and same-`seed` reproducible; different `seed` diverges placement); auto/explicit `alt_range` layout (`cap=3000 ‚Üí L=256, 12 chunks`; `cap=4096 ‚Üí L=512, 8 chunks`); full-chunk rollback (no corruption, count unchanged); config validation + `VacuumFilterError.detail`; stats / reset / reset-preserves-layout; 10-thread concurrent inserts + concurrent insert/delete; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. `DELETE`-with-body delete + deterministic FP-and-clear + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `binaryfuse`).
- ‚úÖ 109E: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 235 test modules registered (Phase 109 appends `test_vacuum_filter.py` + `test_vacuum_web.py`).

**Phase 110 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 237 test modules green. Sovereign Stable Bloom Filter (Deng & Rafiei, SIGMOD 2006) ‚ÄĒ a Bloom variant for **unbounded data streams**. A classic Bloom (Phase 72) or Counting Bloom (Phase 107) **saturates** on an endless stream: every cell eventually fills, the false-positive rate climbs to 1, and the filter is useless. The Stable Bloom Filter fixes this by **continuously forgetting** ‚ÄĒ it stores an array of small `d`-bit **cells** (each in `0..Max`, `Max = 2^d ‚ąí 1`) and on *every* insertion first **decrements `P` uniformly-random cells** (floored at 0) before **setting the element's `k` hashed cells to `Max`**. The decrement step evicts stale information at a constant rate, so the count of zero cells converges to a non-zero steady state regardless of stream length ‚ÄĒ the fill ratio (and hence the FP rate) **stabilises** instead of growing (measured: fill plateaus at **~0.58** across 5k‚Üí120k inserts, never saturating). `contains` reports membership when every one of an element's `k` cells is `‚Č• 1`; because a set cell can later be decremented to 0, the filter admits a small **bounded false-negative** rate for *old* elements (recent inserts recalled with ~1.0 probability; stale items measured ~0.87 forgotten after flooding) ‚ÄĒ the deliberate price for bounded memory on an infinite stream, and exactly what separates it from the no-false-negative Bloom family. `P` defaults to `num_hashes ¬∑ max_value` (the balance point where mass removed ‚Čą mass added), tunable for a tighter FP/FN trade (Deng & Rafiei derive the optimal `P` from a target stable FP). Cells are one byte each in an `array.array('B')` (`Max ‚Č§ 255`); hashing is double-hashing `h_i = (h1 + i¬∑h2) mod m` from one seeded BLAKE2b digest (the MinHash/Counting-Bloom idiom); the eviction draws from a `random.Random(seed)` so a fixed seed + insertion sequence reproduce the filter exactly. Pure stdlib (`array` + `hashlib` + `random`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/stable_bloom_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 110A: `pradyos/core/stable_bloom.py` ‚ÄĒ `StableBloomError(detail)`; `StableBloomFilter(num_cells=10000, num_hashes=5, max_value=3, decrement=None, seed=0)` with `add(element)` (evict `P` random cells then set `k` cells to `Max`), `contains(element)` / `__contains__`, `fill_ratio()` (fraction of non-zero cells), `reset(...)` (clear / reconfigure; re-seeds the eviction RNG), `__len__`, and `num_cells` / `num_hashes` / `max_value` / `decrement` (P) / `seed` / `count` properties, plus `stats()` (num_cells / num_hashes / max_value / decrement / count / fill_ratio / seed). `decrement` defaults to `min(num_hashes¬∑max_value, num_cells)`; invalid `num_cells` / `num_hashes` / `max_value` (‚ąČ 1..255) / `decrement` (‚ąČ 1..num_cells) / `seed` raise `StableBloomError` (bools rejected).
- ‚úÖ 110B: `pradyos/web/stable_bloom_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_stablebloom_routes(app, stable_bloom=None)` (defaults to a fresh `StableBloomFilter`) mounts 4 (all-static) routes ‚ÄĒ **no remove (the filter forgets on its own)**: `POST /api/v1/stablebloom/add` (body `{element}`; 422 on missing / non-dict), `GET /api/v1/stablebloom/contains` (`?element=`), `GET /api/v1/stablebloom/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/stablebloom/reset` (body `{num_cells?, num_hashes?, max_value?, decrement?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ‚úÖ 110C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase110.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `stable_bloom` param, and a single `register_stablebloom_routes(app, stable_bloom)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 110D: `tests/test_stable_bloom.py` (43) + `tests/test_stablebloom_web.py` (18) ‚ÄĒ **fresh add recalled**; **empty contains ‚Üí False**; **stability** (fill plateaus over a 40k stream, never `‚Č• 0.95`); **recent recall** (`‚Č• 0.95`); **forgetting** (stale victims evicted after flooding, FN_old `‚Č• 0.5`); **FP bounded** (`< 0.20` after warmup); **no saturation** under heavy stream; **larger `max_value` ‚áí higher recall**; **determinism** (same seed + sequence ‚Üí identical stats & membership; different seed diverges; reset re-seeds the RNG); default/explicit `decrement` (k¬∑Max, capped at num_cells); config validation + `StableBloomError.detail` (incl. `max_value > 255`, `decrement > num_cells`, bools); stats / properties / fill_ratio; reset clears + reconfigures; 10-thread concurrent adds + concurrent add/contains; all 4 endpoints over HTTP incl. `DELETE`-with-body reset + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `vacuum`).
- ‚úÖ 110E: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 237 test modules registered (Phase 110 appends `test_stable_bloom.py` + `test_stablebloom_web.py`).
- ‚úÖ 110F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 111 planned.

**Phase 111 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 239 test modules green. Sovereign Morris Counter (Morris, 1978 ‚ÄĒ *Counting large numbers of events in small registers*) ‚ÄĒ the original **approximate counting** algorithm. Counting to `n` exactly needs `‚Ćąlog‚āā n‚ĆČ` bits; the Morris counter stores only a small **exponent register** `c` and reaches an estimate of `n` in `‚Čą log‚āā log‚āā n` bits by incrementing `c` only *probabilistically*. For the generalised base `a > 1` (Flajolet 1985): on each event `c ‚Üź c + 1` with probability `a^(‚ąíc)`, and the estimate is `nŐā = (a^c ‚ąí 1)/(a ‚ąí 1)`. The estimate is **unbiased** ‚ÄĒ `E[nŐā] = n` for all `n` ‚ÄĒ which follows by induction (`E[a^c]` rises by exactly `a ‚ąí 1` per event, so `E[a^c] = 1 + n¬∑(a ‚ąí 1)`); the classic **base-2** case is the familiar `increment with prob 2^(‚ąíc)`, `nŐā = 2^c ‚ąí 1`. The base trades memory for accuracy (variance `‚Čą n¬∑(n ‚ąí 1)¬∑(a ‚ąí 1)/2`): a base near 1 is very accurate but the register grows almost like an exact counter, while a larger base keeps the register tiny at higher variance (measured: base-2 register `c = 16` for `n = 100 000`; mean estimate over 400 seeds within ~5 % of `n`; mean |rel error| 0.17 at base 1.1 vs 0.47 at base 2.0). This is a **new feature-class** ‚ÄĒ *approximate counting* ‚ÄĒ distinct from the cardinality sketches (HyperLogLog/P74, Theta/P93, which count *distinct* items) and the frequency sketches (Count-Min/P76, Count-Sketch/P94, per-key counts): the Morris counter estimates a single running **event total**. The compact state is the single integer `register`; an exact `increments` tally is kept only so `stats`/`relative_error` can report observed accuracy (a memory-constrained deployment would omit it). The probabilistic coin is a `random.Random(seed)`, so a fixed seed + increment sequence reproduce the counter exactly. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/morris_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 111A: `pradyos/core/morris_counter.py` ‚ÄĒ `MorrisCounterError(detail)`; `MorrisCounter(base=2.0, seed=0)` with `increment(times=1)` (each event bumps `c` with prob `base^(‚ąíc)`; returns the new register; `MorrisCounterError` on `times ‚ąČ ‚Ą§‚Āļ`), `estimate()` (`(base^c ‚ąí 1)/(base ‚ąí 1)`), `relative_error()` (`|estimate ‚ąí increments|/increments`, 0 when empty), `reset(base=None, seed=None)` (re-seeds the RNG), and `register` (c) / `increments` (exact n) / `base` / `seed` properties, plus `stats()` (register / estimate / increments / base / relative_error / seed). Invalid `base` (‚ąČ (1, ‚ąě)) or `seed` raise `MorrisCounterError` (bools rejected; `int` base coerced to `float`).

**Phase 112 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 241 test modules green. Sovereign Linear Counting (Whang, Vander-Zanden & Taylor, 1990 ‚ÄĒ *A linear-time probabilistic counting algorithm for database applications*) ‚ÄĒ a **cardinality** (distinct-count) estimator markedly more accurate than HyperLogLog at *small-to-moderate* cardinalities, for more space. The structure is one **bitmap** of `m` bits; each item is hashed to one position `h(x) mod m` and that bit is set, so duplicates collapse and the bitmap depends only on the *distinct* items. After the stream, the count is estimated from the **fraction of still-zero bits** `V = zero_bits/m`: `nŐā = ‚ąím¬∑ln(V)`. The derivation is the balls-in-bins empty-bin expectation ‚ÄĒ a bit is zero iff no distinct item hashed to it, so `E[zero_bits] = m¬∑(1 ‚ąí 1/m)^n ‚Čą m¬∑e^(‚ąín/m)`, giving `E[V] ‚Čą e^(‚ąín/m)` and `n ‚Čą ‚ąím¬∑ln(V)` (measured: sub-1 % relative error to load ~0.8; zero-bit count within 0.1 % of `m¬∑e^(‚ąín/m)`). Once **every** bit is set the bitmap is *saturated*, `V = 0`, and the estimate is undefined ‚ÄĒ `estimate()` raises `LinearCounterError`. This is a *different* cardinality algorithm from HyperLogLog (P74 ‚ÄĒ maximum leading-zero registers) and the Theta sketch (P93 ‚ÄĒ KMV / k-minimum-values): bitmap-and-empty-bins rather than order statistics, matching the one-algorithm-per-method pattern. Hashing is a single seeded BLAKE2b digest; a running set-bit count keeps `estimate` O(1). Pure stdlib (`hashlib`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/linear_counter_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 112A: `pradyos/core/linear_counter.py` ‚ÄĒ `LinearCounterError(detail)`; `LinearCounter(num_bits=65536, seed=0)` with `add(item)` (idempotent bit-set; distinct-count semantics), `add_many(items)` (`LinearCounterError` on a non-iterable), `estimate()` (`‚ąím¬∑ln(V)`; **raises when saturated**), `reset(num_bits=None, seed=None)`, `load_factor()`, `__len__` (bits set), and `num_bits` (m) / `bits_set` / `seed` / `saturated` properties, plus `stats()` (num_bits / bits_set / zero_bits / load_factor / estimate (None if saturated) / seed). Invalid `num_bits` (‚ąČ ‚Ą§‚Āļ) or `seed` raise `LinearCounterError` (bools rejected).
- ‚úÖ 112B: `pradyos/web/linear_counter_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_linearcounting_routes(app, linear_counter=None)` (defaults to a fresh `LinearCounter`) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/linearcounting/add` (body `{element}`; 422 on missing / non-dict), `GET /api/v1/linearcounting/estimate` (`{estimate, bits_set}`; **400 when saturated** ‚ÄĒ a state error), `GET /api/v1/linearcounting/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/linearcounting/reset` (body `{num_bits?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ‚úÖ 112C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase112.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `linear_counter` param, and a single `register_linearcounting_routes(app, linear_counter)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 112D: `tests/test_linear_counter.py` (35) + `tests/test_linearcounting_web.py` (17) ‚ÄĒ **accuracy** (rel error `< 0.03` at loads 0.07 / 0.26 / 0.53 / 0.76); **idempotent distinct-count** (1000√ó the same item ‚Üí estimate ‚Čą 1; 3000 distinct from 15 000 adds ‚Üí ‚Čą 3000); **zero-bit law** (measured zeros within 2 % of `m¬∑e^(‚ąín/m)`); **larger `m` lowers error**; **saturation** (`saturated` flag + `estimate()` raises + `stats.estimate is None`); **determinism** (same seed ‚Üí identical bitmap/estimate; different seed diverges the bitmap but the estimate stays within 5 %); config validation + `add_many` non-iterable + `LinearCounterError.detail`; properties / load_factor / stats; reset clears + reconfigures + re-add; 10-thread concurrent adds (estimate within 5 % of 5000 distinct); all 4 endpoints over HTTP incl. the saturated **400**, `DELETE`-with-body reset + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `morris`).
- ‚úÖ 112E: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 241 test modules registered (Phase 112 appends `test_linear_counter.py` + `test_linearcounting_web.py`).

**Phase 113 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 243 test modules green. Sovereign Treap (Seidel & Aragon, 1996 ‚ÄĒ *Randomized search trees*) ‚ÄĒ a **randomized balanced binary search tree**. Each node is simultaneously BST-ordered by `key` and max-heap-ordered by a **random priority**; the heap constraint forces a unique tree shape ‚ÄĒ the one a plain BST would take if keys were inserted in decreasing-priority order ‚ÄĒ and since the priorities are random, that order is a uniformly random permutation, so the tree behaves like a BST built from random insertions: **expected height `‚Čą 2¬∑ln n`** and `search` / `insert` / `delete` / `rank` / `select` all `O(log n)` *expected*, with no balance-factor or colour bookkeeping. `insert` does a BST insert then rotates the new node up while its priority exceeds its parent's; `delete` removes a node by **merging its two subtrees** (higher-priority child becomes the local root, recursively). Every node stores its **subtree size**, making the order-statistics `rank(key)` (keys strictly smaller) and `select(i)` (the `i`-th smallest key) run in `O(log n)`. Measured: height 32 for `n = 5000` random keys (`2¬∑ln n ‚Čą 17`), and ‚ÄĒ the key property ‚ÄĒ **sorted inserts stay balanced** (height 28, where a plain BST would be 5000) because random priorities defeat adversarial order. This is a *different* probabilistic ordered structure from the Skip List (P78, randomized tower levels over a linked list) ‚ÄĒ random priorities + rotations over a tree ‚ÄĒ matching the one-algorithm-per-method pattern. Priorities come from a seeded `random.Random` so a fixed seed + insertion sequence reproduce the tree exactly. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/treap_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 113A: `pradyos/core/treap.py` ‚ÄĒ `TreapError(detail)`; `Treap(seed=0)` with `insert(key, value=None)` (BST insert + rotate-up; updates value in place on a duplicate, no growth), `delete(key)` ‚Üí bool (subtree merge), `contains(key)` / `__contains__`, `search(key)` (raises if absent) / `get(key, default=None)`, `rank(key)`, `select(index)` (raises out of range), `min_key()` / `max_key()` (raise when empty), `keys()` (in-order, iterative), `height()`, `reset(seed=None)` (re-seeds priorities), `__len__`, and `seed` property, plus `stats()` (size / height / min / max / seed). Invalid `seed` raises `TreapError` (bools rejected); every node keeps a maintained `size`.
- ‚úÖ 113B: `pradyos/web/treap_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_treap_routes(app, treap=None)` (defaults to a fresh `Treap`) mounts 7 (all-static) routes with **numeric keys** (so the order statistics have a total order): `POST /api/v1/treap/insert` (body `{key, value?}`; 422 on missing / non-numeric key), `DELETE /api/v1/treap/delete` (body `{key}`; 422 on bad key), `GET /api/v1/treap/search` (`?key=`), `GET /api/v1/treap/rank` (`?key=`), `GET /api/v1/treap/select` (`?index=` `Query(ge=0)`; **400 when out of range** ‚ÄĒ a state error), `GET /api/v1/treap/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/treap/reset` (body `{seed?}`).

Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 113D: `tests/test_treap.py` (44) + `tests/test_treap_web.py` (25) ‚ÄĒ **BST + max-heap + subtree-size invariants** verified by walking the private tree after random inserts and after deletes; **balance** (random-insert height `< 5¬∑ln n`; sorted-insert height `< 5¬∑ln n` where a BST is `n`); **rank / select** vs a sorted reference (incl. gaps, min, beyond-max); **value mapping** (search / get / duplicate-update with no growth; string keys); **delete** (present/absent, len, re-insert, invariants preserved); **min/max/keys**; **determinism** (same seed ‚Üí identical shape; reset re-seeds); validation (`seed` non-int, bool) + `select` out-of-range / negative / non-int + `TreapError.detail`; stats; 10-thread concurrent inserts (BST + sizes intact); all 7 endpoints over HTTP incl. the `select` **400**, `DELETE`-with-body delete/reset + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `linearcounting`).
