**Phase 114 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 245 test modules green. Sovereign Bloomier Filter (Chazelle, Kilian, Rubinfeld & Tal, 2004 ‚ÄĒ *The Bloomier filter: an efficient data structure for static support lookup tables*) ‚ÄĒ the **associative** generalisation of a Bloom filter: instead of *is `x` in the set?* it answers *what value is associated with `x`?* for a **static** key‚Üívalue map. Construction is the same **XOR-peeling** the platform's XOR (P100) and Binary-Fuse (P108) filters use, generalised from storing a fingerprint to storing a *payload*: each key hashes (one seeded mix sliced into three segment-local indices) to three table cells, the cells are assigned by peeling the 3-XOR hypergraph and back-substituting in reverse peel order so that for every key `array[h0] ^ array[h1] ^ array[h2] == payload`, where `payload = (fingerprint << value_bits) | value_index`. A lookup XORs the three cells, splits out the fingerprint and value index, and ‚ÄĒ *only if the fingerprint matches the key's own* ‚ÄĒ returns `value_table[value_index]`. So **members are answered exactly** (measured: 0 wrong over 5000 keys) while a **non-member is reported not-found with probability `1 ‚ąí 2^(‚ąífingerprint_bits)`** (measured 0.0024 ‚Čą 2‚ĀĽ‚Āł; ~0 at 16 bits ‚ÄĒ a fingerprint collision is the only false-positive path). Values are stored verbatim in a positional value table (no hashing of values, so *unhashable* values like lists/dicts work); keys fold to a stable 64-bit BLAKE2b of `repr(key)`; peeling stalls trigger a deterministic seed retry. This is a **new capability** ‚ÄĒ value *retrieval*, not just membership (Bloom/P72, Counting/P107) or counts ‚ÄĒ and a different construction target from the membership-only XOR/Fuse filters. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.RLock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/bloomier_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 114A: `pradyos/core/bloomier.py` ‚ÄĒ `BloomierError(detail)`; `BloomierFilter(fingerprint_bits=8, seed=0)` with `build(mapping)` (static; sorts by folded key, `value_bits = (n‚ąí1).bit_length()`, `BloomierError` on a key hash-collision or peeling cycle after the seed retries), `get(key, default=None)` (exact for members; `default` otherwise; raises before build), `contains(key)` / `__contains__`, `reset(seed=None)` (back to unbuilt), `__len__`, and `seed` / `built` / `fingerprint_bits` / `num_cells` properties, plus `stats()` (built / num_keys / num_cells / fingerprint_bits / value_bits / bits_per_key / seed). Invalid `fingerprint_bits` (‚ąČ 1..32) / `seed` raise `BloomierError` (bools rejected); segments sized at `‚Ćą1.23¬∑n/3‚ĆČ + 4` like the Binary-Fuse filter.
- ‚úÖ 114B: `pradyos/web/bloomier_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_bloomier_routes(app, bloomier=None)` (defaults to a fresh unbuilt filter) mounts 4 (all-static) routes ‚ÄĒ **no insert (the map is static)**: `POST /api/v1/bloomier/build` (body `{mapping: {...}}`; 422 on missing / non-object mapping, **400** on cycle / duplicate), `GET /api/v1/bloomier/get` (`?key=`; `{key, found, value}`; **400 before build**), `GET /api/v1/bloomier/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/bloomier/reset` (body `{seed?}`; 422 on bad seed).
- ‚úÖ 114C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase114.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `bloomier` param, and a single `register_bloomier_routes(app, bloomier)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 114D: `tests/test_bloomier.py` (38) + `tests/test_bloomier_web.py` (20) ‚ÄĒ **exact value for every member** (small & 3000-key); **non-member FP** ‚Č§ 0.02 over 10 000 probes (‚Čą 2‚ĀĽ‚Āł) + **wider fingerprint** (16-bit ‚Č§ 0.001); **arbitrary / unhashable values** (lists, dicts, None, floats) verbatim; **numeric keys**; **determinism** (same seed ‚Üí identical array & value table) + **order-independence** (shuffled dict ‚Üí identical array); **immutability** (rebuild replaces); **build across sizes** `n = 1..300` (incl. the `n=1`, `value_bits=0` edge); **empty build**; `contains` (members True, non-members ‚Čą FP); not-built / reset (`get`/`contains` raise before build; reset ‚Üí unbuilt + rebuildable); config validation (`fingerprint_bits ‚ąą {0,64,8.5,bool}`, bad seed, non-mapping, **duplicate keys via a fake `.items()`**) + `BloomierError.detail`; properties / stats (built & unbuilt, `value_bits == (n‚ąí1).bit_length()`); 10-thread concurrent `get` (all values exact); all 4 endpoints over HTTP incl. the build/`get` **400**s, `DELETE`-with-body reset + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `treap`).
- ‚úÖ 114E: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 245 test modules registered (Phase 114 appends `test_bloomier.py` + `test_bloomier_web.py`).

**Phase 115 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 247 test modules green. Sovereign MinHash LSH (Indyk & Motwani 1998; Broder 1997 ‚ÄĒ *locality-sensitive hashing* over MinHash signatures) ‚ÄĒ a **similarity-search index** for fast approximate near-duplicate / nearest-neighbour retrieval over sets. The platform already *estimates* set similarity (MinHash/P88, SimHash/P89); LSH turns that into an **index**. Each item's token set is reduced to a `k = bands¬∑rows` MinHash signature via universal hashing `h_i(t) = (a_i¬∑base(t) + b_i) mod (2‚Ā∂¬Ļ‚ąí1)`, `signature[i] = min_t h_i(t)` (two sets agree on a position with probability equal to their Jaccard similarity `s`). The signature is split into `bands` bands of `rows` rows; an item is bucketed per band by that band's whole `rows`-tuple, so two items collide in a band iff their signatures agree on every row of it (`s^rows`) and share **at least one** band with probability `1 ‚ąí (1 ‚ąí s^rows)^bands` ‚ÄĒ the classic LSH **S-curve** with threshold `‚Čą (1/bands)^(1/rows)`. `query(set)` gathers the candidates sharing any band bucket and refines them by the signature-agreement estimate, returning those at/above a similarity threshold (sorted by descending similarity). Measured: self-query similarity 1.0, Jaccard estimates within ~0.05‚Äď0.1 of truth, **recall 1.0** on ~0.8-Jaccard near-duplicates over 200 docs, disjoint sets excluded. This is a *new capability* ‚ÄĒ similarity **search / indexing**, not just pairwise estimation. Fully deterministic given the seed (universal-hash coefficients seeded; results sorted by similarity then stringified id, so output never depends on set iteration order). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/minhash_lsh_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 115A: `pradyos/core/minhash_lsh.py` ‚ÄĒ `MinHashLSHError(detail)`; `MinHashLSH(bands=16, rows=4, seed=0)` with `insert(item_id, tokens)` (re-insert replaces), `query(tokens, threshold=0.0)` ‚Üí `[(id, similarity), ...]` desc, `similarity(a, b)` (signature-agreement Jaccard estimate), `remove(item_id)` ‚Üí bool, `contains(item_id)` / `__contains__`, `reset(bands=None, rows=None, seed=None)`, `threshold_estimate()` (`(1/bands)^(1/rows)`), `__len__`, and `bands` / `rows` / `num_perm` (k) / `seed` properties, plus `stats()` (num_items / bands / rows / num_perm / threshold_estimate / seed). Invalid `bands` / `rows` (‚ąČ ‚Ą§‚Āļ) / `seed` / `threshold` (‚ąČ [0,1]) raise `MinHashLSHError` (bools rejected).
- ‚úÖ 115B: `pradyos/web/minhash_lsh_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_minhashlsh_routes(app, minhash_lsh=None)` (defaults to a fresh index) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/minhashlsh/insert` (body `{id, tokens[]}`; 422 on missing id / non-list tokens), `POST /api/v1/minhashlsh/query` (body `{tokens[], threshold?}`; 422 on non-list tokens / bad threshold), `DELETE /api/v1/minhashlsh/remove` (body `{id}`), `GET /api/v1/minhashlsh/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/minhashlsh/reset` (body `{bands?, rows?, seed?}`).
- ‚úÖ 115C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase115.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `minhash_lsh` param, and a single `register_minhashlsh_routes(app, minhash_lsh)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 115D: `tests/test_minhash_lsh.py` (35) + `tests/test_minhashlsh_web.py` (21) ‚ÄĒ **self-query** finds self at sim‚Čą1; **similarity estimate** within 0.1 of true Jaccard (identical‚Üí1, disjoint‚Üí~0); **retrieval** (near-duplicate found, disjoint excluded, threshold filters by estimate, **recall ‚Č• 0.9** over 200 near-dups, results sorted desc, multiple overlapping windows all retrieved); **determinism** (same seed ‚Üí identical query results & signatures); **remove / re-insert** (replaces signature, removed not in query); empty token set + string tokens; validation (`bands`/`rows`/`seed`/`threshold ‚ąČ [0,1]`, bools) + `MinHashLSHError.detail`; properties / `threshold_estimate` / stats; reset clears + reconfigures; 10-thread concurrent inserts; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. `DELETE`-with-body remove/reset + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `bloomier`).

**Phase 116 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 249 test modules green. Sovereign TinyLFU (Einziger, Friedman & Manes, 2017 ‚ÄĒ *TinyLFU: a highly efficient cache admission policy*) ‚ÄĒ a **frequency sketch with aging**, the recency-aware estimator behind modern cache-admission policies (e.g. Caffeine's W-TinyLFU). A plain Count-Min (P76) never forgets, so on a long stream every counter saturates and current popularity is indistinguishable from stale popularity. TinyLFU adds the two ingredients a cache needs: a **doorkeeper** ‚ÄĒ a small Bloom filter that absorbs *one-hit wonders* (a key's first access only sets a doorkeeper bit; the larger Count-Min array is touched only from the second access on, and the estimate adds the bit back: `estimate(x) = countmin(x) + (1 if x in doorkeeper)`); and a **reset / aging** rule ‚ÄĒ a running access counter bumps on every access, and once it reaches the sample size `W` the sketch *ages*: every counter is **halved** (`c >>= 1`) and the doorkeeper cleared, so the estimate tracks a *sliding* frequency that decays. The headline op `admit(candidate, victim)` ‚Üí `estimate(candidate) > estimate(victim)` is the frequency-based eviction decision. Measured: exact frequency below the one-byte saturation (caps at 256), one-sided error (`estimate ‚Č• true`), singletons leave the Count-Min untouched, and a heavy key's estimate **decays 60 ‚Üí 3** after the sketch is aged by flooding. This is a *new feature-class* ‚ÄĒ **windowed / aging frequency for admission** ‚ÄĒ distinct from the platform's plain frequency sketches (Count-Min/P76, Count-Sketch/P94) and heavy-hitter trackers (Space-Saving/P87, Misra-Gries/P99, HeavyKeeper/P102), none of which age. Counters are one byte each (saturating) in a flat `bytearray`; hashing is double-hashing from one seeded BLAKE2b digest. Fully deterministic given the seed. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/tiny_lfu_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 116A: `pradyos/core/tiny_lfu.py` ‚ÄĒ `TinyLFUError(detail)`; `TinyLFU(sample_size=1000, width=None, depth=4, seed=0)` (`width` defaults to `sample_size`) with `add(key)` (doorkeeper on first sight, Count-Min after; ages at `sample_size`), `estimate(key)` (Count-Min min + doorkeeper bit), `admit(candidate, victim)` ‚Üí bool, `reset(sample_size=None, width=None, depth=None, seed=None)`, and `sample_size` / `width` / `depth` / `seed` / `total` / `resets` properties, plus `stats()` (sample_size / width / depth / doorkeeper_bits / total / accesses_since_reset / resets / seed). The doorkeeper is a Bloom sized for ~1 % FP at the sample size. Invalid `sample_size` / `width` / `depth` (‚ąČ ‚Ą§‚Āļ) / `seed` raise `TinyLFUError` (bools rejected).

**Phase 117 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 251 test modules green. Sovereign HyperMinHash (Yu & Weber, 2017 ‚ÄĒ *MinHash in LogLog space*) ‚ÄĒ a single compact sketch that estimates **both cardinality and Jaccard similarity** (hence union/intersection sizes), where the platform otherwise keeps those separate (HyperLogLog/P74 & Theta/P93 for cardinality; MinHash/P88 for similarity). Each element hashes to 64 bits: the top `p` bits choose one of `m = 2^p` **buckets**, and the remaining `w = 64 ‚ąí p` bits give a HyperLogLog **rank** (`leading_zeros + 1`) and an `r`-bit **mantissa** (their low `r` bits). Since the smallest remaining hash has the most leading zeros, "keep the bucket minimum" and "keep the max HLL rank" coincide; each bucket stores the `(rank, mantissa)` of its extremal element (max rank, ties by min mantissa ‚ÄĒ order-independent and **mergeable** by bucketwise max-rank/min-mantissa). **Cardinality** uses the ranks via the standard HyperLogLog estimator `őĪ_m¬∑m¬≤/ő£2^(‚ąírank)` with the small-range linear-counting correction (measured **within ~2‚Äď4 %** of true across 1k‚Äď50k). **Jaccard** counts buckets agreeing on both rank and mantissa; the raw agreement `J + (1‚ąíJ)¬∑C` is corrected by the expected random-collision rate `C = (ő£_k P_A(k)¬∑P_B(k))¬∑2^(‚ąír)` from the two rank distributions, giving `ńī = (agree ‚ąí C)/(1 ‚ąí C)` (measured **within ~0.06 absolute** across overlap levels ‚ÄĒ the residual is a known bias of the compact `(rank, mantissa)` representation; union within ~6 %, intersection within ~20 % as the product compounds). Mergeable, so distributed partitions combine bucketwise. This is a *new capability* ‚ÄĒ a **joint cardinality + similarity** sketch. Fully deterministic given the seed. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/hyper_minhash_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 117A: `pradyos/core/hyper_minhash.py` ‚ÄĒ `HyperMinHashError(detail)`; `HyperMinHash(p=8, r=8, seed=0)` (`m = 2^p`; `r`-bit mantissa) with `add(element)` / `add_many(iter)`, `cardinality()` (HLL + linear-counting), `jaccard(other)` (collision-corrected), `merge(other)` ‚Üí union sketch, `union_cardinality(other)`, `intersection_cardinality(other)` (Jaccard √ó union), `reset(p=None, r=None, seed=None)`, and `p` / `r` / `num_buckets` / `seed` properties, plus `stats()` (p / r / num_buckets / filled / cardinality / seed). Ranks + mantissas are one byte each (`bytearray`). Invalid `p` (‚ąČ 4..20) / `r` (‚ąČ 1..8) / `seed`, or an incompatible (`p`/`r`/`seed`-mismatched) `other`, raise `HyperMinHashError` (bools rejected).
- ‚úÖ 117B: `pradyos/web/hyper_minhash_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_hyperminhash_routes(app, hyper_minhash=None)` (defaults to a fresh sketch) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/hyperminhash/add` (body `{element}`; 422 on missing), `GET /api/v1/hyperminhash/cardinality`, `POST /api/v1/hyperminhash/compare` (body `{tokens[]}`; builds a compatible temp sketch ‚Üí `{jaccard, union, intersection}`; 422 on non-list tokens), `GET /api/v1/hyperminhash/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/hyperminhash/reset` (body `{p?, r?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ‚úÖ 117C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase117.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `hyper_minhash` param, and a single `register_hyperminhash_routes(app, hyper_minhash)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 117D: `tests/test_hyper_minhash.py` (33) + `tests/test_hyperminhash_web.py` (18) ‚ÄĒ **cardinality** (within 5 % at 1k/10k; ignores duplicates; `add_many`); **Jaccard** (self = 1, disjoint ‚Čą 0, within 0.10 across overlaps, symmetric); **union** (within 6 %) / **intersection** (within 20 %); **merge** (bucketwise = the directly-built union sketch); **determinism** (same seed ‚Üí identical ranks/mantissas/cardinality; different seed diverges); **compatibility** (mismatched `p`/`seed` or non-sketch `other` raise) + config validation (`p ‚ąą {3,21}`, `r ‚ąą {0,9}`, bools) + `add_many` non-iterable + `HyperMinHashError.detail`; properties / stats; reset clears + reconfigures; 10-thread concurrent adds; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. `compare` (self/partial/disjoint) + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `tinylfu`).
- ‚úÖ 117E: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 251 test modules registered (Phase 117 appends `test_hyper_minhash.py` + `test_hyperminhash_web.py`).

**Phase 118 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 253 test modules green. Sovereign Scalable Bloom Filter (Almeida, Baquero, Pregui√ßa & Hutchison, 2007 ‚ÄĒ *Scalable Bloom Filters*) ‚ÄĒ a Bloom variant for **sets of unknown, growing size** that keeps a *bounded* overall false-positive rate without knowing the capacity up front. It maintains a **list of ordinary Bloom layers**; when the active layer fills to its capacity it is frozen and a **new layer** is appended ‚ÄĒ **larger** (capacity √ó`growth`) and with a **tighter** target error (√ó`ratio`, `ratio < 1`). Because the per-layer error rates `P_i = P_target¬∑(1 ‚ąí ratio)¬∑ratio^i` form a geometric series, their sum telescopes to `P_target`, so the compounded false-positive probability stays bounded for **any** number of elements (measured **0.0024 ‚Č§ 0.01** after growth to 4 layers, and **0.0081 ‚Č§ 0.02** at 40√ó the initial capacity). `contains` is a logical OR across layers (still **no false negatives**). This is the **dynamically-growing, capacity-free** membership filter ‚ÄĒ distinct from the platform's fixed-capacity Bloom (P72), deletion-supporting Counting Bloom (P107) and forgetting Stable Bloom (P110). Each layer is sized by the standard Bloom formulae; bits live in a `bytearray` and hashing is double-hashing from a seeded BLAKE2b digest salted by the layer index. Fully deterministic given the seed. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/scalable_bloom_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 118A: `pradyos/core/scalable_bloom.py` ‚ÄĒ `ScalableBloomError(detail)`; `ScalableBloomFilter(initial_capacity=1000, error_rate=0.01, ratio=0.9, growth=2, seed=0)` with `add(element)` ‚Üí bool (False if already present; appends a tighter/larger layer when the active one is full), `contains(element)` / `__contains__`, `false_positive_rate()` (compounded `1 ‚ąí ő†(1 ‚ąí P_i)`), `reset(...)`, `__len__`, and `initial_capacity` / `error_rate` / `ratio` / `growth` / `seed` / `num_layers` / `count` properties, plus `stats()` (count / num_layers / initial_capacity / error_rate / ratio / growth / total_bits / false_positive_rate / seed). Invalid `initial_capacity` (‚ąČ ‚Ą§‚Āļ) / `error_rate` (‚ąČ (0,1)) / `ratio` (‚ąČ (0,1)) / `growth` (< 2) / `seed` raise `ScalableBloomError` (bools rejected).
- ‚úÖ 118B: `pradyos/web/scalable_bloom_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_scalablebloom_routes(app, scalable_bloom=None)` (defaults to a fresh filter) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/scalablebloom/add` (body `{element}`; 422 on missing; `{added, count}`), `GET /api/v1/scalablebloom/contains` (`?element=`), `GET /api/v1/scalablebloom/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/scalablebloom/reset` (body `{initial_capacity?, error_rate?, ratio?, growth?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ‚úÖ 118C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase118.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `scalable_bloom` param, and a single `register_scalablebloom_routes(app, scalable_bloom)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 118D: `tests/test_scalable_bloom.py` (31) + `tests/test_scalablebloom_web.py` (18) ‚ÄĒ **growth** (‚Č• 3 layers past initial capacity; `total_bits` grows; low load stays at 1 layer); **no false negatives** after growth; **bounded FP** (‚Č§ 0.015 near a 0.01 target after growth; ‚Č§ 0.03 at 40√ó capacity; design bound ‚Č§ target; tighter ratio still bounded); duplicate `add` ‚Üí False + distinct `count`; **determinism** (same seed ‚Üí identical layers & bits; different seed diverges); config validation (`initial_capacity`/`error_rate`/`ratio`/`growth`/`seed`, bools) + `ScalableBloomError.detail`; properties / stats; reset clears + reconfigures; 10-thread concurrent adds; all 4 endpoints over HTTP incl. growth-over-HTTP + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `hyperminhash`).

**Phase 119 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 255 test modules green. Sovereign Rendezvous Hashing / HRW (Thaler & Ravishankar, 1998 ‚ÄĒ *highest random weight hashing*) ‚ÄĒ a distributed key‚Üínode assignment scheme that, like the platform's Hash Ring (P73, consistent hashing), spreads keys uniformly and **minimises reassignment** when the node set changes, but by an entirely different mechanism: each key `k` is assigned to the node `n` **maximising a score** derived from `hash(k, n)`. No ring, no virtual nodes ‚ÄĒ just `O(N)` score evaluations per lookup. Two properties fall out for free and were verified empirically: **uniform load** (each of `N` nodes wins ‚Čą `1/N` of keys ‚ÄĒ measured 955‚Äď1047 per node over 8000 keys / 8 nodes), and **minimal disruption** ‚ÄĒ removing a node reassigns *only its own* keys (every other key provably unchanged) and adding a node pulls *only* the keys it newly wins (‚Čą `1/(N+1)`, measured 0.116 ‚Čą 1/9) to it, disturbing nothing else. Weighted nodes use `score = ‚ąíweight/ln(h)` (a 3√ó node wins ‚Čą 3√ó keys ‚ÄĒ measured 2.98√ó); `get_replicas(key, k)` returns the `k` highest-scoring nodes for replica placement (first replica = `assign`). A different algorithm in the same distributed-hashing class as the Hash Ring ‚ÄĒ HRW scores vs ring positions. Deterministic given the seed. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/rendezvous_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 119A: `pradyos/core/rendezvous_hash.py` ‚ÄĒ `RendezvousError(detail)`; `RendezvousHash(nodes=None, seed=0)` with `add_node(node, weight=1.0)` (also re-weights), `remove_node(node)` ‚Üí bool, `contains` / `__contains__`, `assign(key)` (argmax score; `RendezvousError` if no nodes), `get_replicas(key, k)` (top-`k` nodes; `RendezvousError` on `k < 1` or no nodes), `weight_of(node)`, `reset(seed=None)`, `__len__`, and `seed` / `nodes` properties, plus `stats()` (num_nodes / nodes / total_weight / seed). The score `‚ąíweight/ln(h)` uses `h ‚ąą (0,1)` from a seeded BLAKE2b of `(seed, key, node)`; ties broken by stringified node id. Invalid `seed` or non-positive `weight` or non-iterable `nodes` raise `RendezvousError` (bools rejected).
- ‚úÖ 119B: `pradyos/web/rendezvous_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_rendezvous_routes(app, rendezvous=None)` (defaults to a fresh ring) mounts 6 (all-static) route-method combos: `POST /api/v1/rendezvous/nodes` (body `{node, weight?}`; 422 on missing / bad weight), `DELETE /api/v1/rendezvous/nodes` (body `{node}`), `GET /api/v1/rendezvous/assign` (`?key=`; **400 if no nodes**), `GET /api/v1/rendezvous/replicas` (`?key=&k=` `Query(ge=1)`; **400 if no nodes**), `GET /api/v1/rendezvous/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/rendezvous/reset` (body `{seed?}`).
- ‚úÖ 119C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase119.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `rendezvous` param, and a single `register_rendezvous_routes(app, rendezvous)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 119D: `tests/test_rendezvous_hash.py` (36) + `tests/test_rendezvous_web.py` (21) ‚ÄĒ **deterministic** assignment (member node, stable, insertion-order independent, different seed diverges); **uniform load** (within 15 %); **minimal disruption** (remove moves exactly the removed node's keys & nothing else; add moves keys only to the new node, ‚Čą 1/(N+1)); **weighted load** (3√ó node ‚Čą 3√ó keys; re-weight); **replicas** (distinct, first = assign, capped at node count, `k < 1` raises, empty raises); node management (add / remove present-absent / contains / numeric ids); validation (`seed`/`weight`/non-iterable nodes, bools) + `weight_of` absent + `RendezvousError.detail`; properties (`nodes` sorted) / stats; reset; concurrent assigns + mutations; all 6 endpoints over HTTP incl. assign/replicas **400** with no nodes + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `scalablebloom`).
- ‚úÖ 119E: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 255 test modules registered (Phase 119 appends `test_rendezvous_hash.py` + `test_rendezvous_web.py`).

**Phase 120 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 257 test modules green. Sovereign Maglev Hashing (Eisenbud, Cilingiroglu et al., 2016 ‚ÄĒ *Maglev: A Fast and Reliable Software Network Load Balancer*) ‚ÄĒ Google's **consistent hashing** scheme and the **third** distributed key‚Üínode assignment algorithm, alongside the Hash Ring (P73, ring) and Rendezvous/HRW (P119, per-key argmax). Maglev precomputes a fixed-size **lookup table** of `M` entries (`M` prime, `M ‚Čę N`): each node proposes a pseudo-random **permutation** of the slots (`offset = h1(node) mod M`, `skip = h2(node) mod (M‚ąí1) + 1`, so `permutation[j] = (offset + j¬∑skip) mod M` visits every slot since `M` is prime), and the nodes take turns claiming their next-preferred still-empty slot until the table is full. A lookup is then an `O(1)` index `table[hash(key) mod M]`. This yields **near-perfect even load** (measured `load_ratio = 1.01`, max/min slots ‚ÄĒ far tighter than ring hashing) and **small disruption** on membership change (measured ~0.12 of keys move when 1 of 10 nodes is removed, with no key mapping to the removed node), with the fastest lookups of the three. A *different* mechanism again ‚ÄĒ permutation-filled lookup table vs ring positions vs per-key argmax. The requested `table_size` is bumped to the next prime; the table is rebuilt on node changes; hashes are seeded BLAKE2b so it is deterministic. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/maglev_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 120A: `pradyos/core/maglev.py` ‚ÄĒ `MaglevError(detail)`; `MaglevHash(nodes=None, table_size=65537, seed=0)` (table size rounded up to a prime via `_next_prime`) with `add_node(node)` / `remove_node(node)` ‚Üí bool (rebuild the table), `lookup(key)` / `assign(key)` (`MaglevError` if no nodes), `contains` / `__contains__`, `reset(table_size=None, seed=None)`, `load_distribution()`, `__len__`, and `table_size` / `seed` / `nodes` properties, plus `stats()` (num_nodes / table_size / nodes / min_load / max_load / load_ratio / seed). Invalid `table_size` (< 2) / `seed`, non-iterable `nodes`, or more nodes than table slots raise `MaglevError` (bools rejected); duplicate nodes deduped.
- ‚úÖ 120B: `pradyos/web/maglev_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_maglev_routes(app, maglev=None)` (defaults to a fresh table) mounts 5 (all-static) route-method combos: `POST /api/v1/maglev/nodes` (body `{node}`; 422 on missing, **400** on table overflow), `DELETE /api/v1/maglev/nodes` (body `{node}`), `GET /api/v1/maglev/lookup` (`?key=`; **400 if no nodes**), `GET /api/v1/maglev/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/maglev/reset` (body `{table_size?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ‚úÖ 120C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase120.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `maglev` param, and a single `register_maglev_routes(app, maglev)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 120D: `tests/test_maglev.py` (37) + `tests/test_maglev_web.py` (19) ‚ÄĒ prime helpers (`_is_prime` / `_next_prime`); table-size bumped to prime; **deterministic** lookup (member, stable, order-independent, different seed diverges); **even load** (`load_ratio < 1.10`; distribution sums to table size; all nodes present); **disruption** (< 0.20 of keys move on remove; no key ‚Üí removed node); single node owns all; node management (add rebuilds / dup ‚Üí False / remove present-absent / numeric ids); validation (more nodes than slots, `table_size`, `seed`, non-iterable, bools) + `MaglevError.detail`; properties / stats (incl. empty); reset; concurrent lookups + mutations; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. lookup **400** with no nodes + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `rendezvous`).
- ‚úÖ 120E: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 257 test modules registered (Phase 120 appends `test_maglev.py` + `test_maglev_web.py`).

**Phase 121 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 259 test modules green. Sovereign Invertible Bloom Lookup Table (Goodrich & Mitzenmacher, 2011) ‚ÄĒ a probabilistic **key‚Üívalue store that can be fully enumerated and differenced**, a capability the platform's filters and sketches lacked. The cells are **partitioned** into `k` sub-tables (one cell per sub-table per key, so a key touches `k` distinct cells); each cell holds four XOR accumulators ‚ÄĒ `count`, `key_sum`, `value_sum`, `key_hash_sum`. `insert` / `delete` XOR a key's `(key, value)` into its `k` cells and adjust counts by `¬Ī1` (a `delete` may drive counts negative ‚ÄĒ that powers reconciliation). Beyond a *best-effort* `get` (decodes a key only from a pure cell ‚ÄĒ measured recall 0.967 at load 0.15, **never a wrong value**), two operations make it invertible: **`list_entries()`** decodes the *whole* table by **peeling** ‚ÄĒ repeatedly find a pure cell (`|count| == 1` whose `key_hash_sum` matches the hash of its `key_sum`), emit its `(key, value)`, XOR it out of its other cells, exposing new pure cells ‚ÄĒ recovering **every** entry below the load threshold (verified 300/300; raises when overloaded); and **`subtract(other)`** combines two tables cellwise into an IBLT of the **symmetric difference**, which `decode_difference()` peels into *only-in-self* (positive count) and *only-in-other* (negative) ‚ÄĒ the basis of **set reconciliation** (verified: A\B and B\A recovered exactly). A *new capability* ‚ÄĒ listable, differenceable storage ‚ÄĒ distinct from the static Bloomier map (P114). Keys/values are any hashable (folded to 64-bit ids with a registry for output). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/iblt_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 121A: `pradyos/core/iblt.py` ‚ÄĒ `IBLTError(detail)`; `InvertibleBloomLookupTable(num_cells=1000, num_hashes=4, seed=0)` (partitioned: `m = (num_cells // k)¬∑k`) with `insert(key, value)` / `delete(key, value)`, `get(key, default=None)` (best-effort) / `contains` / `__contains__`, `list_entries()` (raises `IBLTError` if it cannot fully decode), `is_listable()`, `subtract(other)` ‚Üí new IBLT, `decode_difference()` ‚Üí `(only_self, only_other)`, `reset()`, `__len__`, and `num_cells` / `num_hashes` / `seed` properties, plus `stats()` (size / num_cells / num_hashes / listable / seed). Invalid `num_cells` / `num_hashes` (‚ąČ ‚Ą§‚Āļ) / `seed`, or an incompatible `other`, raise `IBLTError` (bools rejected).
- ‚úÖ 121B: `pradyos/web/iblt_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_iblt_routes(app, iblt=None)` (defaults to a fresh table) mounts 7 (all-static) route-method combos: `POST /api/v1/iblt/insert` (body `{key, value}`; 422 on missing), `DELETE /api/v1/iblt/delete` (body `{key, value}`; 422 on missing), `GET /api/v1/iblt/get` (`?key=`; `{key, found, value}`), `GET /api/v1/iblt/list` (`{entries, count}`; **400 if not decodable**), `POST /api/v1/iblt/reconcile` (body `{pairs: [[k,v],...]}` ‚Üí `{only_here, only_other}`; 422 on bad pairs, **400 if the difference is too large**), `GET /api/v1/iblt/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/iblt/reset`.
- ‚úÖ 121C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase121.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `iblt` param, and a single `register_iblt_routes(app, iblt)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.

**Phase 122 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 261 test modules green. Sovereign b-bit MinHash (Li & K√∂nig, 2010 ‚ÄĒ *b-bit minwise hashing*) ‚ÄĒ a **space-compressed similarity sketch**: where MinHash (P88) stores `k` full 64-bit minimum-hash values, b-bit MinHash keeps only the **lowest `b` bits** of each (often `b = 1` or `2`), shrinking the stored signature ~`b/64`√ó while preserving Jaccard accuracy via a **bias-corrected estimator**. Two sets of Jaccard `J` agree on a position with probability `J + (1 ‚ąí J)¬∑C`, where `C = 2^(‚ąíb)` is the chance two *different* minimums share their low `b` bits; the estimator inverts this: `ńī = (match_rate ‚ąí C)/(1 ‚ąí C)`. A larger `b` shrinks the correction (lower variance, toward full MinHash); a smaller `b` saves more space (measured: Jaccard within ~0.03 across overlap levels at `b=4, k=512`; mean error falls as `b` grows). This is a *different* algorithm from MinHash/P88 (full signatures) and MinHash-LSH/P115 (banded index) ‚ÄĒ the compact estimator you store or transmit at scale. The builder keeps full running minimums (needed to fold incrementally); `signature()` exposes the compact `b`-bit form and `jaccard()` / `estimate_jaccard()` compare two signatures. Universal hashing with seeded coefficients keeps it deterministic. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/bbit_minhash_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 122A: `pradyos/core/bbit_minhash.py` ‚ÄĒ `BBitMinHashError(detail)`; module-level `estimate_jaccard(sig_a, sig_b, b)`; `BBitMinHash(num_perm=128, b=2, seed=0)` with `add(item)` / `add_many(iter)`, `signature()` (compact `b`-bit tuple), `jaccard(other)` (bias-corrected; `BBitMinHashError` on incompatible / non-sketch), `signature_bits()` (`k¬∑b`), `reset(num_perm=None, b=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, and `num_perm` / `b` / `seed` / `count` properties, plus `stats()` (num_perm / b / count / signature_bits / seed). Invalid `num_perm` (‚ąČ ‚Ą§‚Āļ) / `b` (‚ąČ 1..32) / `seed` raise `BBitMinHashError` (bools rejected).
- ‚úÖ 122B: `pradyos/web/bbit_minhash_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_bbitminhash_routes(app, bbit_minhash=None)` (defaults to a fresh sketch) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/bbitminhash/add` (body `{element}`; 422 on missing), `POST /api/v1/bbitminhash/compare` (body `{tokens[]}` ‚Üí `{jaccard}`; 422 on non-list), `GET /api/v1/bbitminhash/signature` (`{signature, signature_bits}`), `GET /api/v1/bbitminhash/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/bbitminhash/reset` (body `{num_perm?, b?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ‚úÖ 122C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase122.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `bbit_minhash` param, and a single `register_bbitminhash_routes(app, bbit_minhash)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.

**Phase 123 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 263 test modules green. Sovereign Conservative-Update Count-Min Sketch / CU Sketch (Estan & Varghese, 2002) ‚ÄĒ a frequency sketch *strictly more accurate* than the platform's Count-Min (P76), differing only in the **update rule**. Both keep a `depth √ó width` counter grid and report `estimate = min` of an item's `depth` counters; but where Count-Min increments **all** `depth` counters, the conservative update computes `est = min` of those counters and raises each only to `max(counter, est + amount)` ‚ÄĒ i.e. only the counter(s) at the current minimum move. This provably **never under-counts** (the minimum still rises by the inserted mass) and **never exceeds the Count-Min estimate**, while sharply cutting over-estimation (measured against an inline reference Count-Min on a collision-heavy stream: **mean over-estimate 22.7 vs 44.3 ‚ÄĒ roughly half**; every key `CU ‚Č§ CM`; heavy hitter exact within 2 %). The trade-off: conservative update can't be safely reversed, so it is an **insert-and-query** estimator with no `delete`. A *different* algorithm from Count-Min/P76 (all-counter increment) and Count-Sketch/P94 (signed + median) ‚ÄĒ same grid, smarter writes. Double-hashing from one seeded BLAKE2b digest; arbitrary-width Python int counters. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/cu_sketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 123A: `pradyos/core/cu_sketch.py` ‚ÄĒ `CUSketchError(detail)`; `CUSketch(width=2048, depth=4, seed=0)` with `add(item, amount=1)` (conservative update; `CUSketchError` on `amount ‚ąČ ‚Ą§‚Āļ`), `estimate(item)` (min of `depth` counters), `reset(width=None, depth=None, seed=None)`, and `width` / `depth` / `seed` / `total` properties, plus `stats()` (width / depth / total / num_counters / seed). Invalid `width` / `depth` (‚ąČ ‚Ą§‚Āļ) / `seed` raise `CUSketchError` (bools rejected).
- ‚úÖ 123B: `pradyos/web/cu_sketch_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_cusketch_routes(app, cu_sketch=None)` (defaults to a fresh sketch) mounts 4 (all-static) routes ‚ÄĒ **no remove (conservative update is irreversible)**: `POST /api/v1/cusketch/add` (body `{item, amount?}`; 422 on missing / bad amount), `GET /api/v1/cusketch/estimate` (`?item=`), `GET /api/v1/cusketch/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/cusketch/reset` (body `{width?, depth?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- ‚úÖ 123C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase123.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `cu_sketch` param, and a single `register_cusketch_routes(app, cu_sketch)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 123D: `tests/test_cu_sketch.py` (26) + `tests/test_cusketch_web.py` (17) ‚ÄĒ **never under-counts**; **`CU ‚Č§ Count-Min`** for every key (vs an inline reference CM) + **CU mean error < CM**; exact at low load; heavy hitter within 2 %; `amount` increments (default 1) / `total`; determinism (same seed ‚Üí identical counters; different seed diverges); validation (`width`/`depth`/`seed`, bools, `amount ‚ąą {0, ‚ąí1, 2.5}`) + `CUSketchError.detail`; properties / stats; reset clears + reconfigures; 10-thread concurrent adds; all 4 endpoints over HTTP incl. never-undercount + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `bbitminhash`).

**Phase 124 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 265 test modules green. Sovereign Jump Consistent Hash (Lamping & Veach, 2014) ‚ÄĒ Google's strikingly compact consistent-hashing scheme and the **fourth** distributed key‚Üíbucket assignment algorithm, alongside the Hash Ring (P73), Rendezvous/HRW (P119) and Maglev (P120). Its whole state is a single integer ‚ÄĒ the **bucket count** ‚ÄĒ with no ring, score array, or lookup table. `assign` runs a short loop using the key's 64-bit hash as a seeded LCG: `b=-1, j=0; while j<num_buckets: b=j; key=key¬∑2862933555777941757+1; j=‚Ćä(b+1)¬∑(2¬≥¬Ļ/((key>>33)+1))‚Ćč; return b` ‚ÄĒ `O(ln N)` time, `O(1)` space, zero allocation. It provably gives **uniform load** (measured 1937‚Äď2063 per bucket over 20k keys / 10 buckets) and **optimal minimal disruption**: growing `N ‚Üí N+1` moves *exactly* `1/(N+1)` of keys, only into the new bucket (measured 0.0906 ‚Čą 1/11, every move into bucket 10, all others unchanged ‚ÄĒ the information-theoretic minimum). The trade-off vs ring/HRW/Maglev: buckets are an ordered range `[0, N)` with no arbitrary names, and only the *last* bucket removes cheaply. A *different* mechanism again ‚ÄĒ a stateless jump loop. The key folds via seeded BLAKE2b; the loop is deterministic. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/jump_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 124A: `pradyos/core/jump_hash.py` ‚ÄĒ module-level `jump_consistent_hash(key_hash, num_buckets)` (the Lamping‚ÄďVeach core); `JumpHashError(detail)`; `JumpHash(num_buckets=1, seed=0)` with `assign(key)`, `assign_for(key, num_buckets)` (stateless probe), `set_buckets(n)` / `add_bucket()` / `remove_bucket()` (last only; raises on the final bucket), `reset(num_buckets=None, seed=None)`, `load_distribution(keys)`, and `num_buckets` / `seed` properties, plus `stats()` (num_buckets / seed). Invalid `num_buckets` (‚ąČ ‚Ą§‚Āļ) / `seed` raise `JumpHashError` (bools rejected).
- ‚úÖ 124B: `pradyos/web/jump_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_jump_routes(app, jump_hash=None)` (defaults to a fresh hasher) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `GET /api/v1/jump/assign` (`?key=`; `{key, bucket, num_buckets}`), `POST /api/v1/jump/buckets` (body `{num_buckets}`; 422 on missing / bad), `GET /api/v1/jump/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/jump/reset` (body `{num_buckets?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).

Sovereign Frugal Streaming quantile / Frugal-2U (Ma, Muthukrishnan & Sandler, 2014) ‚ÄĒ a quantile estimator in **O(1) memory** (essentially a single value), where the platform's other quantile sketches (GK/P91, KLL/P92, t-Digest/P79, DDSketch/P96, Q-Digest/P105, Moment/P106) all keep many summaries. For a target quantile `q` it holds an estimate `mŐÉ` and an adaptive integer `step`; on each item it nudges `mŐÉ` up (`x > mŐÉ` and `rand() > 1 ‚ąí q`) or down (`x < mŐÉ` and `rand() > q`), with the step accelerating on consecutive same-direction moves and resetting on reversals ‚ÄĒ a stochastic-approximation chase that converges to the true `q`-quantile of a stationary stream and tracks a drifting one. Measured on a uniform[0,1000) stream of 200k (errors are *tiny* despite the constant memory): **median 498.4 (true 500), q=0.25 ‚Üí 257, q=0.75 ‚Üí 745, q=0.9 ‚Üí 902**; estimates monotonic across `q`; it tracks a distribution shift (median 54 ‚Üí 951) and lands a skewed (exponential) median at 79.7 (true ‚Čą 69). The *extreme-low-memory* point of the quantile design space ‚ÄĒ no buckets, no centroids, just a tracker. The coin is a seeded `random.Random` so a fixed seed + stream reproduce the run. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/frugal_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 125A: `pradyos/core/frugal.py` ‚ÄĒ `FrugalError(detail)`; `FrugalQuantile(quantile=0.5, seed=0)` with `add(value)` (Frugal-2U update; first sample seeds `mŐÉ`), `add_many(iter)`, `estimate()`, `reset(quantile=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, and `quantile` / `seed` / `count` properties, plus `stats()` (quantile / estimate / step / count / seed). Invalid `quantile` (‚ąČ (0,1)) / `seed` / non-numeric `value` raise `FrugalError` (bools rejected).
- ‚úÖ 125B: `pradyos/web/frugal_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_frugal_routes(app, frugal=None)` (defaults to a fresh median estimator) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/frugal/add` (body `{value}`; 422 on missing / non-number), `GET /api/v1/frugal/estimate` (`{estimate, quantile, count}`), `GET /api/v1/frugal/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/frugal/reset` (body `{quantile?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).

**Phase 126 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 269 test modules green. Sovereign Cosine LSH / Random-Hyperplane LSH index (Charikar, 2002; Indyk & Motwani, 1998) ‚ÄĒ a **similarity-search index for cosine similarity over vectors**, the cosine counterpart to the platform's MinHash-LSH (P115, which indexes *Jaccard* over sets). Each item vector is reduced to a `k`-bit **SimHash** signature by `k` random hyperplanes (bit `i` = sign of the dot product with hyperplane `i`, drawn from a seeded standard normal); two vectors at angle `őł` agree on a bit with probability `1 ‚ąí őł/ŌÄ`, so the bit-agreement fraction estimates the angle and `cos(ŌÄ¬∑(1 ‚ąí agreement))` estimates the cosine (measured within **0.04** of true across angles 0‚Ä¶ŌÄ). The signature splits into `bands` bands of `rows` bits and buckets per band, so vectors collide in a band iff they match every bit ‚ÄĒ the tunable LSH S-curve, now over *angular* distance; `query(vector)` gathers band-bucket candidates and refines by estimated cosine ‚Č• threshold (measured **recall 1.0** on near-duplicate vectors; orthogonal correctly excluded at threshold). A *different* index from MinHash-LSH/P115 (min-hashes over sets) ‚ÄĒ random hyperplanes over real vectors ‚ÄĒ and the *indexed search* the SimHash estimator (P89) lacks. Deterministic given the seed. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/simhash_lsh_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 126A: `pradyos/core/simhash_lsh.py` ‚ÄĒ `SimHashLSHError(detail)`; `SimHashLSH(dim=64, bands=16, rows=4, seed=0)` (`k = bands¬∑rows` hyperplanes of dimension `dim`) with `insert(item_id, vector)` (re-insert replaces; validates dimension + numeric), `query(vector, threshold=0.0)` ‚Üí `[(id, cosine), ...]` desc, `similarity(a, b)` (estimated cosine), `remove(item_id)` ‚Üí bool, `contains` / `__contains__`, `reset(dim=None, bands=None, rows=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, and `dim` / `bands` / `rows` / `num_perm` (k) / `seed` properties, plus `stats()`. Invalid `dim` / `bands` / `rows` (‚ąČ ‚Ą§‚Āļ) / `seed`, wrong-dimension or non-numeric vector, or `threshold ‚ąČ [‚ąí1, 1]` raise `SimHashLSHError` (bools rejected).
- ‚úÖ 126B: `pradyos/web/simhash_lsh_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_simhashlsh_routes(app, simhash_lsh=None)` mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/simhashlsh/insert` (body `{id, vector[]}`; 422 on missing / non-list / wrong-dim), `POST /api/v1/simhashlsh/query` (body `{vector[], threshold?}`; 422 on bad), `DELETE /api/v1/simhashlsh/remove` (body `{id}`), `GET /api/v1/simhashlsh/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/simhashlsh/reset` (body `{dim?, bands?, rows?, seed?}`).
- ‚úÖ 126C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase126.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `simhash_lsh` param, and a single `register_simhashlsh_routes(app, simhash_lsh)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 126D: `tests/test_simhash_lsh.py` (31) + `tests/test_simhashlsh_web.py` (18) ‚ÄĒ **cosine estimate** (self = 1, within 0.12 across angles, opposite ‚Čą ‚ąí1); **retrieval** (near-parallel found, orthogonal excluded at threshold, sorted desc, threshold filters, **recall ‚Č• 0.9** on near-dups); **remove / re-insert / contains**; **determinism** (same seed ‚Üí identical query; different seed diverges signature); validation (`dim`/`bands`/`rows`/`seed`, bools, wrong-dimension & non-numeric vectors, `threshold ‚ąČ [‚ąí1,1]`) + `SimHashLSHError.detail`; properties / stats; reset clears + reconfigures; 10-thread concurrent inserts; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. wrong-dim 422 + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `frugal`).

**Phase 127 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 271 test modules green. Sovereign Random Projection / Johnson‚ÄďLindenstrauss sketch (Johnson & Lindenstrauss, 1984; Achlioptas, 2001) ‚ÄĒ a **distance-preserving dimensionality-reduction** sketch, a new capability for the platform. It multiplies each `d`-dimensional input vector by a fixed random `k √ó d` matrix (`k ‚Č™ d`) of **Rademacher** entries `¬Ī1/‚ąök` (each sign w.p. ¬Ĺ) to produce a `k`-dimensional sketch; since those entries are zero-mean / unit-variance after scaling, `E[‚ÄĖRx‚ÄĖ¬≤] = ‚ÄĖx‚ÄĖ¬≤` and `E[‚ü®Rx, Ry‚ü©] = ‚ü®x, y‚ü©`, so the projection is an *unbiased isometry in expectation*. The Johnson‚ÄďLindenstrauss lemma then guarantees that for `k = O(ln n / őĶ¬≤)` *all* pairwise **Euclidean distances and dot products are preserved within `(1 ¬Ī őĶ)`** with high probability ‚ÄĒ so similarity search, clustering and nearest-neighbour work on the small sketches at a fraction of the cost (measured: mean distance ratio **0.9992**, >85% of pairs within ¬Ī30% at `k=64`, distortion shrinks as `k` grows). Distinct from the platform's *hashing*-based sketches (MinHash/SimHash/LSH, which each preserve a single similarity): random projection preserves the *geometry* of the whole space ‚ÄĒ every distance and angle at once ‚ÄĒ in a dense real sketch. Exposes `project(vector)`, plus `distance` / `dot` / `norm` estimators on the projected space. Exposed at `/api/v1/randomprojection`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`; the random matrix is drawn from a seeded `random.Random` for reproducibility. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/random_projection_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 127A: `pradyos/core/random_projection.py` ‚ÄĒ `RandomProjectionError(detail)`; `RandomProjection(input_dim=128, output_dim=16, seed=0)` with `project(vector)` ‚Üí `k`-vector, `distance(a, b)` / `dot(a, b)` / `norm(v)` estimators over the projection, `reset(input_dim=None, output_dim=None, seed=None)` (redraws the matrix; optional reconfigure), `input_dim` / `output_dim` / `seed` properties, and `stats()` (`input_dim` / `output_dim` / `compression_ratio` = d/k / `seed`). Invalid `input_dim` / `output_dim` (‚ąČ ‚Ą§‚Āļ) or `seed` (‚ąČ ‚Ą§), and wrong-dimension or non-numeric vectors, raise `RandomProjectionError` (bools rejected).
- ‚úÖ 127B: `pradyos/web/random_projection_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_randomprojection_routes(app, random_projection=None)` mounts 5 routes: `POST /api/v1/randomprojection/project` (body `{vector[]}`; 422 on missing / non-list / wrong-dim), `POST /api/v1/randomprojection/distance` (body `{a[], b[]}`), `POST /api/v1/randomprojection/dot` (body `{a[], b[]}`), `GET /api/v1/randomprojection/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/randomprojection/reset` (body `{input_dim?, output_dim?, seed?}`).
- ‚úÖ 127C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase127.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `random_projection` param, and a single `register_randomprojection_routes(app, random_projection)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.

**Phase 128 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 273 test modules green. Sovereign Golomb-Coded Set (Putze, Sanders & Singler, 2007; Golomb‚ÄďRice coding, 1966) ‚ÄĒ a **compressed, space-optimal static set-membership** structure, a new capability for the platform. Where the Bloom family (P72/counting/scalable/stable/cuckoo/xor/binary-fuse/ribbon/quotient) keeps membership in a *live bit-array*, a GCS stores the set as a *compressed byte stream*: it hashes the `n` items into the universe `[0, N)` with `N = ‚Ćąn/p‚ĆČ` for target false-positive rate `p`, sorts the fingerprints (dropping duplicates), and stores the **gaps** between consecutive fingerprints with **Golomb‚ÄďRice codes** whose parameter is the optimum `M ‚Čą ln2¬∑(N/n) = ln2/p` for the (nearly geometric, mean `1/p`) gaps ‚ÄĒ each gap `g` written as `g // M` in unary then `g % M` in truncated binary. This reaches within ~1.5 bits of the `log‚āā(1/p)` information-theoretic lower bound per item ‚ÄĒ *more compact than a Bloom filter* (which needs `1.44¬∑log‚āā(1/p)`): **measured 8.12 bits/item vs Bloom's 9.57 at `p=0.01`** (floor 6.64) ‚ÄĒ at the cost of being **immutable once built** and `O(n)`-decoded per query (the canonical use is shipping a compact set over the wire, √† la Chrome's CRLSet). `contains(item)` re-hashes and walks the decoded gap stream with an early exit ‚ÄĒ **zero false negatives** and a **measured FP rate of 0.0093** against the 0.01 target. A *different* structure from every existing membership filter (those are mutable bit-array sketches; this is a static, near-entropy-optimal *compressed encoding*). Exposed at `/api/v1/gcs`. Pure stdlib (`hashlib.blake2b` fingerprints); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`; deterministic given the seed. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/gcs_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 128A: `pradyos/core/golomb_coded_set.py` ‚ÄĒ `GolombCodedSetError(detail)`; `GolombCodedSet(items=None, p=0.01, seed=0)` (static ‚ÄĒ built from the full item set) with `build(items)` (rebuild, replacing contents), `contains(item)` / `__contains__`, `reset(p=None, seed=None)` (clear / reconfigure), `__len__` (distinct fingerprints), and `p` / `seed` / `num_items` / `universe` / `golomb_m` / `num_bits` properties + `bits_per_item()` + `stats()`. Internal `_BitWriter` / `_BitReader` (MSB-first, bounded to the exact real bit count so padding is never misdecoded) and a truncated-binary Golomb codec handling `M=1` (pure unary) through power-of-two (Rice) and arbitrary `M`. Items are type-tagged (`int 1` / `str "1"` / `bytes b"1"` never alias); invalid `p` (‚ąČ (0,1)) / `seed` (‚ąČ ‚Ą§) / item type (float, bool, ‚Ä¶) raise `GolombCodedSetError`.
- ‚úÖ 128B: `pradyos/web/gcs_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_gcs_routes(app, gcs=None)` mounts 5 routes: `POST /api/v1/gcs/build` (body `{items[], p?, seed?}`; 422 on missing / bad config / bad item), `POST /api/v1/gcs/contains` (body `{item}`), `POST /api/v1/gcs/contains_many` (body `{items[]}` ‚Üí `{results[], count}`), `GET /api/v1/gcs/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/gcs/reset` (body `{p?, seed?}`).
- ‚úÖ 128C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase128.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `gcs` param, and a single `register_gcs_routes(app, gcs)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 128D: `tests/test_golomb_coded_set.py` (48) + `tests/test_gcs_web.py` (21) ‚ÄĒ **membership guarantees** (all members present = zero false negatives; FP within 1.5√ó`p`); **Golomb codec** round-trips exactly across 11 `M` values incl. `M=1` & powers of two, consuming the bit stream exactly (no padding misread) + reader-exhaustion guard; **compression** beats Bloom `1.44¬∑log‚āā(1/p)` yet stays above the entropy floor, smaller `p` ‚áí more bits/item, `universe = ‚Ćąn/p‚ĆČ`, optimal `M`; **type handling** (str/bytes/int accepted & type-tagged; float/bool/non-iterable rejected); **fingerprint self-collisions only shrink the distinct count, never cause a false negative** (exact counts verified in a collision-free `p=1e-6` regime); validation (`p`/`seed`, bools) + `GolombCodedSetError.detail`; reset clears + reconfigures; 10-thread concurrent `contains`; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. 422s + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `randomprojection`).

**Phase 129 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 275 test modules green. Sovereign Flajolet‚ÄďMartin / PCSA cardinality sketch (Flajolet & Martin, 1985 ‚ÄĒ *Probabilistic Counting with Stochastic Averaging*) ‚ÄĒ the **original distinct-count estimator** and the progenitor of every later cardinality sketch on the platform, with a fundamentally different mechanism: it estimates distinct counts from **bit patterns**. Each element is hashed; the **trailing-zero count** `ŌĀ` of the (low) hash bits is geometric (`P(ŌĀ=i) = 2^‚ąí(i+1)`), so setting bit `ŌĀ` of a bitmap leaves a frontier whose **lowest unset bit** `R` satisfies `E[R] ‚Čą log‚āā(ŌÜ¬∑n)` with `ŌÜ ‚Čą 0.77351`. **Stochastic averaging** routes each item to one of `m` bitmaps by a leading-hash prefix and averages the lowest-unset positions `A = (1/m)¬∑ő£ R_j`, giving estimate `nŐā = (m/ŌÜ)¬∑2^A` with standard error `‚Čą 0.78/‚ąöm`. This is *different* from the platform's other cardinality sketches: HyperLogLog/P74 (harmonic mean of *max*-leading-zero registers), Theta/P93 (KMV min-hashes), Linear Counting (bit-array fill ratio), HyperMinHash/P117 ‚ÄĒ FM/PCSA is the bit-pattern-observable original they descend from. Mergeable (bitmap-wise OR). **Measured** (honest, `m=64`): mean estimate within ~**4%** of truth for `n ‚Č≥ m` (ratio ‚Čą 1.025 at n=5000, 1.037 at n=50000), typical single-run error ‚Čą **7.6%** (vs SE 9.75%), merge of two disjoint 5000-sets estimates 9817; the **empty sketch reports exactly 0** and ‚ÄĒ like the original FM ‚ÄĒ **very small cardinalities are overestimated** (the classic small-range bias, `n=1 ‚Üí ‚Čą1.29m`). Exposed at `/api/v1/fmsketch`. Pure stdlib (`hashlib.blake2b`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`; deterministic given the seed. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/fmsketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 129A: `pradyos/core/fm_sketch.py` ‚ÄĒ `FMSketchError(detail)`; `FMSketch(num_bitmaps=64, num_bits=32, seed=0)` with `add(item)` / `add_many(items)` ‚Üí count, `estimate()` ‚Üí float / `count()` ‚Üí int / `__len__`, `merge(other)` (bitmap-OR; configs must match), `reset(num_bitmaps=None, num_bits=None, seed=None)`, and `num_bitmaps` / `num_bits` / `seed` / `standard_error` (`0.78/‚ąöm`) properties + `stats()`. `num_bitmaps` must be a power of two in `[1, 65536]`, `num_bits ‚ąą [1, 32]`, `seed ‚ąą ‚Ą§`; items are type-tagged str/bytes/int (float/bool rejected) ‚ÄĒ all violations raise `FMSketchError`.
- ‚úÖ 129B: `pradyos/web/fmsketch_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_fmsketch_routes(app, fm_sketch=None)` mounts 5 routes: `POST /api/v1/fmsketch/add` (body `{item}`; 422 on missing / bad type), `POST /api/v1/fmsketch/add_many` (body `{items[]}` ‚Üí `{added, estimate}`), `GET /api/v1/fmsketch/estimate` (`{estimate, count}`), `GET /api/v1/fmsketch/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/fmsketch/reset` (body `{num_bitmaps?, num_bits?, seed?}`).
- ‚úÖ 129C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase129.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `fm_sketch` param, and a single `register_fmsketch_routes(app, fm_sketch)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 129D: `tests/test_fm_sketch.py` (39) + `tests/test_fmsketch_web.py` (19) ‚ÄĒ **accuracy** as multi-seed means (unbiased to ~8% at n=5000 & n=50000; larger `m` tightens typical error; loose single-run bound); **structural** (empty‚Üí0, count rounds, len, monotone, add-from-zero, **idempotent on duplicate adds**, add_many count, documented small-n overestimation); **determinism** (same seed identical; different seed diverges bitmaps); **merge** (‚Čą union of disjoint sets, OR-with-self idempotent, subset adds nothing, config/seed/non-sketch mismatches raise); validation (`num_bitmaps` power-of-two & ‚Č§65536, `num_bits‚ąą[1,32]`, `seed`, bools) + `FMSketchError.detail`; type handling (str/bytes/int; float/bool rejected); reset clears + reconfigures; 10-thread concurrent adds; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. 422s + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `gcs`).

**Phase 130 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 277 test modules green. Sovereign AMS sketch / tug-of-war second-moment estimator (Alon, Matias & Szegedy, 1996 ‚ÄĒ the G√∂del-Prize *frequency-moments* work) ‚ÄĒ a **streaming `F‚āā` (second-moment / squared-L2-norm / self-join-size) and inner-product estimator**, a new aggregate-estimation capability for the platform. Each update `(key, ¬Īcount)` is mapped by a sign hash `őĶ(key) ‚ąą {‚ąí1, +1}`; a single counter `X = ő£_i f_i¬∑őĶ(i)` has `E[X¬≤] = ő£_i f_i¬≤ = F‚āā` (the cross terms cancel because the signs are zero-mean and independent), so `X¬≤` is an *unbiased* estimator of `F‚āā`. The classic **median-of-means** construction tames its variance (`Var[X¬≤] ‚Č§ 2F‚āā¬≤`): average `X¬≤` across `width` independent counters (relative SE `‚Čą ‚ąö(2/width)`) and take the **median** across `depth` rows. With the same sign hashes, two sketches estimate the **inner product** `ő£_i f_i¬∑g_i` (join size) via `median_r mean_c (XŠ∂†¬∑XŠĶć)`, and sketches are **mergeable** by counter-wise addition ‚ÄĒ the sketch is linear in the counts, so it natively supports the turnstile model (negative updates). **Measured** (honest, `width=64`, `depth=7`): mean `F‚āā` within ~**1.6%** of exact over 40 seeds, typical single-run error **6.4%** (median-of-means beats the per-row SE 0.177), `width=256 ‚Üí 3.5%`; inner-product mean ratio 1.007, merge-linearity 0.998; **empty ‚Üí exactly 0**, turnstile `+c` then `‚ąíc` cancels to 0, a single `‚ąí7` update gives `F‚āā = 49`. This is *different* from CountSketch/P94 and Count-Min/P76, which answer *point queries* (per-key frequency): AMS estimates a *scalar aggregate* of the whole frequency vector ‚ÄĒ its second moment, L2 norm, or join size. Exposed at `/api/v1/ams`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`; deterministic given the seed ‚ÄĒ the `width¬∑depth` independent ¬Ī1 signs per key are sliced from the bits of a (multi-block) seeded `blake2b` digest. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/ams_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 130A: `pradyos/core/ams_sketch.py` ‚ÄĒ `AMSError(detail)`; `AMSSketch(width=64, depth=7, seed=0)` with `update(key, count=1)` (count may be negative ‚ÄĒ turnstile), `update_many(keys)` ‚Üí count, `f2()` / `second_moment()` / `l2_norm()`, `inner_product(other)` and `merge(other)` (configs must match), `reset(width=None, depth=None, seed=None)`, and `width` / `depth` / `seed` / `num_counters` / `standard_error` (`‚ąö(2/width)`) properties + `stats()`. `width`/`depth` positive ints with `width¬∑depth ‚Č§ 65536`; `seed`/`count` ints; keys type-tagged str/bytes/int ‚ÄĒ violations (incl. bools, float keys/counts) raise `AMSError`.
- ‚úÖ 130B: `pradyos/web/ams_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_ams_routes(app, ams=None)` mounts 5 routes: `POST /api/v1/ams/update` (body `{key, count?}`; 422 on missing / bad type), `POST /api/v1/ams/update_many` (body `{keys[]}` ‚Üí `{added, f2}`), `GET /api/v1/ams/f2` (`{f2, l2_norm}`), `GET /api/v1/ams/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/ams/reset` (body `{width?, depth?, seed?}`).
- ‚úÖ 130C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase130.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `ams` param, and a single `register_ams_routes(app, ams)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 130D: `tests/test_ams_sketch.py` (43) + `tests/test_ams_web.py` (21) ‚ÄĒ **`F‚āā` accuracy** as multi-seed means (unbiased to ~8%; larger `width` tightens; loose single-run bound); **identities** (`l2_norm = ‚ąöF‚āā`, `inner_product(self) = F‚āā`, `merge(self)` quadruples `F‚āā`, disjoint inner-product mean ‚Čą 0); **turnstile** (cancellation ‚Üí 0, single `‚ąí7` ‚Üí 49, default-count accumulation, `F‚āā ‚Č• 0`); **merge** linearity vs exact summed-stream `F‚āā`; `update_many` matches per-item updates; **determinism** (same seed identical; different seed diverges counters); validation (`width`/`depth`/`width¬∑depth‚Č§65536`/`seed`/`count`, bools) + `AMSError.detail`; type handling (str/bytes/int; float/bool rejected); reset clears + reconfigures; 10-thread concurrent updates; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. 422s + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `fmsketch`).

**Phase 131 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 279 test modules green. Sovereign Priority Sampling (Duffield, Lund & Thorup, 2007) ‚ÄĒ a **bounded-size weighted sample that gives unbiased subset-sum estimates**, a new sampling capability distinct from the platform's Reservoir/P85 (uniform sample) and Weighted-Reservoir/P98 (a single weighted draw). Each arriving item `(key, weight>0)` gets a **priority** `q = weight / u` where `u ‚ąľ Uniform(0,1]` (a deterministic per-key hash); the sketch keeps the `k` highest-priority items in a min-heap (lazy deletion on re-add). The threshold `ŌĄ` is the `(k+1)`-th largest priority ‚ÄĒ the largest priority among *evicted* items (`ŌĄ = 0` while ‚Č§ `k` items have been seen, so the sample is then **exact**), and each retained item gets an **adjusted weight** `ŇĶ = max(weight, ŌĄ)`. Then for **any** subset `S`, `ő£_{i‚ąąS‚ą©sample} ŇĶ_i` is an *unbiased* estimator of `ő£_{i‚ąąS} w_i` ‚ÄĒ so a single bounded sample answers arbitrary subset-sum / total-weight queries (addressed here by a **category** tag) with provably zero bias and variance `O(1/k)`. **Measured** (honest, `k=256`): mean total estimate within ~**1.4%** of exact over 40 seeds (ratio ‚Čą 0.986), typical single-run error **3.7%**, `k=1024 ‚Üí 1.8%`; per-category sums unbiased (ratios 0.96‚Äď1.02); `N ‚Č§ k` is **exact** with `ŌĄ=0`; the result is **order-independent** (identical total / sample / threshold across shuffles). This is *different* from uniform reservoir sampling (which estimates counts, not weighted sums) and from a single weighted draw: priority sampling is the unbiased-aggregate-over-a-bounded-sample primitive. Exposed at `/api/v1/prioritysample`. Pure stdlib (`heapq`, `hashlib.blake2b`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`; deterministic given the seed. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/priority_sampling_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 131A: `pradyos/core/priority_sampling.py` ‚ÄĒ `PrioritySampleError(detail)`; `PrioritySample(capacity=256, seed=0)` with `add(key, weight, category=None)` ‚Üí sampled-bool, `add_many(items)` ‚Üí count, `estimate(category=None)` (unbiased subset-sum) / `total()`, `sample_keys()`, `reset(capacity=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, and `capacity` / `seed` / `num_seen` / `threshold` properties + `stats()`. Keys are type-tagged str/bytes/int; `capacity` positive int, `seed` int, `weight` a number > 0, `category` str-or-None ‚ÄĒ violations (incl. bools, float keys, zero/negative weights) raise `PrioritySampleError`.
- ‚úÖ 131B: `pradyos/web/priority_sampling_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_prioritysample_routes(app, priority_sample=None)` mounts 5 routes: `POST /api/v1/prioritysample/add` (body `{key, weight, category?}`; 422 on missing / bad), `POST /api/v1/prioritysample/add_many` (body `{items: [[key, weight(, category)], ...]}`), `GET /api/v1/prioritysample/estimate` (query `?category=`), `GET /api/v1/prioritysample/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/prioritysample/reset` (body `{capacity?, seed?}`).
- ‚úÖ 131C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase131.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `priority_sample` param, and a single `register_prioritysample_routes(app, priority_sample)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 131D: `tests/test_priority_sampling.py` (41) + `tests/test_priority_sampling_web.py` (22) ‚ÄĒ **unbiasedness** as multi-seed means (total to ~6%, per-category to ~10%, larger `k` tightens, loose single-run bound); **exact when `N ‚Č§ k`** (total & per-category exact, `ŌĄ=0`, holds all); **order independence** (total / sample / threshold identical across shuffles) & determinism; structural (capacity cap, `ŌĄ>0` when `N>k`, `num_seen`, sampled-bool, empty‚Üí0); `add_many` arity; re-add last-write-wins; validation (`capacity`/`seed`/`weight>0`/`category`, bools, float keys) + `PrioritySampleError.detail`; reset clears + reconfigures; 10-thread concurrent adds; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. 422s + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `ams`).

**Phase 132 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 281 test modules green. Sovereign Cuckoo Hash Table (Pagh & Rodler, 2001) ‚ÄĒ an **exact key‚Üívalue dictionary with worst-case `O(1)` lookup**, a new capability for the platform. This is *categorically different* from the Cuckoo **Filter** of P86 (at `/api/v1/cuckoo`), which is an *approximate set-membership* sketch with a false-positive rate: a Cuckoo Hash *Table* stores the actual key/value pairs and answers `get` / `contains` with **zero error** in **at most two slot probes**, independent of load. Two tables `T1`, `T2` (each `m` slots) and two independent hashes give every key exactly two candidate homes; an item lives in one of them, so lookup checks both ‚ÄĒ *worst-case two probes*. Insert seats the item in its `T1` home and, if occupied, **evicts** the resident (re-seated in its `T2` home, displacing the next, ‚Ä¶) ‚ÄĒ the "cuckoo" kicking chain; if the chain exceeds a bound the table **rehashes** (new seeds, growing if needed) and replays every item (amortised `O(1)`). The lookup cost is independent of item count or load factor ‚ÄĒ the defining cuckoo-hashing guarantee. **Verified** (honest): a **differential test against a Python `dict` found 0 mismatches over 20 000 mixed put/remove/query ops**; inserting 5 000 keys into a tiny `capacity=8` table grew it to 8 192 over 27 rehashes with **zero loss** and every key retrievable via the ‚Č§2-probe path. Exposed at `/api/v1/cuckoohash` (distinct from the P86 filter at `/api/v1/cuckoo`). Pure stdlib (`hashlib.blake2b` for the two hashes); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`; deterministic given the seed. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/cuckoohash_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 132A: `pradyos/core/cuckoo_hashtable.py` ‚ÄĒ `CuckooHashError(detail)`; `CuckooHashTable(capacity=16, seed=0)` with `put(key, value)` (insert/update), `put_many(items)` ‚Üí count, `get(key, default=None)` (‚Č§2 probes), `contains` / `__contains__`, `remove(key)` ‚Üí bool, `keys()`, `reset(capacity=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, and `capacity` / `seed` / `size` / `num_rehashes` / `load_factor` properties + `stats()`. Keys are type-tagged str/bytes/int (bool/float rejected ‚Üí `CuckooHashError`); the kicking chain rehashes (new seed, then grows) on cycles, always replaying every item.
- ‚úÖ 132B: `pradyos/web/cuckoohash_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_cuckoohash_routes(app, cuckoo_hashtable=None)` mounts 5 routes: `POST /api/v1/cuckoohash/put` (body `{key, value}`; 422 on missing / bad key), `POST /api/v1/cuckoohash/get` (body `{key}` ‚Üí `{key, found, value}`), `DELETE /api/v1/cuckoohash/remove` (body `{key}` ‚Üí `{key, removed}`), `GET /api/v1/cuckoohash/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/cuckoohash/reset` (body `{capacity?, seed?}`).
- ‚úÖ 132C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase132.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `cuckoo_hashtable` param, and a single `register_cuckoohash_routes(app, cuckoo_hashtable)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.

**Phase 133 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 283 test modules green. Sovereign Splay Tree (Sleator & Tarjan, 1985) ‚ÄĒ a **self-adjusting binary search tree** with amortised `O(log n)` operations and an *access-locality* guarantee, a new ordered-map mechanism for the platform. Distinct from the *randomised* balance of Treap/P113 and the *probabilistic levels* of Skip List/P78: a splay tree carries no balance metadata and instead **splays** every accessed node to the root via `zig` / `zig-zig` / `zig-zag` rotations (implemented here as the classic **top-down splay**), so recently/frequently accessed keys stay near the root and repeated-access and sequential workloads run faster than the `O(log n)` worst case (the *static-* and *dynamic-optimality* lineage). Supports ordered-map operations ‚ÄĒ `insert`, `find`, `delete`, `min`/`max`, predecessor/successor, in-order keys ‚ÄĒ each restructuring the tree by splaying. **Verified** (honest): a **differential test against a Python `dict` agreed on every `find`, the full key set, and size across 20 000 mixed insert/delete/find ops**; in-order traversal is sorted, `min`/`max`/predecessor/successor match a sorted reference, and `find`/`insert`/repeated-access provably leave the touched key at the root. Exposed at `/api/v1/splaytree`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`; **deterministic** ‚ÄĒ no randomness, so the tree shape is a pure function of the operation sequence. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/splay_tree_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 133A: `pradyos/core/splay_tree.py` ‚ÄĒ `SplayTreeError(detail)`; `SplayTree()` with `insert(key, value=None)` (update in place), `find(key, default=None)` / `contains` / `__contains__`, `delete(key)` ‚Üí bool, `min()` / `max()` (raise on empty), `predecessor(key)` / `successor(key)` ‚Üí key-or-None, `keys()` (sorted), `reset()`, `__len__`, and `size` / `root_key` / `key_kind` properties + `height()` + `stats()`. Keys must be mutually orderable ‚ÄĒ `int`/`float` (one numeric kind) or `str` ‚ÄĒ bools and non-orderable types raise `SplayTreeError`, and mixing kinds raises; every access splays the touched node to the root via top-down splay.
- ‚úÖ 133B: `pradyos/web/splay_tree_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_splaytree_routes(app, splay_tree=None)` mounts 5 routes: `POST /api/v1/splaytree/insert` (body `{key, value?}`; 422 on missing / bad / mixed-kind key), `POST /api/v1/splaytree/find` (body `{key}` ‚Üí `{key, found, value, root_key}`), `DELETE /api/v1/splaytree/delete` (body `{key}` ‚Üí `{key, deleted, size}`), `GET /api/v1/splaytree/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/splaytree/reset`.
- ‚úÖ 133C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase133.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `splay_tree` param, and a single `register_splaytree_routes(app, splay_tree)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 133D: `tests/test_splay_tree.py` (38) + `tests/test_splaytree_web.py` (23) ‚ÄĒ **ordered-map semantics** (insert/find/update/delete, in-order sorted, len, keys); **splay behaviour** (find/insert/repeated-access leave the key at the root; min/max splay up); **predecessor/successor** matched against a sorted reference incl. absent keys; **a differential test against `dict`** over thousands of mixed ops; key kinds (int/float numeric, str; bool & non-orderable rejected; mixed-kind insert raises; wrong-kind find returns default); determinism (same op sequence ‚Üí identical keys & root); reset; height in `[1, n]`; validation + `SplayTreeError.detail`; 10-thread concurrent inserts; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. 422s + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `cuckoohash`).

**Phase 134 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 285 test modules green. Sovereign Rank/Select succinct bitvector (Jacobson, 1989) ‚ÄĒ the **foundational succinct-data-structure primitive**: `O(1)` `rank` and `O(log n)` `select` over a static bit array using `o(n)` extra index bits, a new capability for the platform. `rank1(i)` counts the set bits in `bits[0..i)` and `select1(k)` returns the position of the `k`-th set bit (with `rank0`/`select0` duals); these are the operations every succinct structure (wavelet trees, succinct tries, balanced-parenthesis trees) is built on. Bits are packed into 64-bit words; a two-level index stores an absolute set-bit count before each **superblock** (8 words = 512 bits) and a relative count before each **block** (one word), so `rank1` is a superblock lookup + a block lookup + one partial-word `int.bit_count` ‚ÄĒ **constant time** ‚ÄĒ and `select` **binary-searches the cumulative rank** (`O(log n)`, cheap given `O(1)` rank). Distinct from the platform's *frequency/counting* sketches: this is an exact, deterministic index over a known bit array, not an approximate counter. **Verified** (honest): a **differential test against a naive scan matched `rank1`/`rank0`/`select1`/`select0`/`get` on genuinely-mixed bitvectors across 12 sizes ‚ÄĒ including word boundaries (63/64/65/127/128/512/513) and a superblock-crossing 6 000-bit vector** ‚ÄĒ and all identities hold (`rank1(i)+rank0(i)=i`, `arr[select1(k)]=1`, `rank1(select1(k))=k‚ąí1`). Exposed at `/api/v1/rankselect`. Pure stdlib (`int.bit_count`, Python ‚Č• 3.10); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`; deterministic (static ‚ÄĒ built once from the bit array). Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/rank_select_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 134A: `pradyos/core/rank_select.py` ‚ÄĒ `RankSelectError(detail)`; `RankSelect(bits=None)` (a `'0'/'1'` string or an iterable of `0/1`/bool) with `build(bits)` (static rebuild), `rank1(i)` / `rank0(i)` (`i ‚ąą [0, n]`), `select1(k)` / `select0(k)` (1-indexed; raise outside `[1, count]`), `get(i)`, `reset()`, `__len__`, and `size` / `count1` / `count0` properties + `stats()`. Out-of-range indices/ranks and malformed bits (non-`0/1`, non-iterable) raise `RankSelectError` (bool indices rejected).
- ‚úÖ 134B: `pradyos/web/rank_select_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_rankselect_routes(app, rank_select=None)` mounts 5 routes: `POST /api/v1/rankselect/build` (body `{bits}`; 422 on missing / malformed), `GET /api/v1/rankselect/rank` (query `?i=&bit=`, `Query(ge=0)`), `GET /api/v1/rankselect/select` (query `?k=&bit=`, `Query(ge=1)`), `GET /api/v1/rankselect/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/rankselect/reset`.
- ‚úÖ 134C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase134.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `rank_select` param, and a single `register_rankselect_routes(app, rank_select)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 134D: `tests/test_rank_select.py` (37) + `tests/test_rankselect_web.py` (23) ‚ÄĒ **a differential test against naive** for `rank1`/`rank0`/`select1`/`select0`/`get` over mixed vectors across 12 sizes + a superblock-crossing sparse vector; **identities** (`rank1+rank0=i`, `select`‚ÜĒ`rank` round-trips); edge cases (all-zeros, all-ones, empty, single bit, word boundaries); input forms (string / list / bool); select & rank bound checks (raise outside range, `Query(ge=‚Ä¶)` 422s); validation + `RankSelectError.detail`; build replaces; reset; 10-thread concurrent read queries; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. 422s + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `splaytree`).
