**Phase 158 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 333 test modules green. Sovereign Leftist Heap (Crane, 1972) ‚ÄĒ a **mergeable min-priority-queue with a *worst-case* `O(log n)` `meld`** (and hence `insert` / `extract_min`), achieved by keeping every node's **null-path-length (rank)** so that `rank(left) ‚Č• rank(right)`, which forces the right spine to length `‚Č§ log‚āā(n+1)`. Merging walks only the two right spines ‚ÄĒ the smaller root adopts the merge of its right child with the other heap, then swaps children to restore the invariant. This is a *different guarantee* from the platform's other heaps: the Skew Heap/P136 melds in *amortized* `O(log n)` with no balance field, the Pairing/P150 and Fibonacci/P154 heaps target `O(1)`-amortized `decrease_key`, and the Min-Max Heap/P144 is an array double-ended queue. It also supports an explicit `merge(other)` of two instances. Supports `insert(value)`, `find_min()`, `extract_min()`, `merge(other)`, `size`, and `reset`. **Verified** (honest): a **full-drain == `sorted` check across 60 random trials** + a 5 000-element drain, an **interleaved insert/extract run matched against `heapq` (200 ops √ó 40 trials)**, and a **`merge` differential ‚ÄĒ melding two heaps drains to `sorted(both)` and empties the source ‚ÄĒ across 40 trials**, all with the leftist invariant (`rank(left) ‚Č• rank(right)`, rank correctness, min-heap order) re-checked after every op and the root rank confirmed `‚Č§ log‚āā(n+1)`; duplicates, floats/negatives, and insertion-order independence hold. Exposed at `/api/v1/leftist`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock` (two-instance `merge` acquires both locks in `id()` order); deterministic; merge recursion descends only the right spine ‚ÄĒ depth structurally bounded at `O(log n)`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/leftist_heap_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 158A: `pradyos/core/leftist_heap.py` ‚ÄĒ `LeftistHeapError(detail)`; `LeftistHeap()` with `insert(value)`, `find_min()`, `extract_min()`, `merge(other)`, `reset()`, `is_empty()`, `size` / `len()` + `stats()`. `value` a number (bools rejected); empty `find_min`/`extract_min` raise; `merge` requires another `LeftistHeap` (not self). Rank-maintaining recursive `_merge` down the right spines; `merge` empties the source heap.
- ‚úÖ 158B: `pradyos/web/leftist_heap_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_leftist_routes(app, leftist_heap=None)` mounts 6 routes: `POST /api/v1/leftist/insert` (body `{value}`), `GET /api/v1/leftist/find_min` (null when empty), `POST /api/v1/leftist/extract_min` (422 if empty), `POST /api/v1/leftist/merge` (body `{values: [...]}` ‚ÄĒ melds a heap of those values in), `GET /api/v1/leftist/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/leftist/reset`.
- ‚úÖ 158C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase158.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `leftist_heap` param, and a single `register_leftist_routes(app, leftist_heap)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 158D: `tests/test_leftist_heap.py` (31) + `tests/test_leftist_heap_web.py` (17) ‚ÄĒ full-drain == `sorted` (60 trials) + 5 000-drain, interleaved-vs-`heapq`, **merge two heaps == `sorted(both)`** (40 trials) with the leftist invariant re-checked each op, rank bound, order-independence, duplicates, floats/negatives, merge edge cases; validation (empty pop, non-num, bool, merge-non-heap, merge-self) + `LeftistHeapError.detail`; reset; determinism; 4-thread concurrent inserts; all 6 endpoints over HTTP incl. 422s + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `rangetree`).

**Phase 159 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 335 test modules green. Sovereign Scapegoat Tree (Galperin & Rivest, 1993) ‚ÄĒ a **self-balancing BST that uses no per-node balance field and no rotations**: it lets the tree drift on insertions and, when a freshly inserted node ends up deeper than `log_{1/őĪ}(n)`, walks up to the **scapegoat** (the highest ancestor that is not weight-`őĪ`-balanced ‚ÄĒ found by computing subtree sizes on the way up) and **rebuilds that entire subtree perfectly balanced** in linear time; deletions unlink the node and rebuild the *whole* tree once the live count falls below `őĪ ¬∑ (high-water size)`. This is a balancing *paradigm* the platform lacks ‚ÄĒ amortized rebuild, distinct from the rotation-balanced AVL/P155, the split/merge B-Tree/P156, the randomized Treap, and the move-to-root Splay Tree/P133 ‚ÄĒ yet still guarantees `O(log n)` amortized `insert` / `delete` and worst-case `O(log n)` `contains`. Supports `insert(key)`, `delete(key)`, `contains(key)`, `minimum()`, `maximum()`, `in_order()`, `height()`, `alpha`, `size`, and `reset`. **Verified** (honest): a **differential test against a sorted reference set matched `in_order == sorted` and `contains` across őĪ ‚ąą {0.55, ‚ÖĒ, 0.75, 0.9} (80 trials), with the height re-checked `‚Č§ log_{1/őĪ}(n) + 3` after *every* op**; 5 000 *sorted* insertions stay at the height bound (h = 21 = ‚Ćälog‚āĀ.‚āÖ(5000)‚Ćč, the naive-BST worst case kept balanced), reverse-insertion, sorted-delete-half, delete-all-to-empty, leaf/one-child/two-child deletes, and string/float keys all hold. Exposed at `/api/v1/scapegoat`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`; deterministic; rebuilds keep height `‚Č§ log_{1/őĪ}(n)` so descent recursion is bounded. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/scapegoat_tree_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 159A: `pradyos/core/scapegoat_tree.py` ‚ÄĒ `ScapegoatTreeError(detail)`; `ScapegoatTree(alpha=2/3)` with `insert(key)` ‚Üí bool, `delete(key)` ‚Üí bool, `contains(key)`, `minimum()`, `maximum()`, `in_order()`, `height()`, `reset()`, `is_empty()`, `size` / `len()` / `alpha` + `stats()`. `alpha ‚ąą (0.5, 1.0)`; keys `int`/`float`/`str` (no bool/None); mixed-type comparisons raise `ScapegoatTreeError`. No per-node augmentation ‚ÄĒ sizes computed on demand; scapegoat-find walks the insertion path; subtree rebuild via in-order flatten ‚Üí median build.
- ‚úÖ 159B: `pradyos/web/scapegoat_tree_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_scapegoat_routes(app, scapegoat_tree=None)` mounts 6 routes: `POST /api/v1/scapegoat/insert` (body `{key}`, type-preserving), `POST /api/v1/scapegoat/delete` (body `{key}`), `GET /api/v1/scapegoat/contains` (`?key=`), `GET /api/v1/scapegoat/keys` (in-order), `GET /api/v1/scapegoat/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/scapegoat/reset`. Non-orderable / mixed-type ‚Üí 422.
- ‚úÖ 159C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase159.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `scapegoat_tree` param, and a single `register_scapegoat_routes(app, scapegoat_tree)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 159D: `tests/test_scapegoat_tree.py` (34) + `tests/test_scapegoat_tree_web.py` (16) ‚ÄĒ **a differential test against a sorted reference set** across 4 őĪ's with the height-bound re-checked each op; sorted/reverse 5 000-insert balance, sorted-delete-half, delete-all, delete node types, string/float; validation (őĪ out of range, None, bool, unorderable, mixed-type) + `ScapegoatTreeError.detail`; reset; determinism; 4-thread concurrent inserts; all 6 endpoints over HTTP incl. 422s + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `leftist`).

**Phase 160 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 337 test modules green. Sovereign Binomial Heap (Vuillemin, 1978) ‚ÄĒ a **mergeable min-priority-queue** structured as a forest of **binomial trees** (a `B‚āĖ` tree has `2ŠĶŹ` nodes and is two `B‚āĖ‚āč‚āĀ` trees linked), with at most one tree of each order. Its hallmark is that `merge` works exactly like **binary addition**: equal-order trees are linked with a carry, giving `O(log n)` `merge` / `insert` / `extract_min` / `decrease_key`. This completes the platform's mergeable-heap family alongside the *amortized*-meld Skew Heap/P136 and the *worst-case*-meld Leftist Heap/P158 ‚ÄĒ binomial is the structure the Fibonacci Heap/P154 lazily improves upon. Stable integer handles drawn from a **process-wide counter** (so two heaps never collide) make `decrease_key` addressable and keep cross-instance `merge` valid; `decrease_key` bubbles the element up its tree by exchanging the `(key, handle)` payload with ancestors and keeping the handle map in sync. Supports `insert(value)` ‚Üí handle, `find_min`, `extract_min`, `decrease_key(handle, value)`, `merge(other)`, `size`, and `reset`. **Verified** (honest): a **full-drain == `sorted` check (50 trials) + a 5 000-element drain**, a **differential against a brute `{handle ‚Üí value}` dict matched `find_min` after every op over 10 000 random insert/extract_min/decrease_key operations**, and a **`merge` differential** ‚ÄĒ with the **binomial structural invariant (strictly-increasing root degrees, each `B‚āĖ` holding exactly `2ŠĶŹ` nodes, min-heap order, and handle-map consistency) re-checked after every op**, and a handle that originated in the *merged-away* heap remaining valid for `decrease_key` afterward. Exposed at `/api/v1/binomial`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock` (two-instance `merge` acquires both in `id()` order); deterministic; root list `O(log n)` trees, each tree depth `O(log n)` ‚ÄĒ no recursion. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/binomial_heap_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 160A: `pradyos/core/binomial_heap.py` ‚ÄĒ `BinomialHeapError(detail)`; `BinomialHeap()` with `insert(value)` ‚Üí handle, `find_min`, `find_min_handle`, `extract_min`, `decrease_key(handle, value)`, `merge(other)`, `reset`, `is_empty`, `size` / `len()` + `stats()`. `value` a number (bools rejected); empty pops raise; `decrease_key` must not increase; `merge` requires another `BinomialHeap` (not self). CLRS `_union` (merge root lists by degree, then link equal-degree with carry), child-reversal `extract_min`, payload-swap `decrease_key`; process-wide handle counter.
- ‚úÖ 160B: `pradyos/web/binomial_heap_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_binomial_routes(app, binomial_heap=None)` mounts 7 routes: `POST /api/v1/binomial/insert` (body `{value}`), `GET /api/v1/binomial/find_min` (null when empty), `POST /api/v1/binomial/extract_min` (422 if empty), `POST /api/v1/binomial/decrease_key` (body `{handle, value}`), `POST /api/v1/binomial/merge` (body `{values: [...]}`), `GET /api/v1/binomial/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/binomial/reset`.
- ‚úÖ 160C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase160.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `binomial_heap` param, and a single `register_binomial_routes(app, binomial_heap)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 160D: `tests/test_binomial_heap.py` (35) + `tests/test_binomial_heap_web.py` (20) ‚ÄĒ full-drain == `sorted` (50 trials) + 5 000-drain + a 10 000-op differential vs a brute dict, **binomial invariant re-checked each op**, merge (incl. merged-away handle still valid), decrease-to-new-min, order-independence, duplicates, floats/negatives; validation (empty pop, non-num, bool, bad/dead handle, key-increase, non-int handle, merge-non-heap, merge-self) + `BinomialHeapError.detail`; reset; determinism; 4-thread concurrent inserts; all 7 endpoints over HTTP incl. 422s + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `scapegoat`).

**Phase 161 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 339 test modules green. Sovereign Binary Lifting (LCA / k-th ancestor) ‚ÄĒ a **rooted-tree ancestor-query structure**: after `O(n log n)` preprocessing of a jump table `up[k][v]` (the `2ŠĶŹ`-th ancestor of `v`), it answers **lowest-common-ancestor** `lca(u, v)`, **`kth_ancestor(v, k)`**, `depth(v)`, and `is_ancestor(u, v)` each in `O(log n)`. This is the platform's first *tree-query-preprocessing* structure ‚ÄĒ it operates on a given rooted forest (a parent array) rather than maintaining an ordered set/heap, distinct from every search tree and priority queue shipped so far. Build is a BFS from the roots that detects cycles / invalid parents. Supports `build(parents)`, `lca(u, v)`, `kth_ancestor(v, k)`, `depth(v)`, `is_ancestor(u, v)`, and `reset`. **Verified** (honest): a **differential test against a naive ancestor-walk matched `lca`, `kth_ancestor`, `is_ancestor` and `depth` over 480 queries across 60 random forests** plus a 4 000-node balanced-binary-tree `lca` sweep; a 1 000-deep chain, a 500-leaf star, a two-tree forest (cross-tree `lca` ‚Üí `None`), self-LCA, reflexive `is_ancestor`, and single-node cases all hold. Exposed at `/api/v1/binarylifting`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`; deterministic; the jump table has `‚Ćąlog‚āā n‚ĆČ` levels so every query is iterative and structurally bounded. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/binary_lifting_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 161A: `pradyos/core/binary_lifting.py` ‚ÄĒ `BinaryLiftingError(detail)`; `BinaryLifting(parents=None)` with `build(parents)`, `lca(u, v)`, `kth_ancestor(v, k)`, `depth(v)`, `is_ancestor(u, v)`, `reset`, `is_empty`, `size` / `len()` / `levels` + `stats()`. `parents[v]` an int in `[-1, n)` (‚ąí1 = root) forming a forest (cycles / self-parents / out-of-range raise); nodes ints in `[0, n)`; `k ‚Č• 0`. `lca`/`kth_ancestor` return `None` when no such node.
- ‚úÖ 161B: `pradyos/web/binary_lifting_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_binarylifting_routes(app, binary_lifting=None)` mounts 7 routes: `POST /api/v1/binarylifting/build` (body `{parents}`), `GET /api/v1/binarylifting/lca` (`?u=&v=`, may be null), `GET /api/v1/binarylifting/kth_ancestor` (`?v=&k=`, may be null), `GET /api/v1/binarylifting/depth` (`?v=`), `GET /api/v1/binarylifting/is_ancestor` (`?u=&v=`), `GET /api/v1/binarylifting/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/binarylifting/reset`. Out-of-range / cycle / negative-k ‚Üí 422.

Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 161D: `tests/test_binary_lifting.py` (31) + `tests/test_binary_lifting_web.py` (19) ‚ÄĒ **a differential test against a naive ancestor-walk** for lca/kth/is_ancestor/depth (480 q / 60 forests) + a 4 000-node binary tree; chain, star, forest cross-tree `None`, self/reflexive cases, single node, `kth` exceeding depth; validation (self-parent, cycle, out-of-range, non-int, node-out-of-range, negative-k) + `BinaryLiftingError.detail`; build / reset; determinism; 10-thread concurrent queries; all 7 endpoints over HTTP incl. 422s + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `binomial`).

**Phase 162 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 341 test modules green. Sovereign Implicit Treap (rope / indexable sequence) ‚ÄĒ the platform's first **sequence** structure: a randomized balanced binary tree keyed *implicitly by position* (a node's index is the size of its left subtree), supporting `O(log n)` **insert-at-index**, **delete-at-index**, **get / set by index**, and **range-sum** (each node caches its subtree sum), all built on the treap `split`/`merge` primitives. Unlike every ordered set/heap shipped, it represents a *list* whose middle can be spliced in `O(log n)` (an array needs `O(n)`) ‚ÄĒ distinct from the key-ordered Treap, the AVL/P155, and array-backed structures. Random priorities (from a **seeded** RNG, so results are deterministic) keep the height `O(log n)` with high probability ‚ÄĒ and because priorities are internal, *no* operation sequence can force it deep. Supports `insert(index, value)`, `delete(index)`, `get(index)`, `set(index, value)`, `range_sum(lo, hi)`, `to_list()`, `size`, and `reset`. **Verified** (honest): a **differential test against a Python list matched `to_list`, `get`, `delete`'s returned value, and `range_sum` after every op across 40 random op-sequences** plus a 2 000-op run; a 1 000-element build, insert-in-the-middle, front/back/mid deletes, floats, and same-seed determinism all hold. Exposed at `/api/v1/implicittreap`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`; deterministic (seeded); `split`/`merge` recursion descends one `O(log n)`-height path. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/implicit_treap_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 162A: `pradyos/core/implicit_treap.py` ‚ÄĒ `ImplicitTreapError(detail)`; `ImplicitTreap(seed=0)` with `insert(index, value)`, `delete(index)` ‚Üí value, `get(index)`, `set(index, value)`, `range_sum(lo, hi)`, `to_list()`, `reset`, `is_empty`, `size` / `len()` + `stats()`. `index` int in `[0, size]` (insert) / `[0, size)` (others); `value` a number; `lo ‚Č§ hi` ‚ÄĒ violations raise `ImplicitTreapError`. Position-keyed `split`/`merge`; size + sum aggregates maintained per node.
- ‚úÖ 162B: `pradyos/web/implicit_treap_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_implicittreap_routes(app, implicit_treap=None)` mounts 8 routes: `POST /api/v1/implicittreap/insert` (body `{index, value}`), `POST /api/v1/implicittreap/delete` (body `{index}`), `GET /api/v1/implicittreap/get` (`?index=`), `POST /api/v1/implicittreap/set` (body `{index, value}`), `GET /api/v1/implicittreap/range_sum` (`?lo=&hi=`), `GET /api/v1/implicittreap/list`, `GET /api/v1/implicittreap/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/implicittreap/reset`. Out-of-range / non-num / inverted ‚Üí 422.

Existing routes untouched.

- ‚úÖ 162F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 163 planned.

**Phase 163 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 343 test modules green. Sovereign Lazy Segment Tree (range-update + range-query) ‚ÄĒ a segment tree with **lazy propagation** that supports `O(log n)` **range updates** ‚ÄĒ both range-add and range-assign ‚ÄĒ alongside `O(log n)` **range-sum / range-min / range-max** queries. Pending updates are buffered as a lazy tag at each node and pushed down only when a child is visited, so an update touching `O(n)` leaves still costs `O(log n)`. This is a new capability for the platform: the Segment Tree/P81 is *point-update* only and the Sqrt Decomposition/P147 does range-add/range-sum in `O(‚ąön)` ‚ÄĒ the lazy segment tree adds `O(log n)` range *assignment* and range *min/max*. The two lazy tags compose with **assign-dominates** semantics: a pending assign clears any pending add, then later adds accumulate on top (pushed down assign-then-add). Supports `build(values)`, `range_add(lo, hi, delta)`, `range_assign(lo, hi, value)`, `range_sum(lo, hi)`, `range_min(lo, hi)`, `range_max(lo, hi)`, `point_query(i)`, `size`, and `reset`. **Verified** (honest): a **differential test against a brute reference array over *interleaved* range_add + range_assign + range_sum/min/max/point_query across nine sizes** plus a 1 000-element / 500-update run; the assign-clears-pending-add-then-add-accumulates ordering, min/max shift under add, nested/overlapping ranges, full-range assign, single-element and float cases all hold. Exposed at `/api/v1/lazysegtree`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`; deterministic; `O(n)` nodes, recursion depth `O(log n)` (perfectly balanced). Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/lazy_segment_tree_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 163A: `pradyos/core/lazy_segment_tree.py` ‚ÄĒ `LazySegmentTreeError(detail)`; `LazySegmentTree(values=None)` with `build(values)`, `range_add(lo, hi, delta)`, `range_assign(lo, hi, value)`, `range_sum`/`range_min`/`range_max(lo, hi)`, `point_query(i)`, `reset`, `size` / `len()` + `stats()`. `values` numbers; indices ints with `0 ‚Č§ lo ‚Č§ hi < n`; delta/value numbers ‚ÄĒ violations raise `LazySegmentTreeError`. Per-node sum/min/max + `add` and `assign` lazy tags; `_apply_assign`/`_apply_add` with assign-dominates composition, push-down on descent, pull-up on return.
- ‚úÖ 163B: `pradyos/web/lazy_segment_tree_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_lazyseg_routes(app, lazy_segment_tree=None)` mounts 9 routes: `POST /api/v1/lazysegtree/build`, `POST /api/v1/lazysegtree/range_add` (body `{lo, hi, delta}`), `POST /api/v1/lazysegtree/range_assign` (body `{lo, hi, value}`), `GET /api/v1/lazysegtree/range_sum` / `range_min` / `range_max` (`?lo=&hi=`), `GET /api/v1/lazysegtree/point_query` (`?i=`), `GET /api/v1/lazysegtree/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/lazysegtree/reset` (body `{values?}`).
- ‚úÖ 163C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase163.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `lazy_segment_tree` param, and a single `register_lazyseg_routes(app, lazy_segment_tree)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 163D: `tests/test_lazy_segment_tree.py` (33) + `tests/test_lazy_segment_tree_web.py` (18) ‚ÄĒ **a differential test against a brute array** for interleaved add/assign + sum/min/max/point (9 sizes) + a 1 000/500-op run; assign-clears-add composition, min/max under add, nested overlapping, full assign, single-element, floats; validation (non-num, `lo>hi`, out-of-range, non-num delta/value, empty) + `LazySegmentTreeError.detail`; build / reset; determinism; 10-thread concurrent range_adds; all 9 endpoints over HTTP incl. 422s + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `implicittreap`).
- ‚úÖ 163E: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 343 test modules registered (Phase 163 appends `test_lazy_segment_tree.py` + `test_lazy_segment_tree_web.py`).
- ‚úÖ 163F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 164 planned.

**Phase 164 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 345 test modules green. Sovereign Ternary Search Tree (Bentley & Sedgewick, 1997) ‚ÄĒ a **string symbol table** that stores keys character-by-character in a *ternary* BST: each node holds one character and three children ‚ÄĒ `lo` / `eq` / `hi` ‚ÄĒ so a search compares the current character and branches left/right (different char) or down via `eq` (matched, advance to the next char). It combines a trie's prefix structure with a BST's space efficiency, supporting `O(|key| + tree-depth)` `insert` / `contains` / `delete`, plus **prefix enumeration** (`keys_with_prefix`) and **longest-prefix-of** queries ‚ÄĒ distinct from the Radix Tree/P140 (Patricia, edge-compressed) and the bit-tries already shipped. Deletion is lazy (the terminal node is unmarked), so re-insertion is `O(1)` extra. **Verified** (honest): a **differential test against a Python set of strings matched `insert`/`delete`/`contains` (40 trials), `keys()`, `keys_with_prefix`, and `longest_prefix_of` (40 trials each)**; a 2 000-key shared-prefix build proves the iterative descent survives a degenerate character-BST, plus Unicode keys, single-character keys, and delete-then-reinsert. Exposed at `/api/v1/tst`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`; deterministic; every descent and the prefix `collect` use explicit loops / a stack ‚ÄĒ no recursion. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/ternary_search_tree_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 164A: `pradyos/core/ternary_search_tree.py` ‚ÄĒ `TernarySearchTreeError(detail)`; `TernarySearchTree()` with `insert(key)` ‚Üí bool, `contains(key)`, `delete(key)` ‚Üí bool, `keys_with_prefix(prefix)`, `longest_prefix_of(query)`, `keys()`, `reset`, `is_empty`, `size` / `len()` + `stats()`. Keys are non-empty strings on `insert` (non-str / empty raise); `contains`/`prefix`/`longest` accept any string (empty ‚Üí no match). Iterative `lo`/`eq`/`hi` descent; lazy delete; stack-based prefix collect.
- ‚úÖ 164B: `pradyos/web/ternary_search_tree_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_tst_routes(app, ternary_search_tree=None)` mounts 8 routes: `POST /api/v1/tst/insert` (body `{key}`), `POST /api/v1/tst/delete` (body `{key}`), `GET /api/v1/tst/contains` (`?key=`), `GET /api/v1/tst/keys_with_prefix` (`?prefix=`), `GET /api/v1/tst/longest_prefix_of` (`?query=`, may be null), `GET /api/v1/tst/keys`, `GET /api/v1/tst/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/tst/reset`. Non-str / empty-key insert ‚Üí 422.
- ‚úÖ 164C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase164.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `ternary_search_tree` param, and a single `register_tst_routes(app, ternary_search_tree)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 164D: `tests/test_ternary_search_tree.py` (31) + `tests/test_ternary_search_tree_web.py` (18) ‚ÄĒ **a differential test against a Python set** for insert/delete/contains/keys/keys_with_prefix/longest_prefix_of; 2 000 shared-prefix keys (no recursion overflow), Unicode, single-char keys, delete-reinsert, empty-input handling; validation (non-str, empty-key insert) + `TernarySearchTreeError.detail`; reset; determinism; 4-thread concurrent inserts; all 8 endpoints over HTTP incl. 422s + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `lazysegtree`).
- ‚úÖ 164E: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 345 test modules registered (Phase 164 appends `test_ternary_search_tree.py` + `test_ternary_search_tree_web.py`).
- ‚úÖ 164F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 165 planned.

**Phase 165 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 347 test modules green. Sovereign Heavy-Light Decomposition (Sleator & Tarjan, 1983) ‚ÄĒ the platform's first **tree path-aggregate** structure: it decomposes a rooted tree into *heavy chains* (each node links to its largest-subtree child), assigns every node a contiguous position so each chain (and each subtree) is a contiguous range, and lays a point-update segment tree (carrying both sum and max) over those positions. A **path query** `path_sum(u, v)` / `path_max(u, v)` walks up `O(log n)` chains ‚ÄĒ at each step querying the segment for the head-to-node span and jumping to the head's parent ‚ÄĒ for `O(log¬≤n)` path aggregates, plus `O(log n)` `update(node, value)` and `O(log n)` `subtree_sum(v)`. This is distinct from Binary Lifting/P161 (ancestor queries only, no aggregates) and every array segment tree (no tree structure). **Verified** (honest): a **differential test against a naive path-walk matched `path_sum`, `path_max` and `subtree_sum` over 1 286 queries across 40 random trees** (with interleaved updates) plus a 2 000-node balanced-binary-tree sweep; a 1 000-node chain, a 500-leaf star, single-node, self/adjacent-path, and a 5 000-node chain (proving the iterative build doesn't overflow) all hold. Exposed at `/api/v1/hld`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`; deterministic; build uses iterative BFS/DFS (chain trees can be `O(n)` deep) and the segment tree is iterative. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/heavy_light_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- ‚úÖ 165A: `pradyos/core/heavy_light.py` ‚ÄĒ `HeavyLightError(detail)`; `HeavyLight(parents=None, values=None)` with `build(parents, values)`, `update(node, value)`, `path_sum(u, v)`, `path_max(u, v)`, `subtree_sum(v)`, `depth(v)`, `reset`, `is_empty`, `size` / `len()` + `stats()`. `parents` a *single*-rooted tree (multiple roots / cycle / out-of-range / self-parent raise); `values` length must match; nodes ints in `[0, n)`; value numeric. Iterative size/heavy via reverse-BFS, iterative stack decomposition (heavy child contiguous), embedded bottom-up sum+max segment tree.
- ‚úÖ 165B: `pradyos/web/heavy_light_web.py` ‚ÄĒ `register_hld_routes(app, heavy_light=None)` mounts 8 routes: `POST /api/v1/hld/build` (body `{parents, values?}`), `POST /api/v1/hld/update` (body `{node, value}`), `GET /api/v1/hld/path_sum` / `path_max` (`?u=&v=`), `GET /api/v1/hld/subtree_sum` / `depth` (`?v=`), `GET /api/v1/hld/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/hld/reset`. Malformed tree / out-of-range / non-num ‚Üí 422.
- ‚úÖ 165C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase165.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `heavy_light` param, and a single `register_hld_routes(app, heavy_light)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- ‚úÖ 165D: `tests/test_heavy_light.py` (33) + `tests/test_heavy_light_web.py` (17) ‚ÄĒ **a differential test against a naive path-walk** (1 286 q / 40 trees + a 2 000-node tree); chain / star / single / self / adjacent / through-root, 5 000-node-chain build, subtree-after-update; validation (self-parent, cycle, two roots, out-of-range, values mismatch, node-oob, non-num) + `HeavyLightError.detail`; build / reset; determinism; 10-thread concurrent path queries; all 8 endpoints over HTTP incl. 422s + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `tst`).
- ‚úÖ 165E: `scripts/prove.py` ‚ÄĒ 347 test modules registered (Phase 165 appends `test_heavy_light.py` + `test_heavy_light_web.py`).
- ‚úÖ 165F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 166 planned.

**Phase 166 ‚ÄĒ Planned.** Sovereign Sparse Segment Tree (dynamic segment tree) ‚ÄĒ a segment tree over a **huge coordinate space** `[0, U)` (e.g. `U = 10¬Ļ‚Āł`) whose nodes are **created lazily** on the path of each update, so `q` updates use only `O(q log U)` memory instead of `O(U)`. It supports `O(log U)` **point-add** and **range-sum** without any coordinate compression ‚ÄĒ the capability the dense Segment Tree/P81 and Lazy Segment Tree/P163 cannot offer (they need an `O(U)` array). Each update walks root‚Üíleaf allocating missing children; each query prunes whole missing subtrees (an absent node contributes 0). Supports `update(index, delta)`, `point_assign(index, value)`, `range_sum(lo, hi)`, `point_query(index)`, `num_nodes`, and `reset`. To be exposed at `/api/v1/sparseseg`; `sparse_segment_tree` / `SparseSegmentTree` / `SparseSegmentTreeError` / `register_sparseseg_routes` / `/api/v1/sparseseg` verified free on `origin/main` (all `[0]`). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via `threading.Lock`; deterministic; recursion depth structurally bounded at `O(log U) ‚Č§ ~60`. Differential-tested against a brute `dict` over the coordinate space.

> *Phase-map note:* the Phase 132 slot was pre-verified for **AnchorHash**, but its `K`/`W`/`L`/`R` removal bookkeeping could not be reproduced to the platform's zero-flaw bar with confidence, so it was **pivoted** to the Cuckoo Hash Table (a fully-verifiable exact structure, differential-tested against `dict`). AnchorHash remains available for a future phase.

---

## PradyOS v0.41.0 ‚ÄĒ Self-Driving

**99 test modules. 41 phases. Stdlib + asyncio only.**

A fully autonomous, self-driving OS kernel built in Python, with observe ‚Üí alert ‚Üí plan ‚Üí react ‚Üí heal ‚Üí schedule ‚Üí persist ‚Üí remember ‚Üí control-plane ‚Üí heartbeat capabilities. The OS now drives itself ‚ÄĒ `HeartbeatLoop` ticks `ControlPlane` on a fixed cadence, which in turn ticks the scheduler, healer, and reactor in sequence. No external orchestrator needed.

The OS observes its own metrics (`SignalAggregator`), detects thresholds (`WatchpointSystem`), correlates signals (`CorrelationEngine`), records every decision into a cryptographically chained ledger (`DecisionJournal`), reacts to alerts via rules (`ReactorEngine`), self-heals degraded components (`HealingMonitor`), schedules its own work (`TaskScheduler`), persists state across restarts (`SnapshotStore` + `StateManager`), remembers context with TTLs (`MemoryStore`), wires it all together (`SovereignBus`), exposes a unified introspection layer (`ControlPlane`), and drives itself forward through an async loop (`HeartbeatLoop`).

**Phase 15 ‚ÄĒ Complete.** All 47 test modules green. Sovereign Scheduler ‚ÄĒ cron-style recurring campaigns with priority queues and SLA-aware routing:
- ‚úÖ 15A: `pradyos/sovereign/scheduler.py` ‚ÄĒ `SovereignScheduler` class with
  injectable `clock` for deterministic testing. Pure-stdlib 5-field cron parser
  supporting `*`, `*/N`, and single-integer fields for minute/hour/dom/month/dow.
  `next_run_after(cron_expr, after_ts)` scans minute-by-minute in UTC.
  `add_job()` stores job dicts with `job_id`, `cron_expr`, `campaign_spec`,
  `priority`, `sla_seconds`, `next_run`, `enabled`. `remove_job()` / `enable_job()`
  / `disable_job()` return bool. `tick()` fires all enabled jobs whose
  `next_run <= clock()`, publishes `"scheduler.job.fired"` bus events, advances
  `next_run`, and returns the list of fired job_ids. `start()` / `stop()` manage a
  daemon background thread; both are idempotent. Thread-safe via `threading.Lock`.
- ‚úÖ 15B: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` ‚ÄĒ five new endpoints wired via optional
  `scheduler` param in `create_app()`: `GET /api/v1/scheduler/jobs`,
  `POST /api/v1/scheduler/jobs`, `DELETE /api/v1/scheduler/jobs/{job_id}`,
  `POST /api/v1/scheduler/jobs/{job_id}/enable`,
  `POST /api/v1/scheduler/jobs/{job_id}/disable`. All return HTTP 200; safe
  empty responses when scheduler not injected.
- ‚úÖ 15C: `tests/test_sovereign_scheduler.py` ‚ÄĒ 20 unit tests covering all
  scheduler methods, cron parsing, clock injection, bus event payload,
